Nguva dzakanga dzasvika pakati pahwo usiku apo pakanga pasisina vanhu vanofamba mumigwagwa. Ndipo pavaingonzwa kuchema kwezvikara bedzi zvinenge zviri mumasango.
Kana vari vaya weusiku ndipo pavainyatsoita basa nesimba ravo rese. Mabasa erima ndidzo zvekare nguva dzaaitoitwa. Vaingonzwa imbwa kuhukura wotoziva kuti ndiwo vaye wemabasa erima. Ndipo pavaiona vamwe votsumwaira kwaedza voshaya kuti chii izvo wanga vari pabasa usiku.
Panguva dzimwechetedzo pane rimwe boka rakanga rine musangano pasi pemvura pakadzika dzika mugungwa. Vanhu awa vaisangana nguva nenguva apo vaikurukura zvakasiyana siyana maererano nezvavaizoita kana wava panyika. Vaiswera vari munzvimbo dzavanorarama vari apo vaizosangana nguva idzi.
Vaiti kana vasangana pasi apa vaitaura mutauro mumwe chete kunyangwe zvazvo vaibva kunyika dzakasiyana.
Vicky uyo aiva mambokadzi ndiye akabva apinda mudariro nenyaya dzake dzaaida kuti dzizokurukurwa.
 

Akanga akagara pachigaro chegoridhe chakanga chakakura uye chakanaka kudarika zvevamwe wese. Akanga ari mukadzi mukobvu ari mutsvuku akareba zviripakati nepakati. Bvudzi rake rakanga rakarukwa zvekareba zvekuda kunobata muchiuno chake. Aiti kana otaura vaimedza mate wanzwa inzwi rake.
"Ndinokutendai mese nekuda kwekuuya kwamaita kumusangano uno. Ndine nyaya dzandinadzo dzandinoda kuti timbokurukura tichionesana kuti todzifambisa sei." Panguva iyi mambokadzi vakambonyarara vachidzvuta komichi yavo yaiva newaini yakasangana neropa.
"Ndanga ndichida zvizhinji kuti tigovawo nemukurumbira panyika izvo zvinoda kuti tiise pfungwa dzedu pamwechete. Dai zvaibvira ndaida kuti tizotonga kuhofisi huru dzevakuru wenyika. Zvese izvi zvinoda pfungwa dzedu tese." Vicky akambodzvuta komichi yake achibva aenderera mberi.
"Ndine imwe nyaya zvekare yandinoda kupinza mudariro, munongoviziva kuti tinoshanda neropa revanhu uye ndiko kudya kunosimbisa basa redu. Nyaya iripo ndeyekuti toitasei kuti tirambe tichiwana ropa sezvo pamwe pacho tichimborishaya." Akambonyarara Vicky achibva azoenderera mberi.
 

"Imwe nyaya zvekare ndeyekuti chikwata chedu hachifanirwi kuramba chine vanhu vashoma sezvatakaita izvi. Tinofanirwa kuonesana kuti toitasei patinofamba kunze uko tigowandawo. Kana tawanda zvirinyore kuva nemasimba panyika nekuti ndisu tinenge tava nemukurumbira. Ndidzo dziri mudariro madeko ano. Mumwe nemumwe tichateerera zvaachataura kuti zvitibatsire panyaya idzi." Vicky achipedza kutaura mashoko aya akabva anyarara zvake achimirira vamwe kuti vataure.
Steve uyo aivawo muchikwata umu ndiye akabva apinda mudariro. Vamwe wese vakabva vateya nzeve vachimirira kunzwa mashoko aizotaurwa nechikomana icho.
"Pamusoroi mambokadzi, pamusoroi dare rose raungana pasi pano. Ini ndinoda kutaurawo zvandinokwanisa kuzoita ndichinge ndava panyika. Ndinokwanisa kungoshandisa masimba angu kuti pasi rose kuite nzara, vatungamiri wenyika dzepasi rose pavanoungana vachironga kuti vodii ndipo pandinoita sendinovabatsira kuburikidza nemari izvo zvinobva zvaita kuti tipinzwe muhutungamiri. Zvinhu zvatinoziva tese kuti mari nechikafu zvinotonga." Steve anombonyarara apo vanhu wese waiva pasi pemvura apa vakabva vaombera maoko.
 

"Asi basa iri kuti ribudirire handizokwanisa kuriita ndega, ndinodawo vamwe vandinofamba navo kuti zviite chiremera. Kana hutongi huchinge hwabudirira kupinda mumaoko edu ndipo patinenge toisa mitemo yatinoda isusu nekuti hapana anenge achatidzivisa." Steve achipedza kutaura vanhu vakabva vaombera zvekare.
Akabva avimbisa vanhu kuti zano iri rinobudirira asi raizotora nguva.
Mudariro makabva mapinda Johnson uyo aiva murefu ari mutsvuku. Akanga akasimba zviripakati nepakati.
"Ini hangu ndichange ndichitambira kune vezvitendero. Ndinongoputsa zvitendero apo ndinotanga kupfeka vakuru wavo kuti vashaiwe simba. Kana tichinge takunda kuisa hutongi hwepasi rino mumaoko edu tinenge tavakutonga muzvitendero tichiisa mitemo yedu. Anenge achizopokana nesu anouraiwa." Jonhson achipedza kutaura vanhu vakabva vaombera zvekare.
Pakamboita runyararo apo Hazel akazopindawo mudariro. Mwanasikana uyu akanga akaumbwa pachiso zvekuti runako rwese rwakanga rwakaperera paari.
Vaigona kutsikwa nemota vakamutarisa vakayeva runako rwake.
"Pamusoroi dare rose raungana pano. Kana iri nyaya yeropa idiki kwandiri." Akambonyarara zvishoma.
 

"Runako rwangu urwu ndinokwanisa kurwushandisa kuuraya varume vane ruchiva mumabhawa umu.
Nesimba randinaro zvekare ndinokwanisa kuzvishandura kuita chose chandada pazvinhu zvose zviripasi pano." Chisikana Hazy chakambonyarara pachibva pamboita maungira nemiridzo nekuombera.
"Zvichakadaro ndinoona ndichizokwanisa kupinda pose pandinoda ndichideura ropa. Ndinokwanisa kana kuzvishandura kuita mukoti ndotora ropa revarwere.
Zvisinei basa iri handigoni kuriita ndega asi tichasimudzira vamwe muchikwata chedu sezvo varipowo vandinokwanisa kuita navo basa iri." Hazel akambonyarara achibva azoenderera mberi.
"Kana iri nyaya yekuti chikwata chikure hainetsi ndinokwanisa kungoshandisa mari kana chikafu chaicho nyangwe nehembe dzatinopfeka. Ndinokwanisa kungopinda kana muzvikoro ndozvishandura kuita mwana wechikoro saka hazvinetsi." Vanhu vakazoombera maoko zvekare Hazel apedza kutaura.
Brighton ndiye akazopinda mudariro.
"Ini hangu ndichange ndichizoongorora midziyo inenge ichigadzirwa panyika kunyanya kudzimotokari. Ndinenge ndichizogadzirawo dzangu mota dzakadaro wese anenge atenga anoita tsaona nayo. Kuzvigadzirwa zvese kana michina ndizvo zvandichaita. Chose chandinenge
 

ndagadzira chinenge chichizofanirwa kudeura ropa." Brighton akazopedza kutaura vanhu votoombera kare.
Vamwe vakazopawo pfungwa dzavo maererano nenyaya dzaiva mudariro musi uyu. Vicky ndiye akazovhara musangano uyu nemashoko ekusimbisa.
"Ndinotenda nepfungwa dzose dzashanda muzuva ranhasi uye ndaona tichizosvika kure nebasa redu. Masimba ngaashande haasi ekushandisira mumvura muno asi panyika pamawa kuenda. Mashoko angu ekupedzisira ndeekuti ngatishande nesimba tigowana zvatirikuda." Mambokadzi achipedza kutaura akabva anyangarika. Vamwe vakazoita zvimwechetezvo vachienda kunzvimbo dzavairaramira.



CHAPTER 2
PABLOZ NIGHT CLUB
Wakanga uri musi wechishanu apo mwedzi vakanga vapera. Vanhu vakanga vachifara zvavo vachinwa doro rinodhura sezvo homwe dzakanga dzakasimba.
Kamhanzi kairirira pasi pasi kari kemusambo wehouse.
 

Nechekunerimwe divi kune vasikana vakanga vachitamba zvekuti kana moyo yevarume vakanga vari mubhawa umu yakatomboenda kure. Vamwe vakanga votodemba kuti dai tisina madzimai taitora hedu awa.
Pavasikana vaitamba awa paiva nemumwe musikana mutsvuku mutete ari mupfupi zvishoma. Runako rwake dai rwaizoerwa nemagetsi rwaigona kutodhingura Kariba yese ikasara isina chinhu. Pamwanasikana uyu ndipo paiva nemaziso evarume vazhinji vakanga vari mubhawa umu.
Nechekudivi raiva nevanhu vaitamba awa kwaiva neimwe tafura hombe yaivako. Pane machinda maviri akanga akagara patafura iyoyo achiyeverwa nemwanasikana aitamba. Pavakomana awa paiva naTichaona uyo aiva maneja kuNaughtford investments pamwe naSmart vaaishanda naye ari mutevedzeri vake pakambani imwecheteyo.
"Ko vamboona here kamusikana kari pakati pavanhu varikutamba avo." Apa Tichaona akanga achibvunza mumwe vake atorwa moyo kare nemwanasikana uyu.
"Vatotangaka nyaya dzako dzekuda vakadzi, unombozviziva here kuti zvine makuva izvi. Chimbosiyana nazvo umbodzikama." Apa ndiSmart akanga oyambira mumwe vake asi aitotaura namatsi.
 

"Shamwari mukombe uyu haungambopfuura ndisina kuunwa, ndinofanirwa kuona zvekuita manheru ano chaiwo." Tichaona akanga atoita chandagwinyira panyaya iyi.
Vaviri awa vakaramba vachiitisana nharo dzamara nyaya yacho vazongoisiya yakadaro. Musikana uya akanga atora Tichaona moyo akazobva kunevanhu vaitamba achibva anogara patafura yake ega. Izvi zvose zvakanga zvirimumaziso aTichaona.
Tichaona akazosimuka achienda kwakanga kuine musikana uya vachibva vatanga kutokurukura zvavo. Musikana uya akabva azvizivisa saHazel kuna Tichaona uyo akanga atononokerwa nekupiwa rudo.
Shoko rerudo harina kunonoka kusvika kunaHazel uyo akabva angoridavira ipapo. Tichaona akabva atanga kunyemwerera zvekuti vaiti chana chidiki chatengerwa zviwitsi. Vari pakukurukura Hazel akabva atanga kunzwa kutaura munzeve dzake.
"Murume iyeye tinomuda kuno kuchingoedza. Ropa rake rinofanirwa kuita chibairo kune mukuru wedu." Inzwi iri richipedza kutaura rakabva raenda.
Hazel akabva abata Tichaona vake achimupuruzira ruoko. Panguva iyoyo Tichaona akabva anzwa kuda Hazel zvakapfurikidza.
 

"Shamwari ini ndatofunga hangu kugara newe, dai ndakaziva kuti ndaizosangana newe ndaisambotora mukadzi vandinaye uyu. Runako rwako rwanditenderedza pfungwa zvekuti mangwana chaiye ndinonomudzinga kumba." Tichaona achipedza kutaura Hazel akangosekerera hake. Nechemumoyo aingoti nhasi uchafara kekupedzisira hauzomaona mafaro enyika aya.
"Runako rwako Hazel rwunoita kuti ndikutengere ndege, kana vazowana kwadzinotengeswa unozondiudza ndonokutengera." Tichaona akataura apo Hazel aingonyemwerera.
Zvisinei vaviri awa vakazobuda apo Tichaona akabva atooneka shamwari yake Smart. Akabuda naHazel mubhawa muya apo vakabva vananga kumota yake yaiva yerudzi rweBenz S500.
Mota yakasimudzwa vachibva vaenda apo vakazonopinda mumugwagwa weArmadale takananga kuBorrowdale. Vasati vaenda kure vakabva vasvika paArmadale lodge.
ARMADALE LODGE(BORROWDALE)
 

Tichaona akatyaira mota yake achipinda pahotera apa. Ndiyo nzvimbo yaaizoda kufarira aine mumwe vake Hazel. Vachisvika pareception vakabva vasarudza imba yepamusoro yaidarika dzimwe dzese. Vakabva vapiwa room number apo vakabva vananga ikoko.
Nenguva isipi vakanga vatova mudziva rerudo. Tichaona aiva nemufaro sezvo nguva yaakanga akamirira yakanga yazosvika. Akanga avakudya namambo. Nechemumoyo Hazel akanga achifarira kuti basa rake raakanga avinga panyika rakanga ratotanga.
Mushure mekupedza mutambo wavo werudo vakabva varara zvavo. Hazel ndipo paaivimbiswa kunzi ndichakutora uwe vangu zvachose. Aivimbiswa kuzotengerwa denga zvese nevatumwa vacho.
Tichaona akazomuka zvekare kwoedza achiti vaenderere mberi nemudiwa vake Hazel. Ndipo paakaedza kutsvaga Hazel padivi pake apo akaona iri nzvimbo. Akamuka achida kunyatsoona apo akabva atoona panzvimbo yaHazel paine zinyoka zihombe.
Akashaya kuti chii chainyatsoitika.
Muchinda akasvetuka achibva paaiva apo akambomira nechekure mbijana. Zinyoka riya rakabva ratanga kutofamba richiuya kwaakanga ari.
 

Kuti titi ishato zvairamba nekuti yakanga yakadarika shato kukura uye iri tsvuku.
Izvi zvakabva zvashaisa Tichaona simba rekutiza achibva angoyeva nyoka iya ichiuya. Paaiongorora kudaro akabva awona nyoka iyi ine musoro wemunhu uyo vaakabva aziva. Akatozozviitira weti achinzwa nyoka iya ichitaura.
"Vakaura murume, ruchiva rwako rwazokupinza panguva yakaoma. Nguva yakwana yekuti uchionekana nenyika ino, kana vaenda kumarinda uvaudze variko kuti ruchiva rwakandiparira. Ufambe zvakanaka tozosangana zvekare kana ishe vatendera. Kana uine chekutaura gara vataura." Panguva iyi Tichaona haana chaakakwanisa kutaura asi akangoridza mhere yakavharidzira kunosvika kureception.
Zinyoka riya rakabva ratanga kumumonera monera apo raimutyora tyora. Richipedza kumumonera rakabva rabairira muswe waro nechepamoyo waTichaona.
Muswe wacho vaitoita kunge tsono zvekuti vakabva vapinda mukati chaimo. Ropa rese rakadhonzwa zvekuti Tichaona akasara ari kagwati chaiko kekuti vaitombotanga vafungidzira kuti munhu here kana kuti haasi. Ndipo paakabva angoonekana nenyika asina kumbozvitarisira.
 

Panguva iyi nyoka yakabva yashanduka kuita Hazel. Akabva atobuda muimba iya achiridza mhere akananga kureception. Ndipo paakasangana nevashandi wepahotera apa vachitouyawo vachitsvaga kwaibva ruzha.
Vashandi vakashaya kana remuromo vachiona chimiro chaiva naTichaona. Muviri vake wese panguva iyi vakanga vazara ropa.
Sevanhu vakanga vasina zvavaikwanisa kuita vakabva vangofonera mapurisa ayo asina kutora nguva kusvika. Chakatomboita chishamiso mapurisa achishayawo pekutangira. Hazel ndiye akabva atanga kupiwa mhosva achinzi aiziva zvakanga zvaitika. Akamboedza kuramba asi hapana akambozviteerera. Mutumbi waTichaona vakazotakurwa apo Hazel akabva aendwa naye kukamba yemapurisa.



CHAPTER 3
HARARE POLICE STATION
 

Mapurisa vachisvika kukamba vakabva vavharira Hazel muchizarira. Maiva nerima muchitonhora apo vakasiya vamuudza kuti vaizodzoka vachida mhinduro inogutsa kubva kwaari. Hazel akasara akavharirwa apo akanga avakufunga zvaaizoita nemapurisa aya.
Akabva ambokotsira hake arimo apo akazoona atosvika kunyika yezviroto. Ndipo paakaona achisangana naVicky uyo aiva mambokadzi wechikwata. Vakakwazisana apo Vicky akabva ataura nyaya yake yaakanga anayo.
"Toda ropa remapurisa shamwari, kana vagona uraya vatatu zvichikwira." Vicky akataura achiudza Hazel uyo akambosekerera achifunga tsoro yaaizotamba. Hazel akatozomutswa nekuvhurwa kwaiitwa musuwo nemapurisa.
"Huya kuno tione mwana wembwa utaure nyaya yako, munhu haangangofa zvausingazive iwe wanga unaye tirikuda chokwadi chako izvozvi." Mumwe wemapurisa aya akataura achiita zvekuzvuva Hazel kubva muchizarira.
Vakamufudza vachienda naye kwaaizonobvunzwa nyaya yake. Vakanga vachimutukirira akanyarara haana kana kumbotaura chinhu. Mumwe wacho ndiye akazoita manyemwe achibva arova Hazel nemboma kumusana.
 

Uyu ndiye akabva apisira manje apo Hazel akanga agumbuka. Akangocheuka achitarisa kune mupurisa akanga amurova. Moto vakangotanga kubuda mumaziso aHazel uchipisa mupurisa uya. Akapiswa akasvika pakuoma vamwe vake vakatarisa. Hupenyu hwakabva hwatooneka apo akazoonekwa ava neropa muviri wese zvakanga zvakaita muchinda uya kuhotera.
Hazel akanga asina kuperera ipapo apo akarangarira kuti pane mumwe wacho aimutukirira anova ndiye akaita zvekumuzvuva kubva muchizarira. Iyeye akaita zvekumusimudza nemaziso. Aiti akafambisa maziso ake achienda kumusoro mupurisa uya aibva asimuka mudenga paanomafambisa achimadzikisa kuzasi mupurisa uya aibva arovera pasi.
Aiti akatenderedza maziso ake achimaendesa nemumativi mupurisa uya aibva atanga kutenderera ari mumhepo. Akazongosvipa moto uyo vakabva vanopisa mupurisa uya achibva asara ari chimukuyu. Hapenyu hwakabva hwatama zvekare.
Apa akanga asarirwa nemupurisa mumwechete uyo akanga otya kuti oramba achienda naye here. Akanga aona vamwe vake vachiomeswa saka zvakanga zvavakurema kuti oitasei. Akazongopfugama achikumbira kuti Hazel amuraramisewo.
 

Hazel haana kuda kumuitira hutsinye akangomuti hande kwaurikuda kuenda neni. Vakafamba kwekanguva apo vakasvika muhofisi yaaida kuzobvunzwa nyaya yake pamusoro pezvakanga zvaitika kuhotera. Mupurisa uya achingomusiya muhofisi umu akabva abuda ari shamwari yemhepo achitya kuti angangobatanidzwa.
Hazel akazotanga kubvunzwa nyaya yake apo akaramba kuti akanga asingazvizive. Mupurisa aimubvunza pamusoro penyaya yake akaona kuti zvekubvunza zvirikunetsa achibva afunga kuedza zvimwe.
Akashevedza Hazel apo vakaenda kunechimwe chimba chaiva nerima. Akabva agariswa pachigaro chaivamo apo mupurisa uya akazouya akabata tambo dzemagetsi.
"Nhasi unotaura chete zvavaita kwete zvaurikuda kuita izvi zvekundiita mwana mudiki." Mupurisa uya akataura achouya pedyo naHazel. Avakuda kusvika maoko akanga akabata tambo akabva awoma akadaro.
Hupenyu hwakabva hwatama apo akabva adonha pasi.
Hazel akabva atosimuka pachigaro chiya apo akanga apedza basa. Apa yakanga yava nguva yekudzokera munyika ozoenda kwavanosangana kana nguva yacho yakwana. Akafamba akananga kugedhe apo akaona pane mumwe mupurisa akanga akarinda pagedhe. Basa rake raiva rekuona vanenge vachipinda nekubuda.
 

Paakaona Hazel avakubuda akabva amushevedza kuti adzoke. Hazel haana kuita nharo akangoita zvaakanga achitaurirwa. Akasvika achibvunzwa zita rake apo rakabva rashaikwa pabhuku repagedhe apa kuratidza kuti akanga asina kumbopinda nepo. Akabva avabudira pachena kuti akanga apinda ari musungwa.
Mupurisa uya paakada kushungurudza Hazel akabva audzwa kuti kana achida hupenyu hwake anyarare.
Hazel achipedza kutaura mashoko iwayo akabva atanga kufamba achienda. Mupurisa uya akaita hasha idzo dzakabva dzaita kuti abate pfuti achida kuridzira tsvarakadenga iyi. Hazel akangocheuka achibva asimudza ruoko apo mupurisa uya akasimukawo achibva arembera mumhepo.
Akabva avhara ruoko rwuya achibva arovera chibhakera muvhu. Mupurisa uya akabva aita zvekunorovera pasi nemuromo apo akazosara ava nhoroondo. Chakava chishamiso pakamba yese kurasikirwa nemapurisa mana pazuva rimwechete.
Zvakazowedzera kutyisa pavakaziva kuti musungwa wavo akanga angoenda zvisina akanzwisisa uye ndiye akanga akonzeresa rufu. Zvakazotaurwawo panhau manheru chikava chishamiso. Manheru iwayo Hazel akazodzokera kwavaisangana pasi pemvura.
 

CHAPTER 4 UNDER THE SEA
Vakanga vakaungana zvekare sezvavakanga vakaita pazuva rekutanga. Hazel akasvika vatoungana kare semunhu aibva kumarimuka. Vicky akanga akagara pachigaro chake chemazuva ese akakomberedzwa nezvigaro zvevakanga vari pasi pake. Anozoshamisa muromo vake kuti ataure.
"Ndinoda kutenda nebasa rose ramurikubata kana muripanyika. Ndichidaro ndinoti murambe muchishanda nesimba tinosvika kure chete. Zvikurusa ndoda kutenda mwanasikana wangu Hazel nebasa guru raabata.
Nezuro takanga tisinaye pamusangano wedu akanga aripabasa. Nhasi uno ndinofara nekuti basa redu ravakufamba zvakanaka nekuda kwehuwandu hweropa." Akataura Vicky apo vanhu vakatanga kuombera maoko vamwe vachisimudza Hazel vachimukanda mudenga.
Hazel akanga abata basa guru raidadisa. Akabva atogadzwa musi iwoyo kuva mutevedzeri vaVicky masimba achibva awandudzwa. Akabva apihwa vasikana vaviri vaaizofamba navo kwese kwaaienda. Vicky akazoenderera mberi nekusimbisa vamwe vake.
 

"Zvaitwa apa zvinofadza uye zvinovengwa nemhandu chete. Ngatirambei tichishanda nesimba kusvika humambo hwepasi rose hwava mumaoko edu." Vicky akazopedzisira nemashoko iwayo.
Pakazoitwa mabiko apo vakanga vachipemberera chigaro chakanga chapihwa Hazel. Mabiko akazopera kunze kwavakuda kuedza apo dzakanga dzava nguva dzekubuda kudzokera munyika. Mumwe nemumwe akazonyangarika apo vakanga wavakudzokera kwavanoraramira.
WESTVIEW CLINIC
PaWestview Clinic paibatwa basa rinodadisa zvekuti pakauya murwere airapwa zvine unyanzvi. Chiremba wacho aishevedzwa nezita rekuti Manhiyo aishanda nevakoti vaviri vaiti sister Lindi nasister Nyari. Ndiwo vanhu wavakanga vachibatsirana navo.
Pane murwere akanga achirapwa uyo akanga aita tsaona. Akanga ava nenguva arimo apo Manhiyo nevakoti vake vakanga vachishanda nesimba. Mazuva aifamba apo murwere akanga avapedyo nekupora.
Hama dzemurwere dzakanga dzavakutarisira kuti mazuva mashoma aizotevera aizobuda muchipatara.
 

Mumwe musi Lindi naNyari vakanga vachibatsirana kurapa muchinda uya apo vaimusimbisa kuti aizobuda zuva remangwana. Hazel akanga achifambawo munyika nevasikana vaviri vaakanga anzi anozofamba nawo.
Ndiyo nguva yavakanga wawana yekuvhima ropa munzvimbo dzakasiyana siyana. Pavasikana awa pakanga pana Lisa uyo aiva murefu akasimbawo mbijana. Mumwe vacho ainzi Millicent uyo aiva mutema ari mukobvu. Ndipo pavakabva vatanga kukurukura.
"Saka nhasi tofambirepi vasikana sevanhu vari pakuvhima kudai. Rangarirai kuti tinokwanisa kuenda pese patinenge tada toita basa redu ratakatumwa." Hazel akabvunza mumwe vamwe vake achida kunzwa pfungwa dzavo. Lisa ndiye akabva atanga kupindura apo akanga ava nekwekunanga kare.
"Ini ndinoona sekuti muKuwadzana munoita, pane kachipatara kanonzi Westview kanouya varwere vakawanda vachipona. Tinongosvika ipapo tobata basa iwe ndiwe unenge wavakutitungamira sezvo uri iwe mukuru kwatiri." Lisa akataura apo Millicent akabva aigamha.
"KuWestview kunoita manje nezuro ndakatombopfuura neikoko ndikaona munhu aitoraowa ainzi akaita tsaona. Tinofanirwa kutogumisa hupenyu hwake nhasi." Vakabva vatowirirana wese kunanga ikoko.
 

Vakabva wawirirana kuti sezvo paishanda vanhu vatatu vaizongozvishangura kunge ndiwo vashandi wepo.
Vaikotsirisa Chiremba nevakoti vake apo vaibva vatanga basa iwo. Vaizoshandisa majekiseni avakanga vakatakura mumabhegi pamwe nemushonga wacho vaizoita kuti munhu afe.
Sevanhu vakanga vari mudhorobha vakabva vaenda paimira mabhazi anoenda Kuwadzana. Mabhazi akanga asiri enhamo apo vasikana vakazoona vapinda mubhazi. Rwendo rwakabva rwatotanga apo vaizoburukira pachiteshi cheKuwadzana 2. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatosvika.
Ndipo pavakabva vatanga kufamba vachienda kudivi raiva nezvitoro kunova ndiko kwaiva nechipatara ichi. Ndicho chipatara chavaizotanga kusvika pachiri vasati vasvika pazvitoro. Pakanga pasina mufambo vakakura saka hazvina kuvatorera nguva refu kusvikapo.
Gedhe rakanga rakavhurwa sezvo yaiva nzvimbo inosvika vanhu vakawanda. Vachingopinda pamusuwo Hazel akabva asimudza ruoko rwake rweruboshwe achitaura chirudzi chaisanzwika. Akaramba achitaura kudaro kwekanguva zvakaita kuti vashandi wepachipatara vakotsire. Akabva atanga kufamba nevamwe vake vachienda kumusuwo wechipatara.
Akabva asimudza ruoko zvekare.
 

CHAPTER 5 WESTVIEW CLINIC
Paakasimudza ruoko zvekare akabva atanga kutaura chirudzi chiya chaakanga ambotaura pakutanga.
Akaramba achitaura apo Lisa akabva achinja kuita Sister Lindi. Akaramba achitaura zvekare apo Millicent akabva ashanduka kuita Sister Nyari. Vakabva vatofamba vachipinda muchipatara muya.
Hazel akaita zvekupfugama achibva anotunga pasi kaviri. Akazoona achinja kuita doctor Manhiyo. Basa rake rakanga ratotanga apo akabva atanga kutofamba achipinda mukati. Vakabatana vachibva vapinda mairapirwa muchinda uya.
Muchinda uya akasimudza musoro paakanzwa musuwo uchivhurwa. Paakaona kuti ndivanachiremba akabva adzikama zvake akarara.
"Saka wavakunzwa sei muchinda, pane zvirikuchinja here." NdiHazel aibvunza uyo akanga ari mumutumbi wadoctor Manhiyo. Muchinda uya akabva atopindurawo kuti akanga avakunzwa zvirinani. Akanga avakutoda zvekubuda muchipatara macho sezvo akanga asuwa mhuri yake.
 

"Usatye hako muchinda, mangwana chaiye unenge usisipo pavakarara apa. Rega tibate basa ko ndiko kwatinodanwa tikadairaka. Sister Lindi nditambidzeiwo jekiseni riya repottasium chloride ndimubaye. Ndoda kuti ropa rake rinyatsofamba zvakanaka iwe Nyari tora mapiritsi aya umupe anwe. Murwere kauyu anogona kukanganwa kunwa ngaanwe tichiona." Akataura Hazel achitotambidzwa jekiseni riya.
Akabaya muchinda uya uyo aingoterera nyama semunhu aiona vanachiremba. Millicent uyo akanga ari mumutumbi waNyari akatora mapiritsi achibva apa murwere uya kuti anwe. Akamboda kubvunza kuti aya ndeapi vachibva vamuudza kuti anofambirana nejekiseni raakanga abaiwa.
Vachipedza basa ravo vanobva vasiya vaudza murwere wavo kuti azorore apo vanobva vabuda. Vachisvika panze Hazel anobva asimudza ruoko zvekare. Pakarepo vanobva vadzoka mumitumbi yavo. Vanobva vatanga kufamba vachibva ipapo vachienda sevanhu vakanga vapedza basa.
Ndipo pakapepuka doctor Manhiyo vachitoshama kuti vakanga varara nguvai. Vanotarira Lindi naNyari votoona vakafa nehope. Vanovamutsa nekukasika vachishaya kuti chii chakanga chatora nzvimbo kuti vakotsire zvakadaro.
 

"Ko mukagokotsira kudaro kwakanaka here? Murwere pane ambomuona here?" Lindi naNyari vakavhunduka apo vakanga vatokanganwa zvekuti kune murwere.
Vanobva paya vachitungamidzana apo doctor Manhiyo vakabva vateverawo kumashure.
"Ko matodzoka zvekare, inga munerudo neni. Handina kana maminitsi gumi ndabva kukuonai muchindibaya jekiseni nekundipa mapiritsi madzoka zvekare.
Chokwadi ndinotenda nebasa ramunobata pano." Akataura muchinda uya apo Manhiyo nanaLindi vakangotarisana.
"Vasikana asi mambouya muno here?" Akabvunza Manhiyo achifungidzira kuti zvimwe vakanga vambouya. Vasikana vakapindurawo vakati vakanga vasina kumbopinda muchipatara umu vakanga vakarara sezvavakanga vaonekwa vakaita.
"Mashura chaiwo arikuitika pano vasikana, kana ini handina kumbouya muno ndanga ndakatokotsirawo apo ndapepuka ndichiita zvekuvhunduka. Ndipo pamaona ndichikumutsai pane vanhu vauya vakaita mashiripiti chete." Vakataura doctor Manhiyo izvo zvakabva zvatoshamisawo murwere. Akabva atoramba achisimbisa kuti akanga avaona vari vatatu kudaro vachismurapa. Akavaudza zvekare kuti vakanga vamusimbisa kuti mangwana anobuda muchipatara.
 

"Zvisinei ngatingoenda mberi hedu nebasa redu asi iri ishura chairo. Saka mavakunzwa sei pane zvirikuchinja here." Vakabvunza doctor Manhiyo vachida kuziva kuti votangira papi. Lindi naNyari vakanga vari mubishi kutarisa tarisawo zvimwe pamurwere uyu kasanganisira kunzwa kudziya kwemuviri.
"Ndanga ndavakunzwa zvirinani asi ikozvino muviri wangu hauna simba pamwe zvirikuda kuti ndimbozorora. Musoro wangu urikupisa handisi kunzwisisa kuti chii chirikuitika pandiri." Doctor Manhiyo vanobva vatotanga basa pamurwere wavo vachitsvaga kuti dambudziko riripai. Vakaedza nepavanogona asi hapana chavakaona.
"Ndirikunzwa kuda kurutsa chiremba." Anotaura murwere uya apo anobva atanga kurutsa ropa. Varapi vakambotarisana vari vatatu vachishaya kuti chii chakanga chichitora nzvimbo. Murwere uyu akanga asina chirwere chekuti anganzi anorutsa ropa saka chaitova chishamiso.
Yakava bata murefu bata mupfupi varapi vachiedza nepavanogona kutsvaga nzira yekurapa murwere kuti ararame. Murwere akanga ongoridza mhere achitaura kuti akanga achiona zinyoka richimunanzva. Haana kuzogara nguva refu akabva afuga rake ega apo akanga aita zvekunyura mudziva reropa.
 

CHAPTER 6 DISASTER NEBHAZI
Chakava chishamiso pachipatara apa nekuti mafiro akadai vakanga vasati vambomaona. Zvinhu zvainetsa kutambira kuti munhu airapwa mavanga etsaona vozonzwa kuti afa achirutsa ropa. Muchinda akazouya akatamurwa achibva aendwa naye kunoendeswa vashakabvu.
Hazel zvaakabva nevasikana vake pachipatara vakabva vatanga kufamba vachienda nenzira. Vakanga vasati vaziva kuti vachafamba sei uye kuti rimwe basa raitevera nderipi. Chaidiwa kudeura ropa saka chikuru kwakanga kuri kutsvaga panoita kurideura.
Chimwe chikamu chakanga chatopfuura saka yakanga yava nguva yekuti vapinde munechimwe chikamu.
Varipakufamba vakazoona vasvika pachiteshi chemabhazi apo vakambomira.
Ndipo pakanga pava kutangira basa sezvo Hazel akanga afunga zverwumwe rwendo rwekuuraya. Pfungwa yake yaizoita kuti atendwe nekusingaperi nekuti akanga atofunga kudeura ropa zhinji. Hazel ndiye anobva atanga nyaya yacho.
 

"Munoona chii vasikana, apa ndipo patinoda kunyatsoratidza kuti basa ririkubatwa. Anosekerera hake Vicky mwanasikana wemunhu ropa richiuya nebhande. Apa ndafunga kudeura magaroni chaiwo eropa." Akataura Hazel apo Lisa naMillicent vakambotarisana.
"Manga mafungeiko nhai sisi Hazy, titaurirei tigare taziva pekutangira tisasare mumashure." Uyu ndiMillicent aibvunza atononokerwa nekuziva zvairongwa naHazel.
"Matononoka kutiudza sisi Hazy, nzeve dzangu ndatoteya ndatova nenzara yekunzwa nyaya yacho." Akatsinhira Lisa amirira kunzwa zvaifunga mukuru wavo.
"Haisi nyaya inonetsa zvayo vasikana. Tinofanirwa kudeura ropa mubhazi ratichakwira. Rinofanirwa kubheuka robva rauraya munhu wese. Tinenge tabata basa hombe rinodadisa zvekuti kana Vicky anotitenda nemutupo chaiwo." Akadaro Hazel achiudza vasikana vaakanga anawo pfungwa dzake.
Hapana akapokana nazvo zvakanga zvakanak zvakadaro. Vakabva vamirira bhazi nevamwe sezvo riri iro rakanga rine muripo vakaderera. Hapana kutora nguva pakabva pauya bhazi dzvuku rakanga rakanzi Proratar logistics nechepamberi. Vanhu vakatanga kupinda mukati mumwe nemumwe achinotora chigaro chake. Mutyairi akabva atanga rwendo.
 

Bhazi rakatanga richifamba zvishoma sezvo rakanga richiri kunemota dzakawanda. Hazel nevasikana vake vakanga vakagara zvigaro zvekumashure apo vakanga vakapfeka maboni boni matema. Nenguva isipi mutyairi akanga atopinda mumugwagwa unobatanidza Bulawayo neHarare apo akanga ananga kudhorobha.
Mutyairi akanga ava kurivhetemesa zvekuti akanga asina nguva refu apo aizosvika mudhorobha. Vanhu vaingokurukura dzakawanda wanda vachinzwa kamhanzi kairira pasi pasi kubva pachiridzwa misambo yakasiyana siyana.
"Saka zvoitikira papi nhai vasikana, ngatirangarire kuti kudhorobha hakuzi kure tinogona kungosvika pasina zvataita." Akabvunza Hazy apo bhazi rakanga rakamira parobot repaWarren park high richimirira kuti ritenderwe kupfuura.
"Apa zvikaitikira pakateremuka zvinobuda manje, sezvo tavakusvika paNational sports ndipo panonyatsoita." Uyu ndiLisa aipindura achitotarira kumberi. Ndipo pakabva pachinja robot apo mota dzakabva dzatanga kufamba.
"Hazvinetsi vasikana, ini mutyairi ndakumuonesa mota kumberi kwake, isu tinozongonyangarika." Akataura Hazel achisimudza maoko akabatana nevamwe vake.
 

Mutyairi akanga achimhanya zvekuti vanhu vakanga vakabatira ura mumaoko. Vamwe ndiwo vakanga vamujaira vaikwira bhazi iri mazuva ese. Rakatanga kuteremuka materu apaNational sports stadium apo mutyairi aitoita kunge anosvikirwa.
Ndipo paakana mota ichibva kunerimwe divi ichiuya pamberi pake. Apa pakanga pasingaite kumisa bhazi saka akatiziri kudivi rakanga rabva mota iya. Haana kutora nguva apo akaona mota iya yadzoka kudivi kwaakanga ari zvekare. Mutyairi webhazi akangoridza tsamwa achidzokera kudivi raakanga abva zvekare.
Avakusvika paLong cheng plaza ndipo paakazoona mota iya yadzoka pamberi pake zvaasina kuona kuti yauya sei. Paakada kuti aende kunerimwe divi akaona kwakavharwa neimwe mota. Ndipo paakaona kuti pakanga pasina zvekuita achibva aita zvekubuda mumugwagwa.
Bhazi rakanopinga mumugero vakanga uri mudivi menzira. Nemamhanyiro arakanga richiita rakatadza kumira apo rakabva rabheuka nedivi. Pakarepo vanaHazel vakabva varegedzana maoko vachibva vanyangarika ipapo. Vanhu vakazosvika panzvimbo vachiona ropa richierera apo bhazi rakanga raparara zvekusazodzokazve pamugwagawa. Hapana akararama mubhazi umu.
 

CHAPTER 7
DISASTER PACHIKORO
Hazel paakanyangarika nevamwe vake vakatanga kubhururuka mumhepo vakanga kwavaisaziva.
Vanozongoerekana vamhara pakati kati pedhorobha apo vakanga wavakuronga basa raizotevera. Sevanhu vakanga vashanda nguva refu vakanga wavanenzara saka paida kumbotsvaga zvekudya.
Ndipo pavanosvika paibikwa sadza nezvimwe zvakasiyana siyana. Wese vakabva vafungirana apa vati vanoda machips nesausage pamwe nemapepsi.
Vakabva vanogara havo patafura yavo wega vachimirira chikafu chavo.
Pava paya pakazouya muchinda anoshanda apa achivasvitsa chikafu. Vatambidzwa chikafu muchinda uya akamboramba akatarisa Hazel uyo akabva angonyemwerera. Akazobva hake achibva azvisimbisa kuti aizodzoka uye mukombe uyu vakanga usingapfuure asina kuunwa. Pari parunako Hazel aiva chiredzo chevanhu. Vasikana vakadya zvavo chikafu ichi chakanga chakagadzirwa zvine unyanzvi. Vachipedza vakatenda vachibva vaoneka.
 

Vachingobuda pamusuwo muchinda uya wekuvasvitsa chikafu akabva atevera mumashure. Hazel akabva acheuka apo akanzwa mutsindo wemunhu aifamba kumashure kwake. Ndipo paanoona muchinda uya waakanga amboona achiuya. Akambotarira mberi achibva atanga kufamba nevamwe.
"Sisi ndokumbirawo kutaura nemi ndimi wandirikuda." Akataura muchinda uya apo Hazel akaudza vamwe vake kuti vafambe aizotevera. Akabva ataocheuka achidzoka kumuchinda uya. Vakabvunzana mazita apo muchinda uya akazvizivisa saMunya Hazel achimuudzawo rake zita. Muchinda achiona kuti hove yake inenge yaidyira akabva angoburitsa foni yake achitambidza Hazel.
Semwanasikana akabva aziva zvaidiwa achibva anyora nhamba dzake dzefoni. Achipedza akabva adzosera Munya foni yake achibva amuudza kuti azomufonera. Muchinda uya akazovimbisa kufona apo akazoonekana naHazel uyo aiti akanga ari pakumhanya.
Hazel anombofamba kwechinhambwe muchinda uya akayeva. Akazongozvisimbisa kuti panaHazel mukombe vaisazopfuura asina kuunwa. Ko ndiye aigodii zvake iye akanga atorwa moyo nerunako rwemwanasikana. Hazel anozobatana nevamwe vake avo vakanga vazoita zvekumumirira. Ndipo pavakatanga kukurukura vachienda kwavaisaziva.
 

"Chokwadi sisi Hazy makaoma henyu, nguva diki iyoyo manga matoredza kare. Saka mairevesaka musi uya tiri mumusangano kuti runako rwenyu rwunoshanda kuredza varume." Millicent akataura achishamisika nezvaakanga aona zvichiitika. Hazel akangonyemwerera achibva apindura.
"Shamwari ndiri chamangwiza panyaya dzekuredza idzi, iye muchinda uyu kana ndada haasweri asi handizvo zvandinoda kuita. Ndinoda kumbonzwa rudo rwake semunhu asinawo mukomana anomupa rudo.
Tikadanana kana zvemwedzi ndipo pandinobva ndamutorera hupenyu. Akaitawo rombo rakanaka zvimwe haafe anozongouya muchikwata." Akataura Hazel apo vasikana vaakanga anawo vakanyemwerera.
"Asi mukamuuraya munenge makanganisa, uyu anoita kuchikwata chedu manje kunyanya nebasa rake rekushanda nechikafu uchi. Zvinobva zvaita manje nekuti hupenyu hwevanhu vanouya kuzodya ipapo hunenge hwava mumaoko ake." Akataura Lisa achisimbisa Hazel.
"Zvimwe zvacho tinotanga taera munhu, tinogona kuti tinomuda iye asingade zvichireva kuti anenge asina chekuraramira panyika. anenge achitotipedzera nguva." Akadaro Hazel achitaurira vamwe vake avo vakabva vanzwisisa.
 

"Saka zvatava kudokesa zuva kudai tirikudzokera kugungwa here nhasi?" Uyu ndiLisa akanga achibvunza achida kuziva. Kakanga kari kekutanga kufamba naHazel saka aisaziva mashandiro ake. Iye aiti akabuda ega aidzoka pasi pemvura mazuva ese.
"Nhasi hatidzokere kumvura nekuti basa richiripo rakawanda. Ndineimba yangu iri muZimre park yandakasotenga makore maviri apfuura. Ndiko kwatinorara ikoko nekuti pane chikoro chindinoda kuti tinotsvaga nzvimbo mangwana." Akataura Hazel apo basikana vakambotarisana. Ndipo pavakabvunza Hazel kuti akanga afungei zvakanga zvichiita kuti atsvage nzvimbo pachikoro.
Akabva avaudza pfungwa dzake apo akanga afunga zvekuti chikata chikure uye kudeura ropa kune anenge aita rombo rakaipa. Vasikana vakazonzwisisa apo vakatenderana nazvo. Hazel akabva afonera mutyairi vake kuti auye nemota mudhorobha.
Vamwe vangafunga kuti Hazel aitambura saka aifamba nemabhazi asi zvaienderana nebasa raarikuda kuita kuti rinodei. Nenguva isipi mutyairi akanga asvika apo vakabva vatanga rwendo. Nenguva isipi vakanga vasvika muna orange street munova ndimo maiva neimba yaHazel. Musi uyu vakazorara pakati pehusiku vachironga zvavaizoita wava pachikoro.
 

CHAPTER 8
DISASTER PACHIKORO
Husiku hwakavaitira hupfupi apo vakazomuka vachigadzirira zvekunotsvaga nzvimbo. Mutyairi akamuka achibva abuda nevasikana vake. Mota yakavhetemeswa ichibva yanobata mugwagwa unobva Harare uchienda kwaMutare. Vachangoti dzikei mbichana mota yakabva yabuda mumugwagwa mukuru ichipfuura nepachitoro cheTM.
Mutyairi akaenderera mberi nerwendo achibva azoona avakunopinda muSolomio iyo yakanga isina makore yavakwa. Ndiko kwaiva nechikoro chaidiwa nevasikana awa.
Nenguva isipi vakanga vasvika paRukudzo secondary. Chikoro ichi chakanga chichiri pakuvakwa asi chakanga chavakushanda.
Vakabuda mumota muya vachibva vatanga kufamba vachienda kuhofisi yemukuru wechikoro. Vakangopinda muhofisi umu vari vatatu semhuri apo vakanosangana naamai Mufarandadya mukuru wepachikoro apa.
Vakabva vangotaura nyaya yavo.
 

"Ko zvamagouya muri vana mega vabereki wenyu varipi? Pano nguva zhinji ndinoda mwana nemubereki vake kuitira mangwana." Vakataura amai Mufarandadya apo vasikana vakambotarisana. Hazel ndiye akazoshama muromo kuti ataure.
"Ipapo tapanzwa amai, nyaya iripo ndeyekuti amai wedu vanogara kuBotswana saka vanongotumira mari chete. Isu kuno tinogara tega saka zvinhu zvedu zvakawanda tozviitira tega." Hazel achipedza kutaura kudai pakamboita runyararo amai Mufarandadya vachifunga zvimwe zvekutaura.
"Ipapo ndapanzwa vana vangu, asi zvinhu zvakaita sekukupai nzvimbo pano muri mega zvinenjodzi. Ndinoziva sei kana matiza kune chimwe chikoro kana kuti murikuita zvese izvi mubereki asingazivi." Amai Mufarandadya vaitova nenharo chaidzo. Hazy wacho akanga asingapererwi zvekare kana dziri nyaya dzakadai.
"Hapana kuipa amai, tinogona kungovafonera motaura navo mobva magutsikana." Hazel akabva avapa nhamba yaVicky vachibva vafona. Vakataura wese kwekanguva apo akavaudza kuti chokwadi vakanga vari vana vake.
Vachipedza kutaura akabva adambura runhare. Amai Mufarandadya vakazoenderera mberi nekutaura apo vakanga wavakuda mareport ekawaimbodzidza vanasikana ava.
 

Vanobva wavaudza kuti vakanga vasina sezvo kwavaidzidza vakangobva zvisina kuzivisana apo vakanga wavakubuda munzvimbo iyoyo. Mai Mufarandadya vakamboda kuramba nenzvimbo apo vaisaziva vanhu wavarikutamba nawo.
Hazel anozongosimudza musoro achivatarisa mumaziso chaimo. Vakaramba vakatarisana kwechinguva apo akazotarisa pasi. Vamwe vasikana vakazoshamisika vachinzwa kuti nzvimbo yakanga yavapo. Vakabva vatogadzirisa zvese musi uyu apo vaizouya vachitanga kupinda mufomu 3.
Vakaudzwa zvese zvaidiwa vachibva vaenda zvavo. Vachipinda mumota mutyairi akabva atoisimudza ichitarira kwayakanga yabva. Sevanhu vaizotanga chikoro mangwana acho vakabva vatsvaga zvese zvaidiwa. Vakarara zvinhu zvese zviri panzvimbo vangogadzirira kubuda kuseni.
Hakuna kunonoka kuedza apo vakamuka vachigadzirira zvekuchikoro. Vanasikana wevanhu vakanga vakachena zvekuti pachikoro ndiwo vainotora mukombe. Vakanga vakapfeka marokwe avo matema aigumira mumabvi nemashati acho machena. Havana kuzotora nguva apo vakabva vaperekedzwa nemutyairi wavo. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatoburuka pachikoro vachibva vamuudza nguva dzekuzodzoka achivatora.
 

Apa ndipo pakanga patanga basa manje nekuti vakanga wavakukwanisa kuita zvese zvavanoda pachikoro apa. Vaikwanisa kupinza vamwe muchikwata pamwe nekuuraya wavanenge vada. Mazuva akafamba vasikana vachienda kuchikoro vachidzoka masikati. Pakati pehusiku vaipota vachimboenda kumvura pavanenge vachidiwako.
Ndipo pavaisimbiswa kuti vabate basa vasadzore tsvimbo. Mumwe musi vana vakaenda kumakwikwi ekumhanya apo vaikwikwidza nezvikoro zvakapoteredza. Zvikoro zvese izvi zvaiungana pachikoro apa panova ndipo paiva neNhandare yakakura.
Pane muchinda wepachokoro apa aikwikwidza zvekuti vanhu wese vaingoombera paaipinda mudariro. Hazel akanga akagara munevamwe achionawo asi akanga atova nedzimwe pfungwa. Hupenyu hwemuchinda uyu ainzi Peace hwakanga hwatova mumaoko ake.
Peace aimhanya apo rakanga riri jana rake rakupedzisira. Vanhu wese vaiombera maoko zvaibva zvamupa manyemwe ekuwedzera kuenda. Hazel akangoerekana abata tsono mumaoko achibv aipotsera mumhepo yakananga divi iroro. Pakarepo Peace akazongoerekana awira muvhu achibva atanga kurutsa ropa. Yakava batai batai vachiedza kununura mwanabasi vakanga vanonoka. Akabva angofuga rake ega.
 

CHAPTER   9 DISASTER CONTINUES
Chiitiko ichi chakaunza kusuwa pachikoro apa sezvo pakanga pasina kutarisirwa zvakadai. Mai Mufarandadya vakabva vafonera mapurisa kuti asvike pachikoro nekukasika. Vabereki wemwana vakanga varipo apo mutambo uyu vakanga vashevedzwa vabereki.
Amai vacho ndivo vakanga vasisagoni kugarisika moyo uchirwadza. Zvinhu zvaisava nyore kuti munhu anoona mwana vake achitorerwa hupenyu akatarisa.
Zvakazowedzera kurwadza nekuti ndiye akanga akabata mutambo.
Mutambo vakabva vatovharwa sezvo pakanga pasisaite kuti vaende mberi. Zvemusi uyu zvakabva zvapfuura apo Hazel akaenda nevasikana vake vaaifamba nawo kumba.
Peace akazosvika pakuvigwa asara musoro chete ropa rese rapera. Vana wepaRukudzo vakanga varipo pamwechete nevadzidzisi wavo vachionekana negamba ravo. Achipedza kuvigwa vanhu vakabva vaparara.
Yakanga yava nguva yekutarira mberi.
 

Mazuva akaramba achifamba akasvika pakuva mwedzi. VanaHazel vaingoenda kuchikoro vachinosanganawo mevamwe. Mumwe musi Lisa naMillicent vakanga vachifamba nepakati panhandare ari masikati. Vanhu wese pachikoro apa vaingocheuka sezvo runako rwevanasikana awa rwakanga rwakapfurikidza.
Nechekunerimwe divi renhandare kwakanga kune vakomana vaikurukura vakamirira murairidzi wavo webhora. Vakomana ava vakazoerekana vatorwa nerunako rwevanasikana vaipfuura. Pakati pavo pakanga paina Elvis naTawanda avo vakazvipira kuti tinokundikana tasvika.
Vakabva vatotanga kutevera mumashure mevasikana vaya apo mumwe nemumwe akanga asarudza vake. Menguva isipi vakanga vatosvika paiva naLisa naMillie. Nyaya dzakatanga kutsva vachiperekedza vanasikana kwavaisaziva.
Elvis akazenga avakufamba naLisa varikumberi apo Tawanda aifamba naMillicent vari kumashure. Munhu ndiye aizvizivira nyaya yake yaaida kutaura. Kuna Elvis zvakabva zvafamba apo Lisa akabvuma kupinda murudo naye. Panguva imwecheteyo nyaya yaTawanda yakabva yadairwawo naMillicent. Vakazoonekana pava paya sezvo dzakanga dzava nguva dzekuenda kumba.
 

VanaLisa vakazobatana naHazel vachibva vaenda kumota iyo yakanga yatovamirira. Vakapinda mumota mavo muchairi achibva atanga rwendo. Vakasvikomira paTM vachibva vatenga zvibhodhoro zvavo zvewaini yavaida kuzonwa kumberi. Vachibva paTM vakabva vananga kumba. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatogara mumba wava muhurukuro.
Mudariro makabva mapinda yevakomana vatsva vakanga vapfimba Lisa naMillie. Wese vakabva wawirirana kuti machinda aya aifanirwa kufa sezvo Lisa naMillie vakanga vasati vamboendesawo ropa.
Vakazowirirana kuti vaifanirwa kurara nevakomana ava pachikoro ipapo apo vaibva vapedza basa. Zvezuva iri zvakazopfuura vapedza kuronga tsoro yavo. Mazuva akafamba rudo rwuchipisa pakati pevanasikana awa nevanakomana wavakanga vazvisarudzira. Mumwe musi vakanga vachikurukura vari kunhandare vakagara zvavo kamastone bench aivako.
Ndipo pavakaerekana vasimuka vachidzika kusango raiva nechekuzasi kwenhandare. Vazhinji vaikushevedza kuti kuSavanna kunova ndiko kwaibatwa mabasa erima. Vakasvikomira paiva nezimuti remupangara. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatopinda mumutambo werudo mumwe nemumwe achitamba nevake. Vachipedza vakabva vamborara zvishoma vachimirira kuzosimudzira.
 

Pairotwa dzehumambo sevanhu vakanga vari panguva inofadza. Pava paya ndipo pakamuka Elvis achiti amutse mudiwa vake. Akashamisika achiona iri nzvimbo.
Akatarisa paiva pakarara Tawanda achaibva aona ari ega zvekare.
Akamumutsa achida kuti abvunze zvaitota nzvimbo zvimwe aigona kuziva. Tawanda achimutswa akatoshamisikawo kuona mudiwa vake asipo. Chakava chishamiso apo machinda aya akamboramba Ã akatarisana kunge machongwe achangobva kurwa.
Chaishamisa ndechekuti hembe dzevasikana ava dzaivapo kureva kuti vakanga varipedyo.
Varipakati pekufunga kudaro vakazongonzwa mutsindo wechinhu chaiuya kumashure kwavo. Elvis ndiye akatanga kucheuka achibva angopera simba nekuda kwezvaaiona. Tawanda akacheukawo achibva aona zinyoka raakanga asati amboona pasi pano.
Raiva nemisoro miviri nemiswe miviri. Vakomana pavakada kubatanidza nguva dzakanga dzaenda. Vakomana vakabatwa vachibva vatanga kusvetwa ropa muviri wese. Hupenyu hwakabva hwatama pakarepo.
Zinyoka riya rakazoshanduka kuita Lisa naMillie avo vakabva vatanga kufamba vachidzoka kunhandare. Musi uyu vadzidzisi vakazoswera vari mubishi kutsvaga Elvis naTawanda vachivashaya.
 

Nyaya yekushaikwa kwaElvis naTawanda yakatekeshera chikoro chese. Mukuru wechikoro akamboedza kuchaya runhare kuvabereki wemachinda aya asi vakanga vasiko. Ndipo pakazoenda mumwe muchinda achinoudza amai Mufarandadya kuti akanga avaona vachienda kuSavanna vane vasikana vaviri asi haana kuona kudzoka kwavo.
Izvi zvaireva kuti vakanga vachiko saka kwakabva kwatumirwa vadzidzisi kunovatsvaga. Apa mai Mufarandadya vakanga vatovimbisa vadzidzise kuti vabve vachivatinha ikoko nekuti vakanga vachiita zvirikunze kwemutemo.
Kwakaenda vadzidzisi vaviri vakabata mazishamhu vachiti vanodzoka vachitinha vana. Ndipo pavakasvika vachiona shura rakanga risati ramboitika pachikoro apa. Vakaona mitumbi miviri yavanakomana yakarara muvhu vachiratidza kuti mweya vakanga vatama kare.
Zvaitotyisa kuzvitsanangura apo miviri yevana awa yakanga yakazara ropa sezvakanga zvakaita Peace musi uya.
Kwakazofonerwa mapurisa kuti wavatakure uye vabereki wacho vakazofonerwawo. Yakanga iri nguva yekuchema apo Tawanda naElvis vakazovigwa. Zvidzidzo zvakazoenderera mberi mushure mekuchema vanakomana awa.
 

CHAPTER 10 BRIGHTON'S MISSION
Mazuva akaramba achifamba zvose zvairongwa pasi pemvura. Mumwe musi vakaita musangano zvekare vachizivisana chinhanho chavakanga wavo nebasa ravo. Hazel ndiye ainyanyotendwa nekuti akanga achibata basa pese paaienda panyika.
Vicky akanga akagara pachigaro chake chemazuva ese vari pahurukuro. Akashevedza Lisa naMillicent achibva avakorokotedza nekuda kwebasa ravakanga vabata.
Hazel uyo akanga akagara pedyo naVicky semutevedzeri vake aingonyemwerera sezvo ariye akanga avasimbisa mubasa.
Vicky akazotarisa kwaiva nevamwe wese achida kunzwa zvavakanga vachironga. Chinangwa chaiva chekuda kuziva kuti vakanga wavapapi nezvavakanga vachivimbisa pazuva ravakaita musangano.
Brighton akabva apinda mudariro achizivisa vamwe vake kuti hurongwa hwake hwakanga hwave pedyo. Akanga ane rwendo rwekuenda kuJapan asi aitanga amboona mota yainyanyotengwa nevanhu. Achipedza kudaro aibva amboenda kunogara kuJapan achiita zvemota.
 

Vamwe wese vakazovimbisa kuti vakanga vari munzira kuzadzisa zvavakanga wavimbisa. Brighton akazovimbisa kuti aizoswera achitenderera nenyika achiona mota yakawandirwa munzira. Vachipedza mudangono vakabva vanyangarika zvavanosiita.
Mumwe memumwe akaenda kunzvimbo yaairarama ari.
Brighton akanga akasarudza kugara muDawnview park achiita zvinhu zvake arimo. Imba yake yaiva yedzimwe imba hombe dzaiverengwa munzvimbo iyi. Akamuka ari makuseni achibva ambotanga nekutenderera pachivanze chake.
Ndipo paaiona maruva anoyevedza achimbovarairwa nekumatarisa. Ari pakutenderera kudaro akabva atanga kukwenya musoro apo akanga afunga zvebasa. Ndipo paakatanga kufunga kwaaizotangira basa rake rekuongorora mota dzake panzira.
Haana kuda kutambisa nguva akabva ananga kumota yake yaaifarira kufamba nayo nguva zhinji. Yaiva mota yerudzi rweRange Rover iri tsvuku. Nenguva isipi akanga atoimutsa achibva abuda muchivanze achienda kwaaisaziva. Akazoona abata mugwagwa mukuru unobva Harare uchienda Bulawayo. Akabva asarudza kuenda nedivi reHarare apo aida kunopinda mudhorobha. Mota yakavhetemeswa zvekuti nenguva isipi akanga atopinda mudhorobha.
 

Paaifamba akamboita ongororo zvishoma asi akanga asati apedza. Akambotenderera mudhorobha achibva abuda akananga kwaMutare. Achibva kwaMutare akatenderera nedzimwe nzvimbo dzakapoteredza Zimbabwe. Akararira kufamba apo akaswera ari munzira zvekare. Mushure memazuva mashanu ndipo paakazodzoka pamba ava nemhinduro.
Rwendo rwake rwakanga rwava kuzotanga sezvo akanga avakuziva mota dzake dzaaida. Akabva atanga nekutoronga zvekugadzira makombi nekuti ndiwo mamwe emota dzaakanga aona pamwe nedzerudzi rwemaToyota Wish nedzimwewo dzaiva muchikwata ichochi.
Kumabhazi akanga aona erudzi rweYutong ayo akanga akawandirwa kudarika mamwe mabhazi ese. Izvi zvaireva kuti aizoita rwendo rwekuChina zvekare kunova ndiko kwaibva rudzi rwemabhazi aya. Akagara pasi achibva atanga kufunga kuti yaizofamba sei tsoro yake iyi.
Akazoronga kuti aizonotsvaga basa mumakambani anogadzira mota apo aizongomirira kuongorora mota inenge ichinzi yakodzera kuenda pamugwagwa. Akanga asina zvikwanisiro asi aiva nesimba rekupinda basa racho. Achipedza kuronga tsoro dzake akabva agadzirira apo aizokwira ndege kuenda kuJapan.
 

Tikiti akanga atenga kare apo aizotora KLM airways iyo yaitanga yaenda nekuNetherlands. Semunhu aida kufamba husiku hwakaita hurefu asi hapana nguva isingasvike. Ndege yaida kuenda naBrighton yaizosimuka masikati saka akamboswera hake achiona nzvimbo kekupedzisira.
Mwanakomana wemunhu akatorana nezvinhu zvake zvaaizoenda nazvo akananga kumota. Zvinhu zvese zvava panzvimbo mota yakazosimudzwa apo yaiva nemutyairi vake aimbopota achifamba naye.
Yakavhetemeswa mota yakananga nekudivi renhandare yendege.
Havana kutora nguva vari munzira vakanga vatosvika panhandare yendege. Pakambova nekusuwa pakati paBrighton nemutyairi vake apo vaivimbisana kuzoonana zvekare. Vakazoonekana apo Brighton akazoita zvese zvaidiwa asati apinda mundege.
Nenguva isipi ndege yakanga yatova mudenga apo yaizotanga yaenda kuSchipol airport kuNetherlands. Yaizosimudzira yakananga kuTokyo kuJapan. Rwaiva rwendo rwurefu apo Brighton aiva muFirst class.
Akazosvika kuTokyo mangwana acho apo akanga ava manheru. Akasvikorara muhotera apo aizotanga basa rake kwaedza.
 

CHAPTER 11 MISSION CONTINUES
Kuchiedza basa raBrighton rakanga ratotanga. Yakanga yava nguva yekuti ambotenderera achiona nzvimbo pamwe nekusvika nzvimbo dzinogadzirwa mota achitsvaga basa. Semunhu akanga asati awana zvaanoda aitofanirwa kushanda nesimba.
Rwendo rwakazotanga apo akatanga kutenderera achitsvaga makambani emota. Rwaiva rwendo rwurefu apo aimbotenderera achiona kushongedzwa kwakanga kwakaitwa nyika iyi. Ndipo paakazosvika paigadzirwa mota dzakafanana nedzakamboona paakaita ongororo yake. Izvi zvaireva kuti basa rakanga rava kutanga asi aisangopinda nyore semunhu akanga asina mapepa akakwana.
Ndipo pakanga pavakufanirwa kushandiswa simba riya repasi pemvura kuti apinde basa raakanga achida. Asati apinda pakambani iyi akabva asimudza ruoko mudenga achibva akotamisa uso hwake. Akataura mashoka echimwe chirudzi chaisanzwika achibva atanga kufamba achienda kumahofisi ekambani iyi. Nenguva isipa akanga atopinda muhofisi yemukuru webasa.
 

Ndipo paakambopinda muhurukuro apo aivaudza nyaya yake. Mukuru weapa akamboda kutsika tsika apo akabva aitwa zvekutariswa mumaziso chaimo. Mukuru uya akazoerekana audza Brighton kuti basa rakanga riripo uye ndiye munhu vaaitotsvaga chaiye.
Brighton akazotenderera nemukuru uya achiratidzwa mamiriro akanga akaita pakambani pese. Kwese kunogadzirirwa mota akaratidzwa apo aitsanangurirwa magadzirirwo adzinoitwa pamwechete nezvadzinitaridirwa kunge dzakaita kuti dzikodzere kufamba mumugwagwa.
Vachipedza kutenderera Brighton akabva apihwa bepa rekusaina raitaura kuti akanga atotanga basa. Aizopota achiita zvekufonerwa ouya achiongorora mota dzake. Achipedza kusaina bepa rake akabva aenda. Semunhu aiva nemari yakawanda akabva adzokera kuhotera kwake kwaaizogara panguva yese yaanenge achienda kubasa.
Mazuva aifamba mota dzichigadzirwa pakambani pakanga patsvagwa basa naBrighton. Dzaigadzirwa nehuwandu hwadzo apo dzaimirira kuzoongororwa. Ndipo pakabva pafonerwa Brighton kuti auye achiita ongororo yake. Mota yese yaaizoti inokodzera yaibva yatopinda mumusika. Achisvika akabva atanga kuita ongororo dzake.
 

Akatanga achamboongorora dzimwe apo akabva asvika pane makombi aaida. Akabva atora tumatracking devices twaakanga ainatwa apo aida kutwuisa pane mwe makombi acho. Nditwo twaizoita kuti azive mota dzinofanirwa kuita tsaona.
Akasvika pane dzimwe diki achibva aita zvimwechetezvo. Aiti yese yaanenge aisa aisimudza ruoko achitaura chirudzi chiya chisinganzwike obva apfuura hake achienda kumberi. Sezvineiwo pakabva pasvika mumwe muchinda aida mota dzakanga dzagadzirwa apa.
Sezvo Brighton ari iye aitendera kuti mota ipinde pamugwagwa ndiye akabva atanga kuita basa rekutengesa racho. Muchinda uya akabhadhara makombi ake ayo ainzi aizoenda nechikepe. Mazuva zvaaifamba chikepe chakasvika kwaizofanirwa kushanda makombi aya.
Brighton aigara ari pakombiyuta yake achiongorora mafambiri aiita mota dzake dzaakanga aendesa.
Pakazenge paenda nedzimwe diki zvekare dzakanga dzatengwa nevakawanda. Chake kwaiva kugara achiona zvinenge zvichiita mota dziya dzichifamba dziri kwadziri. Ndiye aizova nesimba rekupinza yaanenge achida mutsaona ropa robva radeuka.
 

Mutyairi aingogarawo sezita asi Brighton akanga ane simba rekumukotsirisa ari kwaari. Kana afunga kuuraya aingoita zvaanoita akagara pamuchina vake mota yotobheuka kana kubondera iri kwainenge iri.
Mumwe musi akanga akagara pamuchina vake achiona mota dzake dzakanga dziri pamugwagwa. Ndipo paaiona mafambiro adzo apo akanga ane dzimwe pfungwa. Nguva yakanga yakwana yekuti ambodeura ropa sezvo rakanga rava kudiwa.
Akagara pamuchina kudaro ndipo paaiona makombi maviri achidzingirirana akananga divi rekudhorobha. Anobva anzwa inzwi munzeve make richitaura kuti tirikuda ropa ona zvekuita pamota idzi. Panguva iyoyo panobva pabuda imwe Toyota wish ichienda kudivi raibva makombi. Brighton akabva atanga kutaura nechimwe chirudzi achifambisa ruoko rwake kurudyi nekuruboshwe. Panguva iyoyo Toyota wish iya yakabva yaputika vhiri ichitiza mumugwagwa mayo. Payakatiza mugwagwa yakabva yasvika ichirovana nekombi izvo zvakaita kuti iparare kusara yakaita kunge bhora.
Kombi yakapararawo zvekuti yakauraya vazhinji vamwe vakakuvara. Imwe yacho yaitevera mumashure yakaedza kunzvenga ichibva yapidiguka nedivi. Brighton akazobva hake pamuchina achinzwa kuombera kwemaoko semunhu akanga agona basa.
 

CHAPTER 12
DEVIL ON THE MISSION
Nekunerimwe divi Jonhson akanga achironga tsoro yake yekuputsa makereke munyika. Ndipo paanotanga kufamba achienda kwaaisaziva. Chaaingoziva ndechekuri kana iri svondo haashaye paanoona pachidanwa zita raMwari. Yakanga itori nguva yekuti abate basa riende mberi. Nekunerimwe divi Pastor Mazondo vakanga vari pakuparidza vhangeri vana wesangano vakateerera. Vaingonzwa mhururu nemiridzo wobva vaziva kuti vana vakomborerwa.
Vainyatsonzwa kuti Mufundisi vari pabasa ravo.
"Nhasi ndoda kuti mubatisise mashoko aya hama wadiwa. Shoko randinoda kukuudzai ishoko razvokwadi uye achateerera achapona. Ndopa mbiri kunaiye musiki atisanganisa muzuva ranhasi kuti tisimbisane pashoko razvokwadi iri. Ndinoda kuti tose tigare takachenjera nekuti hapana anoziva misi nenguva zvichauya mwanakomana wemunhu." Pastor Mazondo vachipedza kutaura mashoko aya vakambokosora mbijana. Ndipo pavakambopukata kumeso nekajira vachibva vasimudzira.
 

"Zvino ichasvika nguva yekuti huipi huchawanda asi vakakomborerwa vachakunda kusvika pazuva rekupedzisira. Shoko rinotaura roti hapana ibwe richazoiswa pamusoro perimwe akasazowisirwa pasi ese. Nguva ichakwana apo nyika ichaguma ngatigarei takagadzirira." Pastor Mazondo vanombopukuta dikita nekachira kavo kaya. Vachipedza vakabva vasimudzira apo vanhu wese vakanga vateya nzeve kuti vanyatsonzwa shoko.
"Zvirokwazvo ndinoti dai mateerera shoko razvokwadi murege kutsauswa nemunhu, shoko rinobva rataura kuti muchenjere kutsauswa nemunhu nekuti kune vachauya nezita rangu vachitsausa vazhinji. Vaporofita wenhema vachavapo hama wadiwa nazvino vatova panyika. Shoko rotaura kuti vachaita zviratidzo zvikuru kuti vakutsausei. Hama dzangu tisazonamata nekuda kwezviratidzo zvatinenge taoneswa asi tinamate Jesu nemoyo wese." Panomboita maungira vanhu vachifarira shoko rakanga rataurwa naMufundisi.
Mufundisi Mazondo vaiti kana wavakuparidza vanhu wese vanenge vari mukereke vaidzikama. Kana pane munhu anga achipfuura panzira aitotadza kuenda mberi nerwendo rwake abatwa pamoyo nevhangeri. Rimwe gore ndivo vakamboparidza mumwe munhu akanga auya kuzovaedza akadonhedza nyoka mukereke.
 

Kana tasvika pashoko razvokwadi Mufundisi uyu akanga akatumwa zvokwadi. Akakubata musoro akakukumbirira kuti upore vaisadzokera vakadaro. Rimwe gore vakatombosvika pana amai vaitengesa mabanana vachibva vakumbira kungomabata senzira yekuropafadza bhizimusi. Hapana kutora nguva pakabva patosvika mhene yaida mabanana ese iwayo nemari yaidarika yakanga yakatarisirwa maamai ava. Ndiyo zodzo yakanga ina Mufundisa Mazondo.
Vanozoenderera zvavo mberi nevhangeri rovo apo vanhu vakazenge vanyarara.
"Ndinoda kuti musimbe mutsunge moyo parwendo rwatiri kufamba urwu." Vanodaro Mufundisi vachitsinhira mashoko aiudzwa Joshua panguva yaakasarudzwa kuti atungamirire vana vaIsraeri.
"Ndoda kuti mutsunge moyo nekuti muchafamba semakwai pakati pemapere. Vakaipa achauya pamberi penyu semakwai asi mukati vari mapere anoparadza. Mugare makarindira nekuti hapana anoziva misi nenguva. Mwene wemba haazivi musi unouya mbavha saka nemi garai makarindira. Kana ndichitaura zvekugara makarinda handirevi kuti rarai makasvinura kudzimba dzenyu. Ndinoreva kuti garai muchiita zvakanaka nguva dzose." Pakamboita maungita zvekare vanhu vachiombera mufundisi.
 

Panguva iyoyo pakabva panzwikwa kutinhira kwemota panze. Vanhu wese vakanga vari mukereke vakabva vacheuka apo vaiona rudzi rwemota yavakanga vasati vamboona ichiuya apa. Ndiyo mhando yemota yavaingogumira kuona pamifananidzo.
Panguva iyoyo mufundisi vakatombokanganwa kuti vari kuparidza apo vakanga vayevedzwa nemota yakanga iri panze. Vakaramba vakatarisa mota iya vachienzanisa neToyota Noah yavaifamba nayo vachibva vazviona vasiri chinhu. Yaiva mota yerudzi rweLarmbogini Gallardo iri yeruvara rwenhundurwa.
Vakaramba vakatarira vachibva vaona muchibuda muchinda mutsvuku murefu uyo akanga akasimba zviri pakati nepakati. Akanga akapfeka sutu nhema pamwe nemaboni boni acho matema. Akapinda mukereke muya achibva ananga paiva nechimwe chigaro chisina munhu. Panguva yese iyi Mufundisi vakanga vakatarisa kusvika agare pasi.
Vanhu vanozodzosa maziso kuna Mufundisi vachiona kuti akanga asonyarara kuparidza kare. Ivo Mufundisi vakazotoita zvekuvhunduka vachiona kuti vakanga vatokanganwa zvemharidzo. Havana kuzoenda mberi apo vakabva vazopedza mharidzo yavo.
 

CHAPTER 13 MISSION CONTINUES
Mufundisi pavakavhara mharidzo vakabva vaisa munamato vachikumbirira vatendi wavo kuti vagokomborerwa. Pavainamata vaimboita vachivhura maziso wombotarisa muchinda uye weLarmbogini.
Pamwe pacho vaimboita vachikanda ziso kumusuwo kunova ndiko kwakanga kune mota.
Vachipedza munamato vakabva vagara havo pachigaro chavo chakanga chiri kumberi pamwe nezvimwe zvevaivatevera. Zvaiva kumberi apo vaigara vakatarisa kuvatendi wavo. Pakabva pasimuka mumwe muchinda uyo aipota achipa hurongwa hwechechi kusvika payaizopera.
Muchinda uya akabva atanga nekusimudza vaenzi wese vakanga vashanya muzuva iri kuzoshumira navo. Ndivo vakanga uri mukana wekuti vazivane kuitira mangwana.
Sekukumbirwa kwazvakanga zvaitwa vaenzi vakasimuka nehuwandu hwavo vachizvizivisa muimba yaMwari.
Muchinda uya akazopihwawo mukana wekuzvizivisa sezvo akanga asimukawo nevaenzi. Panguva iyi maziso evanhu pamwe naMufundisi akanga ava kwaari.
 

"Rugare vanhu vashe, rugare vanhu vaMwari. Ndinotenda nekundigamuchira kwamaita muimba ino tsvene yakagadzirirwa vanotenda. Neniwo ndinofara kuva pakati penyu ndichinzwa kunaka kweukuru hwaMwari." Vanhu wese vamamboombera maoko vachibva vazonyarara kuti aenderere mberi.
"Zvichakadaro zita rangu ndinonzi mukoma Jonhson ndinogara kuZimre park. Handina kereke yandinobata ndiri parizvino ndiri pakutenderera. Kana Mwari vanditendera ndichabata nemi kusvika ndapinda muguva." Akataura muchinda uya achibva agara pasi. Akatoita zvekuperekedzwa neziso raMufundisi kunogara pasi.
Muchinda uya aifambisa hurongwa akabva asimuka zvekare kuti aenderere mberi. Ndipo paakabva apa mukana uyu kune vakanga vazvipira kupa hupenyu hwavo kuna Kristu. Nguva iyi yaidiwa nevashoma avo vanenge vari pachokwadi chekuda kutendeuka.
Jonhson akabva asimuka zvekare panguva iyi kuti azvipe kumusiki. Akabva apupura pamberi pevanhu wese kuti akanga azvipira kubata nevamwe vachishumira shoko iri. Pakamboita maungira emhururu nemiridzo vanhu vachofarira mutendi mutsva. Mukoma Jonhoson vakazogara pasi muchinda uya achibva azosimuka zvekare kuti aenderere mberi nehurongwa.
 

Ndipo pakabva papihwa mukana wekubvisa zvipo apo mumwe nemumwe aiuya achikanda chipo chake mubucket raiva kumberi kuna Mufundisi. Vanhu vaiti anenge akanda chipo obva abatwa musoro naMufundisi senzira yekumuropafadza. Panguva iyoyo Jonhson akanga achiteveranawo nevamwe kuti abvise chipo.
Achisvika kumberi kwaiva naMufundisi akabva aburitsa mari yakanga yakasungwa ari ma100us ega yaisaverengeka. Panguva iyoyo Pastor vakamboita kunge varikurota vachitadza kuzvitenda kuti ndivo vakanga vachiona mari iyi. Vanhu wese mukereke vakatombomhanyisa maziso avo wese ikoko vachiona huwandu hwemari yavakanga vasati vamboona.
Mufundisi vakangobata Jonhson vachibva vamubata musoro vachimuropafadza. Vakabva vatomuudza kuti Mwari vamuropafadze nekusingaperi vamupe imwe mari yakawanda. Nguva yezvipo ichipera muchinda uya akazosimuka avakupa zviziviso kuvanhu.
Achipedza kupa zviziviso vanhu vakabva vanzi vaende zvavo. Mumwe nemumwe akabuda achienda kumba kwake apo vamwe vainanga kudzimota dzavo. Vanasisi wemukereke ndivo vakazongoonekwa vaungana pamota yaJonhson vachichinjana kutorwa mifananidzo vakaizembera.
 

Jonhson vacho akatomboshaya pekupinda napo mumota make apo akazopedzisira apindawo pakutorwa mifananidzo nanasisi wemuchechi pamwe nanamai.
Wese vaitoita kurwidzana hapana aida kutangirwa kutorwa mufananidzo ana mukoma Jonhson.
Mufundisi vakazobudawo mukereke apo vakanga vachinyara kunopinda mumota mavo. Vanombomira vakayeva mota yaJonhson pamwe nevanhu vakanga varipo apo vakazongozviudza kuti rimwe gore ndichaitawo yangu yakadai. Vakazoshevedza Jonhson apo vakambokwazisana mumaoko vasati vatanga kukurukura.
Havana kuita hurukuro yakakura vakangopanana nhamba dzefoni apo vakazovimbisana kufonerana. Mufundisi vakazopinda mumota mavo vachibva vaenda nemhuri yavo. Jonhson akapindawo mumota make avakunanga kwaanogara.
Akavhetemesa mota kubva kuMarondera kwaipindirwa chechi iyi achidzoka kuZimre park. Nenguva isipi akanga atopinda munaZimre drive apo asina kuzotora nguva kusvika pamba pake. Chaingova chinhambwe chidiki kubva pamba paHazel. Husiku hwemusi uyu akazorara ava kumusangano kwavaisangana achivaudza mafambiro aakanga aita.
 

CHAPTER 14 DEVIL AT WORK
"Tiudze tinzwe Jonhson, kwanga kurisei kumasango kwavanga uchifamba uko. Ndinovimba kuti pane zvirikufamba ikoko." Akadaro Vicky achibvunza Jonhson uyo akanga achangobva kusvika. Vamwe vakanga vasati vasvika asi vakanga vachiri munzira.
"Tirimo musango mambo wangu, pane kereke yandapinda ndiripakuvhima asi pane chandaona hangu. Mufundisi wavo ndatomukurira simba chasara kungosangana naye chete uye ndichauya naye kuno." Akapindura Jonhson Vicky achibva ambonyemwerera.
"Saka zvese zviri mugwaraka, ndinovimba kuti tichamuraura unofanirwa kudzokera vawedzera masimba nekuti unogona kuona Mufundisi ava nedzimwe pfungwa. Wongwarira zvekare mukereke make imomo munogona kuzongomuka mumwe anesimba akakwanisa kumutsa Mufundisi ukazotadza kuvaredza, ukasike kurova simbi ichapisa." Akadaro Vicky achiyambira Jonhson. Jonhson akagutsurira musoro kureva kuti zvaiva munzeve. Anozoenderera mberi achipindura mashoko aVicky.
 

"Izvo zvekurova simbi ichapisa ndizvo chaizvo, dambudziko randaona panaMufundisi rinozoita kuti ndivaraure nderekuchiva upfumi. Pandasvika paKereke pavo neLarmbogini yangu vatombokanganwa kuti ndiwo vari kuparidza. Vanhu wese wanga vakaisa maziso kwandiri kusvika ndigare pasi. Saka chiredzo chaMufundisi imari." Akadaro Jonhson achiudza mambokadzi vake divi rakanga rakareruka pana Mufundisi.
Vicky anozosimbisa Jonhson kuti aramba akabata pakareruka ipapo kusvika aredza Mufundisi. Pana Mufundisi ndipo pakanga pane basa rese kana vapedza ipapo kuredza kereke yese kwaisanetsa. Panguva iyi vamwe vakazenge vasvikawo apo vakanga vokurukura mafambiro avakanga vachiitawo munzvimbo dzavakanga vari.
Zvairatidza kuti zvese zvakanga zvichirongwa zvaiva mugwara nekuti wese vaiuya vachipupura. Vachipedza hurukuro dzavo vakabva vadzokera sekuuya kwavakanga vaita.
Jonhson akazoona asvika kumba kwake kuZimre park. Ndipo paakanga akarara zvake akatarisa mudenga achifunga zano raizomuendesa mberi. Pakarepo foni yake yakabva yarira. Achitarisa akabva aona vari Mufundisi vaifona. Akabva aidaira nekukasika.
 

"Munhu waMwari munofara here?" Akadaro Jonhson achimirira kuzonzwa mashoko aibva kunerimwe divi renhare.
"Ndinofara zvangu mukoma hameno kana makafambawo zvakanaka kubva kukereke." Akadaro Mufundisi apo ainzwika kubva kunerumwe rutivi.
"Haiwa rwendo ndakafamba zvakanaka hameno imiwo kana makasara zvakanaka nemhuri dzese." Akadaro Jonhson achida kunzwawo kana Mufundisi vakasara zvakanaka.
"Haiwa tose takasara mushe, mukoma ndaizokumbirawo kana makasununguka rimwe zuva mugondishanyirawo. Ndine hurukuro yandinoda kuita nemi." Vakadaro Mufundisi vachikumbira nguva naJonhson kumba kwavo.
"Hapana chakaipa Mufundisi, kungondiudza zuva ramunondida chete ndinouya. Nguva zhinji ndogara ndine mukana vakakura saka hazvinditorere nguva kuuya kumba kwenyu." Akadaro Jonhson achipindura Mufundisi.
"Zvakanaka mukoma, ini ndinowanikwa zuva radoka ndabva kubasa ndipo pamunouya." Vakadaro Pastor Mazondo apo vaiudza Jonhson nguva dzavanobatika pamba pavo.
 

Mushure mehurukuro runhare rwakabva rwadambuka. Ndipo pakatarisa Jonhson nguva achiona dziri kuma2. Saka zvaireva kuti pasi pemvura haana kumbogarisa nekuti vaiwanzodzoka kunze kwavakuda kuchena.
Akabva arara hake achipedzisa hope dzake achimirira kuti kuchene.
Ndipo paakatanga kufunga zvaaizoita kana achinge azodzika midzi mukereke umu. KwaMufundisi akabva atoronga kukasika kuendako onzwa nyaya yakanga yakamumirira. Sezvineiwo nguva hadzina kunonoka kufamba kunze kwakabva kwaedza.
Mufundisi vakamuka vachigadzirira kuenda kubasa kwavo. Vaishanda saAccountant pakambani yemabhazi yainzi Proratar logistics kunova ndiko kwaibva raramo yavo. Vasati vabuda vakabva vaona meseji kubva kuna Jonhson achiti aizouya manheru emusi uyu. Mufundisi vakabva varaira mudzimai wavo kuti agobika chikafu chakanaka sezvo vaizotsikwa nemuenzi.
Nguva dzakafamba apo Mufundisi vakanga vanonokerwa nekupedza basa. Nechekunerimwe divi Jonhson akanga atogadzirira kushanyira Mufundisi. Zvemusi uyu akabva asarudza kuvashanyira neimwe mota yake tsvuku iri yerudzi rweFomatic. Akapinda munzira achibva ananga kwaMufundisi. Nenguva isipi akanga atosvika.
 

CHAPTER 15 MEETING NAPASTOR
Akasvikomira pagedhe paakanga arairwa achibva aridza bhero. Pasina nguva akaona gedhe richivhurwa pachibva pabuda kamukomana kechidiki. Akabva arairwa kuti apinde apo akasvikochingurwa naMufundisi mukati.
Panguva yaakakwazisana naMufundisi vakatombokanganwa nezvake vakayeva mota. Vakanga vachishamisika nekuti mota yavakanga vachiona panguva iyi yakanga yakasiyana neyavakamboona pakutamba. Vakazopinda havo mumba apo Jonhson akasvika achipihwa pekugara.
Mai Mufundisi vakabva vatorairwa kuti vabikire muenzi chikafu chakanaka. Chikafu chichibikwa Mufundisi vaitotandara zvavo naJonhson.
Ndipo pavaikurukura dzehupenyu apo vaibata bata zvinoitika munyika. Nenguva isipi Mai Mufundisi vakazopedza kubika. VaMufundisi vakabva vananga kuimba yekudyira naJonhson apo vakadya chikafu chakanga chakabikwa nehunyanzvi.
 

Panguva iyi Amai Mufundisi vaigadzira imba yekutandara nevaenzi vanenge vashanya kuti vaite hurukuro nemunhu waMwari. Vakazodzoka vachiona Mufundisi naJonhson vapedza kudya. Amai Mufundisi vakangotora ndiro vachibva vabuda havo. Mufundisi vakazobudawo naJonhson vakananga kuimba iya yakanga ichigadzirwa nemudzimai. Ndipo pavakabva vatanga kukurukura.
"Saka chikomana urikuzvigona sei kunze uku, ndimika varidzi wemari chimbotiudzaika kuti dzirikuwanika sei." Vakadaro Mufundisi vachibvunza Jonhson kwaibva hupfumi hwake.
"Tinenge tichingotsvaga tsvaga tirimo mukati imomo tozongomuta hedu takaita mari, mari inoda kutsvagwa Mufundisi uye haidi kutya kuitsvaga nekuti munofa nenhamo." Akadaro Jonhson apo Mufundisi vakambonyarara kwekanguva. Vakazowana zvekutaura pava paya.
"Zvakanaka chikomana ndinofara kuva nemunhu akaita sewe mukereke mangu, zvinosimudzirawo vamwe vanenge vachikuona vanonzwa shungu vakatevedzerawo zvakanaka. Kana neni ndatovawo neshungu dzekuita sewe." Vakadaro Mufundisi apo vakanga vatapirirwa nehupenyu hwaJonhson.
 

"Izvi hazvinetsi Mufundisi, ndongoendawo nemi kwandinoenda hamupedzi mwedzi munenge matova nemari isingaverengeki. Kamota kenyu kamunofamba nako ako munenge mavakupa mwana mucheche kuti atambise." Mashoko akataurwa apa akambobata Mufundisi vachibva vamboramba vakanyarara.
Chokwadi mota yavakanga vatambura kuitenga mumwe mungu oti ndeyekupa mwana achitambisa. Hongu iyi yakanga yavabata asi vane mamwe mashoko avakanga vanzwa zvekare panhau iyi.
"Ko kwamunoreva kuti munoenda neni ndekupi Mukoma Jonhson, tauraika muchipedza toziva kwatinenge takananga. Munoti pane kwatingaenda ndikaswera ndatenga mota inenge yenyu iya pamwedzi mumwechete here. Muchadaro mukatirombesa mukoma im." Mufundisi vakataura mashoko aya vachibva vamboseka zvavo. Jonhson akaona kuti anogona kuirasa achibva afunga zvekushandisa simba rake panguva iyi.
Akangotarisa Mufundisi mumaziso apo akaramba akadaro. Kazhinji aiti akadaro mumunhu anenge avakuteerera zvese zvaanenge ataura. Apa yakanga yava nguva yekuzviedza pamunhu waMwari oona kuti zvinoitasei. Mufundisi vakambobata bata maziso avo apo Jonhson akaenderera mberi achivapindura.
 

"Mufundisi zvimwe zvacho hazvidi kuti tipedze nguva tichibvunzana. Chikuru kuenda kwandataura mobva mazvionera. Patinobva ikoko munondiudza Mufundisi kana kereke inokura mukafa nemari." Mufundisi panguva iyi vakabva vatapirirwa nemashoko amukoma Jonhson.
"Pakanaka mukoma Jonhson, senge pamati kereke inoda kukura apa ndapabatisisa. Kuti kereke ikure zvinodawo ini Mufundisi wacho ndichionekera ndowanawo chiremera pamberi pevana wesangano. Kuti zvidaro zvinenge zvichidawo ndinemari seyenyu iyi mukoma Jonhson." Vakadaro Mufundisi apo vakabva vamboseka wese.
Vakakurukura apo vakanga wavakuronga zuva rekuenda. Mufundisi vakanga vatononokerwa nekuenda kwakanga kuchirehwa nemuchinda uyu. Vakanga vatova nechidokwa dokwa chekuziva kuti kwakanga kunei kwaiendwa naJonhson.
Jonhson akazoudza Mufundisi kuti vakanga vakasununguka kuenda naye pavanenge vadira. Vakazowirirana kuti vaizotaura pafoni. Vapedza kukurukura Mufundisi vakazotanga kutaura nyaya yavakanga vashevedzera Jonhson.
 

CHAPTER 16 THE JOURNEY
"Chikomana nyaya yandakushevedzera haina kumbokura, zvimwe tingakurukura hedu asi pane nyay yandinayo." Vakadaro Mufundisi apo vakambokosorera.
"Inyaya yeiko nhai Mufundisi wangu. Ndinovimba kuti nyaya yacho yakanaka." Akadaro Jonhson avakuda kuziva nyaya yacho. Mufundisi vakabva vaenderera mberi nekutaura.
"Ndakaongorora ndikaona kuti vashoma vakomana wechidiki vakarongeka sewe. Zvichakadaro ndakaona zvekare kuti kana ndikaita munhu akaita semi mukoma muhutungamiri hwangu kereke inoenda mberi.
Ndafunga kudaro ndakazofunga kukupai chigaro muchechi." Vakadaro Mufundisi Jonhson achibva asvetuka nemufaro. Basa rake raakanga avinga panyika rakanga richifamba negwara.
"Munorevesa here Mufundisi? Kana neni ndineshungu dzekuti shoko raMwari riende mberi uye vashumiri vanotitevera vakomborerwe." Akadaro Jonhson mushure mekunge audzwa mashoko anofadza naMufundisi.
 

"Ndinorevesa chikomana, ndakagara ndazviona kuti unemoyo vakanaka uye haudi kuona kereke ichidzoka kumashure ndosaka ndakasarudza iwe. Ndiwe uchange uri mutevedzeri wangu kureva kuti unenge une chigaro cheufundisi zvekare." Vakadaro Mufundisi apo Jonhson akambonyarara zvishoma. Akazoshama muromo pava paya kuti ataure.
"Mufundisi ndinotenda nekundisimudzira kwamaita, hazvisi nyore kuti munhu anopinda mukereke zuva rekutanga obva atopihwa basa rekufudza makwai. Basa ramandipa Mufundisi muchaona kuti kereke ichasvika kure uye vanhu vachakomborerwa." Akadaro Jonhson chiso chake chizere nemufaro.
Vakazowirirana naMufundisi kuti aizogadzwa pamberi pevana wesangano nesvondo apo aibva atanga kubata basa mukereke umu. Vachipedza hurukuro yavo vakabva vabuda zvavo apo vakamboenda kuimba yekutandarira. Ndiko kwavakambogara vachiona chivhiti vhiti.
Vakambotandara kwekanguva apo Jonhson akazooneka sezvo nguva dzakanga dzafamba. Akaonekawo Mai Mufundisi achibva abuda. Akasvikosiiwa pamusuwo wemota yake naMufundisi achibva apinda mukati.
Nenguva isipi akanga atotarira nzira apo Mufundisi vakamuperekedza neziso kusvika asisaoneke.
 

Vakazenge vamuvimbisa kuti vaizofona kana wavakuda kuenda kwakanga kuchirehwa naJonhson. Mufundisi vakazopinda mugedhe vaona mota isisaoneke.
Vakafamba vachienda kumota yavo iyo yavakambomira vakatarisa.
Iwe Toyota Noah mota yemawaya, manje manje ndichakupa mwana akutambise ndane mota chaiyo. Hupenyu hwangu hauchazorambi hwakadaro ndinokutendai mukoma Jonhson mukomborerwe nashe." Mufundisi vanodaro havo vakamira pamota yavo vachibva vatanga kusekerera wega. Vakazofamba zvavo vachipinda mumba apo vaingoona nechiso kuti pane mufaro vakawedzera.
Jonhson akaenda mberi nerwendo rwake apo akazoona asvika mumugwagwa mukuru unonanga Harare. Akanga atononokerwawo nezuva resvondo raaizogadzwa kuti apinde muhutungamiri hwekereke. Rwaiva rwendo rwurefu apa akazoona asvika paSakunda.
Akazotyaira kwechinhambwe achipinda muZimre park apo asina kutora nguva kusvika pamba pake. Nenguva isipi akanga atogara mumba make amirira rwendo rwake rwemanheru. Sezvineiwo nguva hadzina kunonoka kufamba apo akabva agadzirira zverwendo. Akazoona asvika pasi pemvura apo akaona vamwe vatosvika.
 

Akasvika nekugara pachigaro chake icho chakanga chakamumirira nechekare. Vakanga vatori pahurukuro pamusoro pemafambiro akanga achiita basa panyika. Jonhson akabva atopinzwa mudariro asati azoorara kana kufema.
"Tipe tinzwa chikomana, basa ririkufamba zvakanaka here kwavabva nako? Pane zvirikubuda here kana kuti masango matema." Akadaro Vicky apo Jonhson akambonyemwerera asati apindura.
"Ko anogoita matema sei nhai mambo wangu? Kutaura kuno ndatopihwa chigaro chehufundisi ndinotogadzwa nesvondo. Uyezve Mufundisi wekereke ndakavasimbisa kuti vagouya kuno vakabvuma. Handifambiri dhongi rakaora ini." Akadaro Jonhson achibva ambonyemwerera. Vanhu wese vakazoombera maoko vachifarira mashoko aJonhson. Husiku humwechete baba naamai Mufundisi vakanga vakarara muimba yemukati vachikurukura.
"Saka tipei tinzweka nhai Mufundisi, manga muchimbokurukura dzei nemukomana wechidiki uyu." Vanobvunza amai Mufundisi vachimirira kunzwa mhinduro kubva kumurume wavo.
 

CHAPTER 17
THE JOURNEY CONTINUES
Baba Mufundisi Mazondo vakanyatsokosorera kuti vataure nyaya yacho kune mudzimai wavo. Mudzimai wacho akaramba akanyarara achimirira mhinduro.
"Amai Mwana tambokurukura hedu dzehupenyu chikomana chiya chinoziva zvachinoita." Vakataura Mufundisi vachibva vanyarara. Mai Mufundisi vakambonyarara zvishoma vachibva vasimudzira.
"Saka munoreva kuti muchinda uyu anoziva zvaanoita nekuti ane mari yakawanda here. Zvimwe zvacho munatarisa kuti zvaanoziva zvaanoita ndezvaMwari here." Vakadaro amai Mufundisi vachibva vanyarara.
"Haisi nyaya iyoyo vadzimai, munhu kana akarongeka chingoyemurawo. Ini ndafarira hangu kurongeka kwake ndavakuda kuva saiye. SaMufundisi ndinenge ndichifanirwa kuonekerawo mukereke ndoita chiremera." Vakadaro Mufundisi vachipindura mudzimai wavo. Amai Mufundisi vakamboseka zvavo nhamo kuita kunge rugare. Mufundisi vakaramba vakanyarara mudzimai wavo achiseka.
 

"Saka munoti munowana chiremera nekuda kwemari here nhai baba wemwana. Ko shoko zvarinotaura wani kuti zvinondibatsirei kuwana pfuma yepanyika mweya uchitambura. Chiremera chenyu chiri mushoko raMwari kwete pamari." Vakadaro amai Mufundisi apo vaiyambira murume wavo.
"Ndizvo hazvo mudzimai wangu asi vanhu vakaonawo mutungamiri wavo achirarama hupenyu hune chiremera kereke inoenda mberi. Ndatovimbiswa kuenda kwaanowana mari uye anditi handimbopedza svondo ndinenge ndane mota hombe kwete kandinotyaira kemwana aka uye ndinenge ndane mari yakawanda." Vakadaro Mufundisi apo mudzimai wavo akambobata muromo achishamisika.
"Baba wemwana muchenjere kuita zvinhu zvinozobvisa pamberi paMwari muchitevedzera zvepfuma yepasi pano. Ndakakuonai musi uya muchiparidza makanga matobva pamberi paMwari nenyaya yekuchiva zvinhu zvenyika ino zvinopfukutwa munoziva kwazvakabva here." Vakadaro amai Mufundisi apo vakanga vasisanzwisise kuti kwaida kuendwa nemurume wavo vaizowana mari ichibvepi. VaMufundisi vakatomboseka mudzimai wavo vachiti akanga ari kumashure. Ivo vakanga vatopinda mudenga rechinomwe kare.
 

"Ndine imwe nyaya yandisina kukuudzai amai wemwana, pakuongorora kwandakaita muchinda uyu ndakaona zvakakodzera kuti ndishande naye. Zvakadaro ndiye achava mutevedzeri wangu aine chigaro chehufundisi zvekare. Nesvondo ndipo paari kugadzwa zviri pamutemo." Vakadaro Mufundisi zvakavhundutsa amai Mufundisi vakabata muromo.
"Ko nhai baba wemwana, chii chaicho chamakapihwa nemuchinda uyu chaita kuti mubva maita kunge mwana mudiki nekuda kwake. Ko zvamaiti munhu anopihwa chigaro mushure mekubata naye mwedzi mitatu zvakaendepi. Mukaita zvekutamba mavakutouraya kereke." Vakadaro amai Mufundisi apo vaitotaura namatsi.
"Ndizvo hazvo kuti munhu anofanirwa kuonekwa kwenguva refu, asika pane mumwe wekuti unotomuona achisvika kuti uyu anokodzera kutungamira kereke.
Ndosaka ndakafunga zvekupa mukoma Jonhson chigaro nekuti ndakaona vachikodzera." Vakadaro Mufundisa vachiedza kuzvinatsa divi ravo. Mai Mufundisi vakamboramba vakanyarara vachidzeya mashoko akanga ataurwa nemurume wavo. Vakaedza kubatanidza zvavakanga vachitaura vachibva vabatanidza neushumiri hwavo hwekare. Vakazongoti rega ndivaudze rekupedzisira vasati varara.
 

"Ipapo ndapanzwa hangu baba wemwana. Handichina mashoko mazhinji ekutaura asi kungoti Mwari ndiwo vanoziva. Ini mukauraya Kereke hamundioni ndichiuyako. Munoisimudza mega naJonhson wenyu iyeye. Asi kana zviri zvaMwari tichazviona hedu." Vakadaro amai Mufundisi vachizvidenesa divi ravo. Vakanga votoitirawo kuti kana zvaizoipa kudivi kwavo kunenge kwakanaka.
Vakazoonekana havo sevanhu vakanga wavakupinda munyika yezviroto. Ndiyo nyika yekuti unoona zvako wega usingazivi kuti mumwe vako arikuonei. Hazvina kuvatorera nguva vakanga wava kutodzipfodora. Ndipo pakatanga kurota amai Mufundisi apo hope dzacho dzaityisa.
Vakatanga kuona mukoma Jonhson vachipinda mukereke vakapfeka mucheka vaiita kunge dehwe rehwai. Vakaramba vakatarira vachiona mukoma Jonhson vachikusha shoko vari kumberi kwevana wesangano. Ndipo pavakazoona dehwe riya richishanduka kuita dehwe reshumba. Vakazongopuka vachiita zvekuvhunduka.
Kuvhunduka kwavo kwakavhundutsawo vaMufundisi vachibva vapepuka. Ndipo pavakabvunza chaitora nzvimbo apo vakabva vaudzwa hope dzakanga dzichangobva mukurotwa. Mufundisi vakazongopedza nyaya yacho nekutaura kuti ihope dzechando.
 

CHAPTER 18
KUGADZWA KWAJONHSON
Amai Mufundisi vakatoona kuti vaidzinganisana memhepo vachibva vanyarara zvavo. Husiku hwakanga hwakareba apo vakazomuka zvavo kuseni. Mufundisi vakagadzirira vachibva vaenda kubasa kwavo. Amai Mufundisi vakasarawo vari pamba sezvo vakanga vasina kubasa kwavanoenda.
Mazuva akaramba achifamba apo svondo yakasvika. Ndiro zuva guru rakanga rakamirirwa naMufundisi apo vaizonogadza chikomana Jonhson. Jonhson akanga akatorimirirawo zuva iroro nekuti ndipo paizotangirawo rwendo rwake nekereke.
VaMufundisi vakamuka vachigadzirira sezvavanosiita svondo yega yega. Amai Mufundisi vakamukawo vachomhanya mhanya nerimwe divi kuti vasazosara nenguva.
Hapana akanga achida kusara nenguva saka wese vaiit vachikasika. Nenguva isipi wese vakanga vachena zvekuti vapinde munzira. Vana wavo wese vakanga vapedza kugadzirira apo vakabva vatungamidzana vakananga kumota.
 

Mufundisi vakamutsa mota vachibva vatotanga rwendo. Rwendo rwacho rwakanga rwusina kunyanyokura sezvo kereke yaiva muMarondera makare. Mufundisi vakasvika nemhuri yavo vamwe vatosvika nechekare.
Sezvo pakanga pachine kanguva Mufundisi vakambotanga vaita kamusangano nevamwe vatungamiri apo vaisimbisa nyaya yekugadzwa kwaMukoma Jonhson. Vakambopikisana zvishoma nevamwe asi mhinduro yakazongosara iri yekuti Mukoma Jonhson vagadzwe.
Kereke yakazotanga apo pakatanga kupinda vasikana nevakomana wePraise and Worship. Vachipedza amai Mufundisi vakambopindawo mudariro vachikusha shoko rehumambo hwaMwari. Mufundisi vakazopindawo apo vakanga wava kupendera shoko rakanga raparidzwa.
Panguva yavakapinda mudariro vachikusha shoko Mukoma Jonhson vakabva vapindawo. Panguva iyi vakanga vaine imwe mota zvekare yakaita kuti Mufundisi vambokakama vari kumberi kwechaunga.
Rwendo rwuno Jonhson akanga auya nemota yerudzi rweFerrari iri itsvuku. Akapinda achibva ananga kumberi apo akaratidzwa pekugara naMufundisi. Mufundisi vakakusha shoko ravo apo vasina kuzotora nguva yakareba. Havana kuda kutora nguva vakabva vapinda muhurongwa hwavo hwemusi uyu.
 

"Ndichivhara shoko rangu ndinoda kukutendai mose mugokomborerwa nashe. Ndinovimba kuti sekunzwa kwamaita shoko muchanoita saizvozvo. Zvisinei ndine hurongwa hwandinahwo muzuva ranhasi hungakushamisai mese." Panguva iyi vanhu vakabva vateya nzeve apo vakanga voda kuziva zvaida kutaurwa. Mufundisi vakabva vashevedza Mukoma Jonhson kuti vauye kwavakanga vachikusha shoko vari.
"Mukoma vamunoona ndimire navo ava vane zodzo yedenga, ndakavaona kubva musi wekutanga ndikaona zvakakodzera kushanda navo muhutungamiri hwangu. Muzuva ranhasi ndinoda kugadza Mukoma ava kuva mutevedzeri wangu. Ndichavagadza kuva Mufundisi mugoteerera zvavanotaura." Panguva iyi pakaita maungira eruzha apo vamwe vaifata vamwe vachinyunyuta.
