Mufundisi vakazoshevedza vamwe vatungamiri apo Mukoma Jonhson vakabva vapfugama kumberi kwevanhu. Vakabva wavanamatira apo vanozodzokera kunogara pavakanga vari. Mufundisi Mazondo vakazopedzisira nekuudza vanhu kuti vagoteerera shoko rinoparidzwa naMufundisi mutsva. Hurongwa hwese hwaitevera hwakazoitwa apo vanhu vakazoparara vachienda kudzimba dzavo. Mufundisi vakapinda mumota mavo nemhuri yavo vachibva vaenda kumba.
 

Mazuva akafamba apo mumwe musi Mufundisi vakachaya runhare kuna Jonhson. Apa vakanga vagadzirira rwendo rwuya rwekwavakanga vachida kuzoendwa navo. Jonhson akabva avaudza kuti vaizoenda manheru saka ndiye aizouya achivatora. Mufundisi vakazovimbisa kuti vaizokasika kupedza basa kuti vasazosara nenguva.
Semunhu akanga anonokerwa Mufundisi vakaswera vakaringa nzira. Vaingoti vakanzwa bhero remota vaibva vatarira kugedhe kuti vaone kana Jonhson akanga auya. Nguva dzakafamba apo vana vakasvika pakunorara.
Mufundisi vakanga vatopera tariro vachifunga kuti havachaenda. Ndipo pavakanzwa kutinhira kwemota panze.
Nenguva isipi vakanga vatogara muLarmbogini mushure mekuonekana nemudzimai wavo. Mudzimai wavo akangoti tinoona madzoka akanga asingafari nerwendo urwu. Nenguva isipi rwendo rwakabva rwatanga.
Mota yaivhetemeswa zvekuti vaifunga kuti varikuenda kudenga kuna musiki. Mufundisi vaifunga kuti varikurota vari mumota yavakanga vasati vambokwira. Jonhson akazoraira Mufundisi kuti vatswinzwinye maziso.
Vakatswinzwinya kwechinguva apo vakazosvinura vachiona vari pakati pemachinda.
 

CHAPTER 19
MUFUNDISI PASI PEMVURA
Mufundisi vakambovhunduka sezvo vakanga vasina kutarisira kusvika nzvimbo yakaita seiyi. Hapana havo zvavaizokwanisa kuita semunhu akanga atopinda mazviri. Uyezve vakanga vatopedzwa simba saka vakanga vatopinda muchikwata.
"Kwazivai Mufundisi, ndimi zvenyu matiunzira shoko kuno kuti timborinzwawo. Ndinotenda nekutishanyara kwamaita muzuva ranhasi." Akadaro Vicky achibva anyemwerera. Vamwe wese vakakwazisawo Mufundisi avo vakabva wavakwazisawo. Vicky akazopinda munyaya yake yaaiva nayo kuna Mufundisi.
"Saka Mufundisi munoda kuti kereke ikure here kana kuti zvekuramba iri panzvimbo imwechete zvairi zvakakunakirai." Akadaro Vicky akatarisa Mufundisi mumaziso chaimo. Mufundisi vakambotorw nguva vachibva vazopindura.
"Ini chishuvo changu ndechekuti kereke yangu ikure zvekutozivikanwa Zimbabwe yese asi zvikwanisiro ndopasina." Vaadaro Mufundisi vachipindura.
 

"Zvakanaka Mufundisi, kuti kereke ikure hunge mutungamiri wacho aine chiremera. Hatingati Mufundisi anofamba nemota yemawaya wotarisira kuti kereke ikure. Mufundisi anofanirwa kuitawo mota yekuti kana mwana wesangano anotaurawo pane vamwe kuti ndiMufundisi wangu." Akadaro Vicky achibva ambonyarara.
"Ipapo ndirikupanzwa sisi wangu. Ndinenge ndine chishuvo chekuti kereke iende mberi asi nechimiro chandinacho ndinenge ndisina chiremera pamberi pavana wavanhu." Akadaro Mufundisi Vicky achibva amboseka mbijana.
"Mufundisi nhamo yemari yamunochema yapera nhasi, muchibva pano mavakuenda kunopfuma. Muchava nesimba rekuporesa uye muchaita zvishamiso zvichaita kuti vazhinji vakuteverei. Zvishamiso zvirikuitwa nevamwe mumakereke vachiunganidza vanhu muchazvigona nekuti simba racho ndichakupai nhasi." Akadaro Vicky apo akabva ambonyarara.
Mufundisi vakazotorwa apo Vicky akadzika pasi pasi kudarika pavakanga vari. Vakasvikoponda muneimwe imba yakanga yakashongedzwa zvakanaka kudarika dzimba dzepanyika. Akasvikogadzwa pachigaro chegoridhe. Panguva iyi vakabva vanzi vatswinzwinye apo Vicky akanga agadzirira kubata basa.
 

Vakatswinzwinya sezvavakanga vaudzwa apo vakanga vanzi vanodanirwa kuramba vakadaro kusvika Vicky apedza zvaaida kuita. Chaingonzwika chete imvura yaierera. Mufundisi vakaramba vakadaro kwakanguva apo vakanzwa Vicky avakutaura nemumwe mukadzi akanga apinda imomo.
Vakamboda kuteerera zvaitaurwa asi chirudzi chacho chaisanzwika. Vakaramba vakateerera Mufundisi vachiti zvimwe vanganzwawo shoko rimwe kana maviri asi hapana zvainzwika. Pava paya Mufundisi vakazonzwa wavakudirwa zvimwe zvinhu mumusoro zvavasina kuziva kuti zvii.
Mukadzi uya aitaura naVicky akazonyarara apo Mufundisi vakanzi vasvinure. Hapana mumwe wavakaona kunze kwaVicky chete. Vakamboshamisika vachiona munhu mumwechete asi vakanga vambonzwa vanhu vaviri.
Vakazongozviudza kuti gandisiyane nekumhanyisana nemhepo nditambe irikurira. Zvakanga zvakangooma kubvunza kuti ko mumwe wandambonzwa achitaura aripi iwe usina kumuona. Vicky akambotenderera Mufundisi kanoverengeka achibva azomira akavatarira. Muruoko rwake akanga akabata tsvimbo iyo yaakabva atambidza Mufundisi.
 

"Iyi inonzi tsvimbo yemoto Mufundisi, tsvimbo iyi muchaenda nayo muguta renyu ramunorarama muri uye ndiyo yamuchange muchishandisa pabasa renyu. Ndiyo tsvimbo ichashanda pakuita zvishamiso uye muchateererwa zvese zvamunotaura nekuda kwayo." Akadaro Vicky apo Mufundisi vaingotarisa tsvimbo iya kasingaperi. Tsvimbo iyi yaiva yegoridhe kubva kumusoro kusvika kuzasi apo vaingonzwa nehuremu hwayo. Chirongwa ichi chichipera Vakabva vabuda muimba iya vachidzokera kuya kwavakanga vachiitira musangano. Vakatoona vamwe vari pakati pehurukuro yemararamiro avakanga vachiita vari panyika.
Yakazomiswa nekusvika kwavo. Vicky akazoshama muromo kuti ataure.
"Ndinoda kutenda mose muri pano nekuuya nehuwandu hwenyu. Ndinoda kukuzivisai kuti Pastor Mazondo vachange vari muchikwata chedu asi anenge akawandira kuchitendero. Pastor Mazondo kubva nhasi matova Muporofita wemandiriri. Kana madzokera
panyika mubate basa uye pfuma yavakuzouya nebhande. Vana wesangano vachakufarirai uye mucharemekedzwa mativi ese enyika." Vicky achipedza mashoko aya akabva avhara musangano. Akanyangarika zvaaisiita mazuva ese mumwe nemumwe achiita saizvozvo.
Mufundisi naJonhson vakanganyangarikawo vachibva vazoona wava mumota.
 

CHAPTER 20
NEW MISSION IN CHURCH
Nzvimbo yavakanga vari havana kuiziva sezvo akanga ari manheru. Yaingozivikanwa naJonhson chete uyo aigara achiisvika. Mota yakamutswa rwendo rwuchibva rwatotanga. Yaitoda mapapiro chaiwo kuti ifambire mumhepo nekuti zvemunzira yakanga yatova ngozi.
Mumota makambotanga muine runyararo pasina aitaura nemumwe. Mufundisi vakanga vachiri pakufunga mari yavakanga vachazoita nezodzo yavakanga vapihwa.
Jonhson akanga achitorukawo mazano ekuti kereke isvike kure vagoraura vamwe wekuenda navo pasi pemvura. Vakambochovha chinhambwe vakadaro apo rwendo rwaiva rwurefu. Jonhson ndiye akazoshamisa muromo vake kuti ataure.
"Zvamunoona zvadai Mufundisi zvatofamba. Rwendo rwekuti mubudirire rwatotanga uye mari inenge isingazivane mumba menyu. Simba ramava naro parizvino richakuunzirai chikafu patafura uye muchatozotenga mota yamunoda. Kamota kenyu kaye kemawaya muchatozokapisa kana kupa vanotambura." Akadaro Jonhson apo aisimbisa Mufundisi.
 

"Ndavakutorota ndakagara pamusoro pemari ine mumvuri. Kana basa ndinosiya nekuti ndinenge ndakugara ndakatandawara ndichingodya mari yemarema. Dai ndaiziva kuti kune nzvimbo dzakaita sekwavandiunza uku ndingadai ndisina kutambura makore ese aya." Vakadaro Mufundisi vachitsinhira mashoko aJonhson.
"Ko kubasa munenge muchaenderei nhai Mufundisi. Tikangoenda kukereke svondo rimwechete munenge matova mumari. Kuzoti tikaenda mwedzi wese tinonotenga mota mbiri dzinenge yangu iyi. Marai muone zvenyu patinosvika musi wesvondo." Akadaro Jonhson achiwedzera kusimbisa Mufundisi.
"Ini ndinotoda kutenga mota yangu inenge yako yauri kutyaira iyi. Ndinoziva kuti ndinenge ndane chiremera kumba nekukereke. Kana vanondiona munzira vanondidedera." Vakadaro Mufundisi vachiwedzera kutsinhira mashoko aJonhson.
Nyaya dzakataurwa vachienderera mberi nerwendo apo vakanga vafamba mitunhu. Vati fambe fambe ndipo pavakazoona wavakupinda muMarondera. Ndipo pakatanga kuziva Mufundisi nzvimbo yavakanga wava nyangwe zvazvo kwakanga kuchakasviba. Mota yakatsikwa yakananga kuArthurstone kunova ndiko kwaigara Mufundisi.
 

Nenguva isipi vakanga vatosvika pamba apo Jonhson akaridza bhero. Hapana kutora nguva gedhe richibva ravhurwa. Mai Mufundisi vakabva vabuda kuti vatambire murume wavo. Vakakwazisa Jonhson pamwe nekubvunzana mufaro vachibva vazopinda mugedhe vakatungamidzana.
Jonhson akasimudza mota yake achibva atotanga rwendo rwekuenda kumba kwake. Mai Mufundisi vakazopindawo mumba nemurume wavo apo vakabva vamudziisira chikafu kuti adye. Mufundisi vachipedza kudya vakabva vatungamidzana nemudzimai wavo kunorara. Ndipo pavakabva vapinda muhurukuro.
"Saka ndekupi kwamakanga maenda kunoendwa usiku chete? Kwakanga kwakanaka here tipei tinzwe." Vakabvunza Amai Mufundisi vachida kunzwa kwakanga kwaenda Murume wavo.
"Mudzimai wangu dzimwe nzendo hadzidi kutaura ndakaneta zvandakaita izvi. Kana ndikatombozorora hangu zvinenge zvirinani nekuti kwandabva kure. Asi chikuru chandinoda kungotaura ndechekuti kereke yavakuzoenda mberi. Kana isu tava kuzobudirira nekuti minamato yataisa yadairwa." Vakadaro Mufundisi vachibva vatorara. Amai Mufundisi havana kuda kuzobvunza zvakawanda vakabva vararawo. Nenguva isipi vakanga wavakutorota.
 

Ndipo pavakatanga kuona Mufundisi vakapfugama pasi pemvura vakakomberedzwa nemachinda. Vanhu vakanga vari apa vakanga vachitamba nekuimba vachipemberera kuuya kwaMufundisi mumuzinda uyu. Vakabva vangopepuka vachiedza kubatanidza hope idzi asi vaishaya mhinduro. Vakamutsa Mufundisi vachibva wavaudza hope dzavakanga vachirota. Mufundisi vakambokwenya musoro apo vakaona hope idzi dzichinanga kwavakanga vabva. Vakazongopindurawo kuti zvimwe ndedzechando sezvo vakanga vapererwa.
Amai Mufundisi havana chimwe chavakazobvunza asi vakasara vaine mubvunzo. Amai Mufundisi havana kuzorara kwenguva refu sezvo kwakanga kwoedza.
Vakasiya vaMufundisi vakarara vachiita basa ravo remumba. Mufundisi vakazomukawo pava paya.
Mazuva akafamba apo zuva resvondo rakabva rasvika. Mufundisi vakamuka semazuva ese vachigadzirira nemhuri yavo. Chaiva chipata pata nhaka yemakonzo mimwe nemumwe achivavarira kuti asasare nenguva. Nenguva isipi Mufundisi nemhuri yavo vakanga vagara mumota kuto vachitangisa rwendo. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatosvika pavainamatira apo vakaona mota yaJonhoson yavapo. Vakashamisika vachiona dzimwe mota dzaivapo dzavakanga vasati vamboona.
Vakazotanga kufamba vachipinda mukereke.
 

CHAPTER 21
MUFUNDISI VANOBATA BASA
Vachipinda mukereke vanoona vanhu vari mavhu nemarara izvo zvakavashamisa. Vakatomboedza kumuka vachifunga kuti vari kurota asi vakatozoona kuti vakanga vakamuka nechekare. Zvavakanga vachiona zvaitova zvechokwadi.
Zvigaro zviya zvaimboshaya vanhu zvakanga zvazara apo vamwe vakanga vatozoita zvekumira. Nziyo dzePraise and worship dzakanga dzichitsva apo Mufundisi vakatanga kufamba vachienda kumberi kwaiva nezvigaro zvevatungamiri.
Jonhson akanga atogara kare apo pakanga pasara chigaro chaMufundisi chete. Vakasvikogara apo chikwata chePraise and worship chaiimba nziyo dzinodakadza zvekuti vanhu vaiita kunge vasvika kudenga.
Chikwata chevaimbi chichipedza vanhu vakatanga kuombera maoko Pastor Jonhson vachiuya pamberi pavana wesangano kuti vaparidze shoko. Vanhu vachipedza kuombera Pastor Jonhson vakabva vatanga kutaura.
 

"Ndinoda kukutendai mose nekuuya kwamaita nehuwandu hwenyu kuti tirumbidze musiki. Ndinodawo kukudza iye musiki atisanganisa panguva ino anovo ndiye atendera kuti vhangeri riparidzwe panguva ino. Ini hangu ndinongoti mukomborerwe nashe nerudo rwamaratidza nekuuya pano." Pakamboita maungira eruzha vanhu vachifarira shoko rekukomborerwa.
"Ndinofara ndimire pamberi penyu saMufundisi kekutanga muhupenyu. Ndiko kubata kwaMwari vanoita zvavanoda nenguva yavanoda. Ndinotenda nezodzo yandakapihwa inova ndiyo irikubata basa panguva dzino. Zvandapiwa zodzo iyi ndinoda kukupai makomborero nhasi, munhu wese chavakaronga muhupenyu hwako chichaitika mangwana chaiye." Pakaita Maungira ekufara sezvo Mufundisi Jonhson vakanga vataura mashoko anofadza.
"Nhasi ndoda kukutaurirai kuti ndakapihwa simba rekuti chese chandangonzwa kuda kuti chiitike chinobva chaitika. Vandinoropafadza anobva aropafadzwa uye vandinotuka zvirokwazvo achatukwa. Ndauya kuzokusunungurai mese makasungwa kuti mubude munyika yehutapwa uye vose vanotambura muchadya nemadzimambo." Vakadaro Mufundisi Jonhson vachibva vambotora chijira kuti vapukute dikita kumeso. Vanhu vakanga vasisagone nekufara.
 

Vamwe vakanga wavakutoona denga rakazaruka vatumwa vachikwidza nekudzika. Mufundisi Jonhson vakanga votoita kunge vachafambira mudenga apo vanhu vakanga vatoita zvekupfugama pamberi pavo kuti vabatwe musoro. Vanhu vakanga wavakutoona makomborero akanga ataurwa achinonoka.
Shoko rakaramba richienderera mberi apo vanhu vakanga vasisina kugarisika. Mufundisi Jonhson vakazogara pasi mushure mekupedza mharidzo yavo. Yakanga yava nguva yaMufundisi Mazondo kuti vachikushira vana shoko. Vanhu vakaita ruzha rwaivharidzira mukereke mavakanga vari.
Mufundisi vachimira pamberi pevanhu vakangoerekana vakanda maziso kumusuwo wekereke. Ndipo pavakaona kereke yaita kufashukira apo vamwe vakanga vatomira kunze. Mufundisi vakashamisika sezvo vakanga vasati vambounganodza vanhu vakadaro muhupenyu.
Vakatombotenderera vachinomira rumwe rutivi vachibva vadzoka zvekare vachidongorera apo vakangoona zvimwechetezvo. Nzvimbo yekunamatira ndiyo yakanga yatova diki saka Mufundisi vaifanirwa kuona zvekuita.
Vachiri mundangariro kudaro ndipo pavakazorangarira kuti vakanga vachiri kuparidza. Maziso evana wese wasangano akanga atarira kwavari sevanhu vakanga vamirira kupihwa shoko.
 

"Nhasi ndinofara ndichiona ungano yakakura seyandiri kuona muzuva ranhasi iri. Ndinotenda Musiki nekutiita varedzi wevanhu. Ndinongotenda nekuwandudzwa kwaitwa Kereke muzuva ranhasi zvandanga ndisina kutarisira. Ndinoda kukuvimbisai kuti Makomborero asvika pamasuwo enyu angomirira kutambirwa chete." Vakataura Mufundisi Mazondo vanhu vachibva vatanga kuombera maoko vamwe vachiridza miridzo.
Mufundisi havana kunyanya kutora nguva refu apo vakazoudza vatendi wavo zvinhu zvitsva zvavakanga wava kuzosangana nazvo mukereke.
"Ndinoda kukuzivisai kuti Mwari vakaburutsa nyasha dzakawedzerwa izvo zvaita kuti pave nezvimwe zvamakanga musati mamboona. Izvi zvauya nekuda kwezodzo yaPastor Jonhson. Pachange pane Prophecy time ndipo pachange pachibatsirwa vane matambudziko zvekare nemunhu waMwari." Vanhu vakamboita ruzha kwekanguva apo vamwe vaishora danho iri vamwe vachirumbidza.
Vakabva vatosimudza Pastor Jonhson kuti vagotanga basa sezvo vaifamba vari vaviri pabasa rechiporofita. Vanhu vakanga vateya nzeve kuti vanzwe mashoko echiporofita aida kutaurwa nevarume ava. Pastor Jonhson vakabva vatanga nekusimudza mumwe musikana wechidiki aiva mukati mechaunga.
 

CHAPTER 22
THE MISSION GOES ON
Pakasimuka musikana uya vanhu wese vakabva vaisa maziso avo ikoko. Vakanga vamirira kunzwa kuti Pastor Jonhson vaida kuzotaura kuti chii pamusoro pemwanasikana uyu. Pastor Jonhson vakatanga kutaura ndimi vachifamba kumberi kwevanhu vachibva vazodzoka kumwanasina uya.
"Ko nhai sisi anonzi Rufaro ndiani." Akabvunza Jonhson achibva amirira mhinduro. Musikana uya akabva apindurawo kuti ndiye aishevedzwa nezita rekuti Rufaro.
"Zvakanaka Rufaro, ndine zvandiri kuona pamweya. Ndirikuoneswa mukomana anonzi Elvis unomuziva here." Akadaro Jonhson apo musikana uya akapindura kuti Elvis aiva mukomana vake.
"Zvakanaka sisi Rufaro, ndoda kuti mufonere Elvis izvozvi munzwe kuti arikupi. Nhasi munodzokera kumba mava nechokwadi chizere. Elvis atori baba wemhuri." Panguva iyoyo Rufaro akabva atochaya runhare kuna Elvis. Pachokwadiwo Rufaro paakafona akatonzwa inzwi rechikadzi raitaura kuti ndiani iyeye baba wemwana.
 

Mwanasikana wevanhu akambodonhedza misodzi achibva azonyaradzwa apo akaudzwa kunzi pane zvikuru zvakanga zvakamumirira mberi. Pastor Jonhson vakabva vatosimudza mumwe muchinda wechidiki aiva nechepamberi muchaunga.
"Muchinda iwewe urikuda mari here? Taura nemoyo vako usatya." Vakadaro Pastor Jonhson vachibva vamirira mhinduro kubva kumuchinda uya. Muchinda uya akabva apindura kuti akanga achitotsvaga mari nemaziso matsvuku.
"Zvakanaka mwanakomana. Kubva zvino wavakuzoita mari ine mumvuri. Uchafamba nemota yaunoda uye uchagara imba yaunoda." Pakataura Pastor Jonhson mashoko aya pakamboita maungira ekupembera vanhu vachifarira kukomborerwa kwemumwe wavo. Vazhinji vakavimbiswa makomborero apo Pastor Mazondo vakabva vapindawo mudariro.
"Pane mukadzi wandiri kuona anotengesa pamusika ngaasimuke kana aripo. Zita rake rekuberekwa anonzi Anna." Pastor Mazondo pavakataura kudai pakabva pasimuka vamwe amai vakanga vakasimba zviri pakati nepakati. Pastor Mazondo vakambotenderera vachitauta ndimi senge dzaitaurwa naPastor Jonhson. Vakataura kwakanguva apo vakazodzoka kuna amai vaya.
 

"Amai ndirikuona muchifamba nemota mwedzi uno usati vapera. Ndirikuona makagara pamusoro pemari asi muchishaya kuti yabvepi. Ndizvo zvamuchasangana nazvo asi musatya inenge itori mari yenyu ishandisei." Panoridzwa mhururu nemiridzo zvekare apo vaMazondo vakanga wavakuvaratidza zvishandwa zvitsva zvakanga zvaburuka pavari. Amai vaya vakabva vagara pasi.
Mufundisi vakabva vasimudza mumwe mukomana wechidiki wavakashevedza nezita rekuti Frank.
"Mukoma Frank pane ndaona maita basa guru pano. Ndakakutarisai handisi kuona Frank asi ndirikuona muprofita mukuru ane zodzo. Ndinoda kukutambidza zodzo iyoyo unozouya kumba kwangu ndokubatsira."Muchinda uya akabva agara pasi apo vanhu vakamboomberera Mufundisi maoko.
Mufundisi vakafamba nadzo tsanangudzo zvekuti nyangwe chiri pasi pemvura vaichiprofita. Vachipedza kuprofita vakabva vavhara memunamato. Vaingonzwa munhu wese achiti I recieve Mufundisi vachiteura.
Mufundisi vakazogara pasi apo vakazosiira muchinda aipa hurongwa nguva yake. Musi uyu vaenzi nevakatendeuka vakanga vasingaverengeki. Pabva zvese izvi pakabva pauya nguva yezvipo. Vanhu vakabva vatanga kufamba mumwe nemumwe vachikanda mari mumabin mahombe aiva kumberi.
 

Mufundisi Mazondo vakanga vakatarira vakagara mberi vachiona vana vachikanda zvipo zvavo. Panguva iyi vakatombofunga kuti varikurota vachiona mabin maviri azara uye rechitatu rakanga rava pakati. Vamwe vakanga vari muhutungamiri vakaita kunge varikuona chipoko kuri kuvhunduka mari.
Kereke ichipera Mufundisi vakabva vashevedza hutungamiri hwavo kuti vagare musangano. Musangano uyu vaiti iwo Mufundisi Mazondo pamwe naMufundisi Jonhson, secretary wavo ainzi vaMavende, naMuvhangeri Sheshe. Pakauyawo Elder Mududu maElder Marwei pamwe naTreasurer ainzi Norest. Ndipo pavakatanga kuronga kuti poitwasei kuti Kereke ifambire mberi. Panguva iyi Treasurer vakanga vachiverenga mari yakanga yabviswa zvipo apo Secretary Mavende vaimhanya nekunyora nyora. Pastor Mazondo vakabva vapinda mudariro nenyaya yavo.
"Muchiona taungana kudai sehutungamiri ndinenyaya yandinayo yakakosha. Ndineshungu kwazvo nekuti kereke ikure uye ndinotenda kuti chishuwo changu chazadziswa. Zvachazadziswa zvavakureva kuti tavakufanirwa kuita mamwe mapazi kuti zvionekwe kuti takura. Toda kubatsirana kupafambisa ipapo kuti basa riende mberi." Pastor Mazondo vakataura mashoko aya vachibva vanyarara kuti vamwe vapindewo mudariro.
 

CHAPTER 23
EXPANSION OF THE CHURCH
Mufundisi Mazondo pavakataura mashoko aya pakamboita runyararo. Mumwe nemumwe akanga achifunga kuti nyaya yakanga yataurwa yotangira papi. Elder Mududu ndiwo vakazopinda mudariro vachipa pfungwa dzavo.
"Ndinofara chaizvo ndichinzwa pfungwa idzi kwamuri Mufundisi. Kana mwana akaberekwa vavakidzani vanokanda maziso avo ikoko vachiona kuti arikukura here. Isu kereke yedu yava nemakore ichingova panzvimbo imwe isina kumwe kwayamboenda.
Zvamataura kudai Mufundisi ndinoti kereke ngaiite mapazi akawanda." Vanombonyarara apo vanozoenderera mberi.
"Kuti zvibudirire tinofanirwa kuti nzvimbo yataenda tonoita crusade yemazuva kana svondo rose. Sezvo makazarurirwa naMwari muchibva mazopihwa mumwe muzodziwa ndinozvitenda nekuti munozobata mabasa makuru kwese kwamunoenda." Vakadaro Elder vachibva vanyarara zvavo. Rwendo rwakanga rwafamba Mufundisi kuenda pasi pemvura vaisarwuziva.
 

Vaingoti chiporofita chaMwari ndosaka vakataura vachiti sezvo makazarurirwa mukapiwha mumwe muzodziwa. Pavanhu vakanga vari mumusangano uyu hapana aiziva kwakanga kwanobuda Mufundisi kuti wawane simba rekuporofita. Jonhson ndiye ega aiziva zvakanga zviri pakati pavo.
"Ipapo Mafunga zvakanaka Elder, vanhu tikavaratidza zvishamiso vanotendeuka nekukasika. Panopera svondo rese pachibatwa basa zvinenge zvatoita. Ipapo patonaka asi tinofanirwa kuwana nzvimbo yekunamatiraka kuti zvitifambire." Vakataura Mufundisi Mazondo mushure mekufarira pfungwa yaElder Mududu.
"Ipapo hapanetse Mufundisi, ini ndine vandinoziva anoita zvekutengesa nzvimbo dzekuvaka kuBulawayo. Zvimwe tinogona kuwana nzvimbo yekuisa kereke yedu tobva tatotanga neikoko. Kana zvichibvira ndogona kutotaura naye izvozvi simbi ichapisa." Vakataura Muvhangeri Sheshe vachipawo pfungwa yavo.
Mufundisi Jonhson vanofadzwa nepfungwa iyi zvekuti vakabva vatoisimbisa kuna Mufundisi Mazondo kuti yakanga yakanaka. Vakabva vatoraira Muvhangeri Sheshe kuti vachaye runhare vanzwe kuti inowanikwa here nzvimbo yekereke. Nenguva isipi Muvhangeri vakanga vatoisa nhare yavo panzeve vachimirira kuti idivirwe kuBulawayo kwayakanga ichidana.
 

Nenguva isipi nhare yakabva yadavirwa navaKhumalo avo vaione nezvekutengeswa kwenzvimbo yekuvaka. VaKhumalo vaigara mumusha weMakokoba muBulawayo. Muvhangeri vakataura nyaya yavo vachibva vatoudzwa kuti nzvimbo yakanga yakazara yaitoda vanotenga. Vakazovimbisana kuti vaizosangana pakati pesvondo apo vaizokurukura nezvenzvimbo yacho yavaizoda.
Vachipedza kutaura pafoni vakabva vakanda maziso kuna Mufundisi Mazondo chiso chine mufaro. Vakaba vangovazivisa kuti nzvimbo yakanga iriko yaingoda mari chete. Ndiyo yakanga yavakuzoita nhanho yavo yekutanga kuti kereke ikure.
Mufundisi Jonhson vakazoronga kuti Muvhangeri Sheshe naElder Marwei vaizouya vachitora mota yekuendesa ikoko. Wese ava vakanga vaine mota dzavo asi vakanzi vaizoshandisa yaJonhson iyo yavaizonotora kumba kwake.
Kana vaizowana nzvimbo vaizotenga tende ravaizopota vachinoisa kusvika paizopera kuvakwa Kereke. Ndiro tende ravaizoshandisa pavaizoita crusade. Wese vakawirirana pfungwa iyi apo vakanga wava kuzotanga nerwendo rweBulawayo. Panguva yavakapedza hurukuro Norest akanga atopedza kuverenga mari.
 

Mufundisi Mazondo vakavhura ziso vachinzwa mari yakanga ichitaurwa apa. Mari yakanga yaverengwa ikasvika pa$300000 yekuAmerica. Muhupenyu hwavo vakanga vasati vamboona mari yakawanda kudaro.
Vamwe wese vakaita kunge vachatiza vachiona mari iyi yakanga isina zera navo.
Musangano vakazovharwa mumwe nemumwe achibva abuda akananga kumba kwake. Jonhson akasimudzawo mota yake akananga kumba kwake. Mufundisi Mazondo akasimudzawo yaka mota akananga kumba kwake.
Amai Mufundisi vakanga vasoenda kare nemota yemumwe wavaibata naye mukereke mavo. Nenguva isipi Mufundisi vakanga vatosvika kumba kwavo.
Vakaona mudzimai wavo akaisa muromo mumhuno vakazvishairwa pazvo. Ndipo pavakasarudza kubvunza kuti vazive chakanga chatizisa mufaro wemudzimai wavo.
"Ko nhai mudzimai wangu, kwaunobva vagumbuka kudaro kwakanaka here. Kana paine zvininetsa nditaurire zvimwe ndinogona kukubatsira nemazano." Vakataura Mufundisi vachida kunzwa chakanga chatsamwisa mudzimai wavo.
"Handina kugumbuka baba wemwana asi ndine zvirikundibata mumoyo mangu" Vakapindura amai Mufundisi.
 

CHAPTER 24
DISPUTE BETWEEN MAI NABABA
Mufundisi vakaona kuti apa pakanga pane nyaya vachibva vanyatsogara pasi. Apa vakanga wavakuda kunzwisisa kuti chii chakanga chanyanyobata mudzimai wavo.
"Chiiko chirikukudya moyo mudzimai wangu? Ndiudze zvimwe ndingakubatsira nekuti handidi kuona vakasuva." Vakataura Mufundisi Mazondo apo vakanga vamirira kunzwa nyaya.
"Nhasi ndoda kumbokubvunzai mubvunzo saMufundisi wangu kwete semurume wangu. Mubvunzo wangu uripakuti kereke yedu irikumbobva kupi ichienda kupi? Kana mukandipindura ipapo ndinezvimwe zvandinoda kutaura zvekare." Mufundisi vakaona kuti apa pakanga pane nyaya uye zvaitoda kuti vapindure zvakachenjera.
Apa vakanyatsoona kuti mudzimai wavo ane zvaakanga ari kunzwisisa maererano nemabatirwo akanga avakuitwa mukereke. Vakambokwenya musoro zvishoma vachifunga kuti votangira kupindura papi.
Pava paya vakazowana pekutangira.
 

"Amai wemwana regai ndikupundurei mubvunzo uyu kunyangwe zvazvo wanga uchida ndine nguva. Sekuziva kwamunoita takavamba kereke iyi tiri vaviri ikasvika pakukurawo nekuti Mwari vakanga vari pakati pedu.
Kereke yaikura asi yaingoramba ichitenderera panzvimbo imwechete." Amai Mufundisi vakanga vakateerera havo paitaurwa mashoko aya.
"Zvataitenderera panzvimbo imwe ndaivawo nechishuvo chekuti kereke isvike kure nyika ipone. Ndakasvika pakudzidza kuti mhinduro yaMwari inouya asi inogona kukasika kuuya kana kunonoka. Ndinotenda kuti takanga tiri tose takarindira kusvika Mwari vatumire muzodziwa wavo." Apa Amai Mufundisi vakambokosora mbijana vanenge vakanga vakachidzwa nemashoko aya. Mufundisi vakaramba vachienderera mberi.
"Kubva zvauya muzodziwa waMwari kereke yabva yatotanga kukura ichienda mberi uye vana waMwari vari kupona. Ndakanga ndisingazvifungiri kuti ndichaporofita asi nhasi ndozvavapo. Kutaura kuno Kereke yavakufambira mberi zvekuti panguva inotevera tinenge taenda nenyika." Vakataura Mufundisi apo vaida kuti mudzimai wavo anzwisise kwakanga kwakananga kereke. Mudzimai wavo akaramba akanyarara achifunga zvakadzama. Pava paya ndipo paakazovhura muromo kuti ataure.
 

"Zvakanaka Mufundisi wangu, kubva pakutanga taibata zvakanaka uye imi Mufundisi maisatendera chakaipa mukereke. Maiva mudzidzisi akanaka uye paibata ruoko rwenyu paisara paine ruponeso. Zvese izvi zvakanga zvakanaka nyangwe zvazvo taitenderera panzvimbo imwechete. Nhasi uno ndinobatikana ndichiona mabatiro amawa kuita." Vakataura amai Mufundisi izvo zvakambovhundutsa Mufundisi zvekushaya kuti vakanga vachizviwana kupi.
"Ko munorevei kana muchiti munobatikana nemabatiro atava kuita. Pane chakaipa here kana kereke ikanzi yavakukura kudarika zvayanga iri. Mwari ndipo pavanenge vazarurawo napo makomborero toraramawo hupenyu hwakanaka kuburikidza nezvipo zvevana wekutenda." Vakataura Mufundisi Mazondo vachida kuti mudzimai wavo anyatsonzwisisa.
"Hapana chakamboipa kana kereke ikanzi yakura. Ndinofara chaizvo ndikanzwa kuti kereke yaenda kana mhiri kwemakungwa asi ngazvive negwara rakanaka. Shoko pane parinotaura kuti zvaiva nani kutambudzika nevanhu vaMwari pane mufaro wenguva shoma tina Farao. Mufundisi nzira yamada kukudza nayo kereke haina kuchena." Mashoko amai Mufundisi aya akasiya Mufundisi vasina kana chekutaura. Vakanga vasina kutarisira kunzwa mashoko akadai panguva iyi.
 

Vakamboedza kuda kuvhara kuti vakanga vari pachokwadi asi vakanga vachitsva kumberi vakarumwa kumashure semudzanga wefodya. Vakaramba vachinetsana apo amai Mufundisi vakabva vaita sarudzo yavo.
Mufundisi vakapindwa nechando vachinzwa mudzimai wavo achiti akanga asisina chekuita nekereke iyi.
Mudzimai wavo akanga asarudza kumbogara pamba achimbofunga kereke yaaizoenda. Mufundisi vakamboedza kumira mira asi mudzimai wavo akanga asingadzori tsvimbo.
Mufundisi vakazongoti hapana hapo chakaipa asi mufaro vakanga vapera. Vakanga vasina kutarisira kuti mudzimai wavo achangoerekana ati haachada zvemukereke. Vaizoremekedzwa sei iwo vachiuya kukereke vasina mudzimai.
Mufundisi vakazobikirwa vachibva vadya zvavo. Musi uyu hapana akatandara nemumwe nguva dzekurara vakanosangana kuimba huru. Husiku hwacho kwakanga hwakareba asi zvaisatadzisa kunze kuti kuchene.
VaMufundisi vakapeputswa zvekare nemudzimai wavo uyo aida kuvaudza zvehope dzaimunetsa.
 

CHAPTER 25
KUDZIVA DZVENE NAFRANK
Vakanyatsoita zvekugara kuti vanzwe hope dzakanga dzichida kutaurwa nemudzimai wavo. Chiso chavakanga vachiona apa chakanga chasiyana nechamai Mufundisi wavaiziva kare.
"Baba wemwana hope dzandarota idzi hadzina kunaka zviri kwamuri kudzitambira kana kurega. Ini ndichadzitaura sekudzirota kwandadziita." Vakadaro amai Mufundisi vachitaurira murume wavo. Vakabva vaenderera mberi nehope dzavo.
"Ndaita kunge ndanga ndichiona zvinhu zvanga zvichiitika panyika. Ndiri pakuona kudaro vana wevanhu vanga vachitambudzwa pamusoro pekunamata kwavari kuita. Vana wevanhu vanga vachiuraiwa vachinzi vanamate zvavasingazive. Ndiripakati pakuona kudaro ndaona maoko enyu akazara ropa uye manga muchitungamira boka iri kuuraya vana wenyu vanokuteverai. Ndazoona mumwe murume anga akapfeka zvichena achidzika kubva kumakore kuti arwire vana vake." Panguva iyi vaMufundisi vakanga vakanyarara vachishaya zvekupindura.
 

"Murume uya asvika akandibata papfudzi achiratidza kuti anenyaya yaanga achida kutaura. Ndipo paandiudza kuti usavhunduka hako zvirikuitika izvi zvichapera.
Uchaona hako kana nguva yakwana asi uchatambudzikawo nekuda kweshoko iroro nekuti uchanzi unoonesesa." Ndidzo hope dzakanga dzarotwa naamai Mufundisi. VaMufundisi vakambotora nguva vakanyarara vachishaya kuti votangira papi kupindura. Vakazotanga kutaura pava paye.
"Amai wemwana manga makafuga machira here pamarota hope idzi kana kuti chando changa chichitokubvunzai mutupo? Kurota kwenyu kunogona kunge kuri kwenhema asi iri nzira yekuda kuparadza kereke yangu zvekare sezvo musisina chekuita nayo." Vakadaro vaMufundisi vachiedza kuchenesa kereke yavo. Hongu kereke yakanga yakachena asi iwo vakanga vasina.
Mai Mufundisi vakazongoti hapana chakaipa zvaizongobuda kana nguva yakwana. Mukadzi uyu aisafarira zvekuita nharo aimirira nguva yechiitiko munhu achizozvionera ega pamhuno sefodya. Vakabva vamuka havo amai Mazondo kuti vatange kuita basa repamba pavo. Murume wavo akasara akagara achiedza kubatanidza hope dziya. Pakarepo nhare yavo yakabva yarira. Pavakadaira vakabva vanzwa ari Frank.
 

Ndiye uya wavakanga vamboporofita vachimuudza kuti achava muporofita mukuru. Aida kuvaudza kuti aizouya kumba musi uyu sekutaura kwavakanga vaita kuti azouya kumba. Vakabva vamuraira kuti aizouya manheru apo vanenge vaine mukana.
Mufundisi vakazomuka vachibva vatanga kutenderera vachiona zvavo nzvimbo. Yaiva tsika yavo kuti vaimuka zuva nezuva vachitenderera nemota yavo vozodzoka zvavo. Vaizviita mazuva avanenge vasingaende kubasa. Vari pakutenderera kudaro ndipo pavakazofunga kuti vakanga vasisafanirwi kushanda. Pfungwa iyoyo ichingouya vakabva vatotyaira vachidzokera kumba.
Apa vakanga vafunga kunyora tsamba kuvakuru wekambani yavaishandira vachivaudza kuti vakanga wavakuzomira basa nekukasika. Vaizoenda kubasa svondo raitevera saka vaibva vaenda netsamba yacho. Vachisvika pamba vakanyora tsamba yavo vachibva vaudza mudzimai wavo zvavakanga varonga.
Mudzimai wavo akangotiwo chero zvamafunga sezvo akanga asina simba rekuzvidzivisa. Mufundisi vakazoswera vachiita gadziriro sezvo vakanga wava nerwendo rwurefu manheru emusi uyu. Vakagara vafonera Jonhson kuti kune muenzi akanga achizouya usiku. Muenzi uyu vakanga vatomugadzirira kuti vaende naye kwavakanga vachienda.
 

Nguva hadzina kumira apo vakazoona kunze kwasviba. Frank akabva afona achiti akanga ari munzira kuuya kumba kwaMufundisi. Jonhson aizouya nguva dzekubuda vobva vananga kwavaisienda. Mufundisi vakaraira Frank kuti aizofanirwa kuchaya nhare asvika pagedhe vakabva vamuudza mafambiro aaizoita.
Nenguva isipi Frank akanga atosvika. Akavhurirwa achibva atambirwa nemhuri yaMufundisi nemufaro. Amai Mufundisi vakanga vasina mufaro mumoyo asi vakangouratidza havo pachiso. Semuenzi akanga ashanya akapihwawo chikafu akadya. Pava paya ndipo paakabva atungamidzana naMufundisi vakananga kuimba yavaitandara nevaenzi.
Mufundisi havana kutambisa nguva vakabva vatora tsvimbo yavo iya yaishevedzwa kunzi tsvimbo yemoto. Vakangoinongedza pahuma paFrank vachitaura mashoko emumwe mutauro. Pava paya vakazoudza Frank kuti akanga asarirwa nekuenda kudziva dzene manheru iwayo obva atambidzwa chipo chake icho chakanga chatenderwa nevekumusoro.
Jonhson akazosvika dzavakuda kutoenda pakati pahwo husiku apo akang asina nguva yekumira. Mufundisi naFrank vakatungamidzana vakananga kumota yaJonhson rwendo rwuchibva rwatotanga.
 

CHAPTER 26
PLAN FOR BULAWAYO
Jonhson akavhetemesa Larmbogini yaakanga auya nayo vachibva pamba paMufundisi. Sezvo nguva dzakanga dzafamba vaisada kusara. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatopinda mumugwagwa mukuru apo dzimwe mota dzakanga dzichisara kunge dzakamira. Mufundisi Jonhson naMufundisi Mazondo ndivo vakanga vachikurukura Frank ari zii. Akanga achiri mutsva kwavari zvimwe ainyara kutaurawo nyaya.
Semazuva ese Vafundisi vakatswinzwinya vachibva varaira Frank kuti aite zvimwechetezvo. Vakazoona vasvika pasi pemvura apo vamwe vakanga vatosvika kare. Zvigaro zvavo zvakanga zviripo nechekare kunze kwechigaro chaFrank uyo akanga achiri muenzi. Akabva apfugama pakati pemachinda semunhu akanga asati agamuchirwa muhumambo uhwu.
"Kwazivai mukoma wangu, ndinofara kuona munesu munzvimbo ino zvichireva kuti panenge pane kuwirirana pakati pedu. Saka nyaya yedu nemurume uyu yakamira sei Jonhson." Akabvunza Vicky achida kuti atange basa rake pana Frank.
 

"Nyaya iripo ndeyekusimbisa murume iyeye pabasa rekuporofita. Tinoda kuti abate basa guru mukereke ndosaka tamudana kuno." Akadaro Jonhson achitaurira Vicky mukuru vake.
"Zvavauya kuno zvanaka muchinda, muno munonzi mudziva dzvene sekuudzwa kwavamboitwa. Pano ndinoda munhu ane hana yakasimba uye kana usina hana hauna rwendo. Ndinokutendera kuita sarudzo ndisati ndatanga basa asi sarudzo yako ndiyo inokupa hupenyu kana rufu. Toenderera mberi here." Akabvunza Vicky apo Frank akabva abvuma kuti vaenderere mberi.
Vakabva vasimuka paiva nevamwe apo Vicky akadzika naFrank pasi pasi pemvura. Vakaenda kuya kwavakamboenda naMufundisi Mazondo musi vavakasimbiswa. Akarairwa kuti atswinzwinye uye adzikame panguva inenge yavakubatwa basa. Nenguva isipi basa rakanga rapedzwa kubatwa paari achibva anzi akanga ava muporofita wamandiriri.
Vakazodzoka kwaiva nevamwe apo Frank akaona chigaro chake chavapo. Ndipo pakatanga kukurukurwa nyaya dzakasiyana siyana kuburikidza nemafambiro akanga achiita basa panyika. Jonhson akabva apinza yerwendo rwekuBulawayo uko vakanga vachida kunotenga nzvimbo yekuvaka imwe kereke. Vaizonoita crusade muvhiki raizotevera.
 

Vicky achipirwa nyaya iyo akabva asimbisa Jonhson naMazondo kuti vasadzore tsvimbo. Vaifanirwa kuzodzoka zvekare pasi pemvura kana mazuva aswedera kuti simba riwandudzwe. Hazel akazovimbisawo kuti aizouya kukereke asi aida kuzobata basa ari kupraise and worship. Vasikana vake vaaifamba nawo vakabvumiranawo nazvo.
Vakaronga zvizhinji zvaifanirwa kuzoitwa sezvo vakanga wavapedyo nekuda kuisa nyika mumaoko avo.
Musangano vakazopera apo mumwe nemumwe akazonyangarika kubva pasi pemvura. Frank akabudawo nanaJonhson vachibva vazoona vagara mumota.
Jonhson akaisimudza semazuva ese vachinanga kwavamanga vabva. Rwakanga rwuri rwendo rwurefu apo vakazoona vapinda muMarondera. Frank akazosiiwa pamba paMufundisi Mazondo Jonhson achibva asimudzira kuenda kumba kwake.
Mai Mufundisi vakangotarira havo semunhu akanga asina zvekuita. Kunze kwakazochena Jonhson achibva aenda kumba kwake muMarondera makare. Zuva iri ndiro raifanirwa kuendwa KuBulawayo kunotengwa nzvimbo yekereke. Muvhangeri Sheshe naElder Marwei vakangomuka vakananga kumba kwaJonhson kuZimre park sezvo vaida kuita zvinhu zvavo nenguva.
 

Nenguva isipi vakanga vatosvika kuZimre apo vakanga vachishandisa mota yaElder Marwei.
Vakasvikotambirwa nemufaro naJonhson apo vasina kuzogara pamba apa. Varume vaviri ava vakashamisika vachiratidzwa ferrari tsvuku yakanga yakatarisa kugedhe nechekare. Ndiyo mota yavakanga vachizoenda nayo.
Muvhangeri Sheshe vakazogara kudivi ramutyairi apo vakabva vamutsa mota kuti vatange rwendo. Dzaitoita kunge hope nekuti wese ava vakanga vasati vambopinda mumota yerudzi urwu. Yakasimudzwa mota ichinopinda mumugwagwa mukuru unobatanidza Harare neMutare.
Vazhinji vairidza mabhero vachiona ferrari ichivasiya kunge vakamira. Vachisvika pamapurisa epaMabvuku vakangozarurirwa kunzi vapinde havana kumiswa. Mota yacho yakanga isiri yekujairira zvaingorema kuimisa.
Vachisvika mudhorobha havana kumbomira vakabva vapinda nemugwagwa mukuru weSamora Machel.
Yakavhetemeswa mota apo vakafamba mitunhu mota ichiita kunge iri kubhururuka. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatopinda muBulawayo. Vakabva vafonera vaKhumalo vachivaudza kuti vakanga vapinda munzvimbo.
VaKhumalo vakatoshamiswa nekuti vakanga vasina kuvatarisira nguva idzi. Vakabva vabudawo kuti vanosangana nemachinda.
 

CHAPTER 27
BULAWAYO PREPARATIONS
VaKhumalo vakanosangana nevarume vakanga vabva Harare paRailway museum tiri muMakokoba makare mavaigara. Havana kutora nguva vakabva vaenda kunoratidzwa nzvimbo yacho kuti vagutsikane vasazodemba kuti yakanga isina kunaka.
Vakafarira nzvimbo yacho vachibva vaenda navaKhumalo kuhofisi kwavo. Vakabhadhara mari yese yaidiwa sezvo vakanga vapihwa mari. Vachipedza kubhadhara mari vakaonekana apo vakagara vakoka vaKhumalo sezvo vaizouya vachiita crusade.
Mota yakasimudzwa yatarisa Harare apo yakanga yazobatwa naElder Marwei. Rwaiva rwendo rwurefu asi nekuda kwemota yavakanga vanayo rwakaita rwupfupi. Varume vakatozoshamisika vachiona vatotarira guta reHarare. Ndipo pavakaona kuti mota yavo yakanga ichimhanya kunge irikuenda kudenga kuna musiki.
Vachipinda mudhorobha kwakanga kwavakuda kusviba saka vakabva vatyaira vakananga kuZimre park nenguva isipi vakanga vasvika pamba paJonhson vachimuratidza matsamba enzvimbo yavakanga vatenga.
 

Chakava chiitiko chinofadza kuva nenzvimbo yakanga yakakura kudaro. Muvhangeri naElder vakazooneka vachibva vanopinda mumota mavo. Rwendo rwakanga rwusina kunyanyokura apo vakazoona vapinda muMarondera. Vakatanga vapfuura nekwaMufundisi vachivaudza nyaya yakanga yava mudariro.
Mufundisi vakapembera vachiona matsamba enzvimbo yakanga yatengwa yatogadzirira kuvakwa. Izvi zvakabva zvaita kuti vade kukasika kunoita crusade ikoko mbiri yavo yobva yaenda kure. Chakashamisa Muvhangeri naElder ndechekuti Mai Mufundisi havana kumbopemberawo pavakanga vachipembera apa.
Vakangozviudzawo kuti ndezvemumba mevanhu hapana anoziva zviripakati pevaviri.
Muvhangeri naElder vakazobuda vachibva vaenda kudzimba dzavo. Mufundisi Mazondo vakasara vachingopembera nemba yese vachifara kuita kunge chana chidiki chapihwa zviwitsi.
Vakazorara nguva dzaenda apo amai Mufundisi vakanga vasorara kare. Mai Mufundisi vakarota zvekare hope dzakanga dzisina kumira mushe. Hope idzi dzakanga dzine chekuita nerwendo rwakanga rwuchazofambwa nevanhu kuenda Bulawayo. Vakaeredza misodzi kuhope ikoko vachiona zvakanga zviri pameso avo.
 

Vakanga vakamira pamusoro pegomo refu vakatarira kuguta reBulawayo. Vakatarira kudaro vaiona mota dzichikwidza nekudzika dzakananga ikoko dzimwe dzichidzoka. Ndipo pavakaona vana wemukereke vakananga Bulawayo. Vakaramba vakatarira vachiona rwendo rwunoyemurika vanhu vachifara.
Vakaramba vakatarira vachibva vaona vanhu vachifara varimo muguta vachirumbidza Mwari. Mai Mufundisi vaisafara vakatarira vachiona nzira yaishandiswa nevatungamiri kurumbidza musiki. Pakudzoka kwakanga kwavakuita vanhu ndipo pavakaona rima munzira. Vakatanga kunzwa ruzha rwekubonderana kwemota pamwe nekuchema kwevanhu. Ndipo pavakaona ropa richierera mumugwagwa.
Vakazongonzwa inzwi raitaura kuti mukereke mapinda chipfukuto iwe uripo.
Vakavhunduka nemashoko aya vachibva vapepuka. Vakabva vaita zvekugara pamubhedha wavo vachifungisisa pamusoro pemashoko akanga achangobva kupinda munzeve dzavo.
Saka vaizozviitasei zvavakanga vachiudzwa kunzi mukereke mapinda chipfukuto iwo varipo? Simba rekurwira vana waMwari vaizoriwanepi iwo mberi kwavo kwakanga kwava nevanhu vane moyo yakaoma vanoda kusveta ropa revasina mhaka.
 

Vakataurira murume wavo hope dziya asi kwaingova kudzingana nemhepo. Vakabva vatonyararidzwa nerekuti unoda kuputsa kereke yangu haufari kuona ichienda mberi. Amai Mufundisi vakazongopedzisa nemashoko ekuti kana zviri zvaMwari zvichaenda mberi asi kana zvisiri zvichaparara nezita raJesu.
Mufundisi vakangozviudzawo kuti vaizotamba inorira. Vakaswera zvavo vari pamba pavo apo vaizodzokera kumvura husiku uhwu. Ndipo pavaizonoronga zverwendo rweBulawayo uye nezvese zvaidiwa.
Usiku hwakasvika vachibva vaita zvavaisiita naJonhson. Vakaona vamwe vatovapo musangano uchibva vatotanga. Ndipo pakabva papinda Vicky mudariro achiti akanga achida ropa pamusangano iwoyo. Izvi zvakanga zvisina kuoma sezvo vaikwanisa kuzvigadzirisa.
Brighton akavimbisawo kuti aizounza mabhazi ekufambisa ayo akanga ava kuzouya nendege kuti akasike kusvika. Mufundisi Jonhson naMazondo vakabvumirana nazvo apo vakanzi vatarisire mazuva maviri aitevera. Aizouya nevatyairi kubva kuSouth Africa kwaaiburukira. Musangano vakaitwa apo Jonhson naMazondo vakazodzwa kunzi vagobata basa guru vasvikako. Vachipedza musangano vakabva vanyangarika vachibuda mumvura semazuva ese.
 

CHAPTER 28 PREPARATIONS CONTINUE.
Mazondo naJonhson vakazoona wava mumota vachibva vatotangisa rwendo. Ndipo pavaikurukura mafambisirwo aizoitwa musangano vakanga uri mberi kwavo.
"Saka tichafambisa hurongwa uhwu sei nhai Mufundisi Mazondo? Hurongwa hwakaita seuhwu haudi kunonokerwa." Akabvunza Jonhson akatarisira kunzwa mhinduro.
"Apa hapachada zvekuti tinoramba tichitenderera, simbi inoda kurohwa ichapisa togara taenda nenyika. Svondo rinotevera iro rinofanirwa kushandwa tichiita gadziriro yerwendo. Rwendo irworwo rwunenge rwusingadanwi anonzwa." Vakapindura Mufundisi Mazondo vachiedza kusimbisa rwendo.
"Ipapo Mufundisi ndinokutsigirai. Sekuziva kwandinoita gadziriro yacho inenge ichisanganisira kuzivisa vagari wenzvimbo yacho nezveukuru hwenyu zvinoita kuti vazouya nehuwandu hwavo." Akadaro Jonhson achiwedzera pane zvakanga zvataurwa naMufundisi.
 

"Izvo ndizvo chaizvo kuti vanhu vanofanirwa kutanga vaziva vasati vaona. Hazvizoite kuti tingoerekana tapinda munzvimbo tisina kana anotiziva. Zvinoreva kuti tinofanirwa kutumira vanhu vachanogara svondo rese vachishambadza kereke yedu nemabatiro ayo." Mufundisi Mazondo vakataura apo Jonhson akabva agutsurira musoro.
"Izvozvo ndinobvumirana nazvo Mufundisi. Svondo yatirikupinda iyi tinofanirwa kutsvaga mutori wemavhidhiyo anenge achitora zvese zvichaitika. Pane vachauya kuzopupura uye vamwe vatichaporofita zvose izvi zvinofanirwa kutorwa vhidhiyo togadzira marekodzi." Mufundisi Mazondo vakanyemwerera vachinzwa Jonhson achitaura mashoko aya.
Vakabva vatoronga matambiro avaizoita nyaya yacho. Vhidhiyo yaifanirwa kuzotorwa uye yaifanirwa kuzogadzirwa nanamazvikokota nekukasika. Vaifanirwa kuzotsvaga projector zvakare kuitira pavaizosvika panzvimbo dzinoungana vanhu vaikwanisa kungoisa vhidhiyo vanhu vachiona.
Zvese izvi zvaisada nguva sezvo Jonhson aiva nevanhu vaaiziva vaiita mabhizimisi aya. Akabva afonera Boss Madzo achimuudza nhau yake yaakanga anayo. Boss Madzo vakabvuma kuti vaizouya vachiita basa ravo.
 

Chikamu chekutanga chakanga chapfuura kwakanga kwasara projector. Jonhson akabva afonera mumwe waaiziva aishevedzwa nezita rekuti Boss Muchinda. Ndiye aiita zvemaprojector saka vaizotenga kwaari. Akabva atodaira achivaudza kuti yaivapo.
Akatomboshamiswa kuona foni yaipinda nguva idzodzo apo Jonhson akazomuudza kuti akanga ari kumashure kwenguva.
Chikamu ichi chakanga chapfuura yakanga yava nguva yekuronga kushambadzwa kwaizoitwa basa raMufundisi.
Mundisi Mazondo vakazovimbisa kuti vaizotaura naElder Mududu kuti vatsvage chikwata chavaizoenda nacho kuBulawayo nechipiri.
Vaizotenderera neguta reBulawayo vachisimbisa kuti vanhu vazouya nehuwandu hwavo. Rwendo rwakachovhwa vachikurukura apo vakazovhunduka vachiona vapanda muMarondera. Jonhson akazosiya Mufundisi Mazondo pamba pavo achibva asimudzira akananga kumba kwake.
Mufundisi vakangorara zvishoma vachibva vamuka vachimbotenderera nechivanze chavo. Ndipo pavakazofunga kuti vane munhu wavakanga vachida kuzotaura naye. Vakaburitsa foni yavo vachibva vatanga kutarisa manhamba aivamo. Vakazoona vasvika panhamba yaElder Mududu.
 

Vakachaya panhamba iyoyo iyo isina kutora nguva kudairwa. Vakakurukura Mufundisi vachibva vapira nyaya yavo. Elder Mududu vakabvumira padenga apo vakati nyaya yekutsvaga vanhu yaisava hombe. Zvinhu zvaingoda zuva rimwechete rinova zuva resvondo.
Vachipedza kutaura Mufundisi vakabva vadzokera havo mumba mavo. Mazuva akafamba apo vakazoona vasvika zuva resvondo. Mabhazi akanga azotumirwa naJonhson ayo aizotakura vanhu kuenda kuBulawayo. Ndiwo musi waaizopembererwa sezvo akanga achiri matsva.
Mufundisi vakamuka vachibva vagadzirira kuenda kisvondo. Mai Mufundisi pamwe nevana wavo vaviri vakabva vati vakanga vasiri kuzoenda kukereke ikoko. Mufundisi vakada kumboshandisa chisimba asi vakakundikana.
Vakabuda vachibva vatyaira mota yavo yakananga kukereke. Nenguva isipi vakanga vasvika vachibva vatoona mota dzakazara kuita kunge dzekuramwirwa. Vakapinda mukati vachiona kumberi kumire vasikana wePraise and worship vachiimba zvinonwisa mvura. Vanhu vakatombofunga kuti vasvika pagedhe rekudenga wanzwa kuimba uku. Mufundisi vakasvikogara pachigaro chavo chemazuva ese.
 

CHAPTER 29 WARANGARIRWA BULAWAYO
Vana wevanhu vakaimba zvinonwisa mvura zvekuti vazhinji vakanga vachinamata nhema vakatendeuka. Boss Madzo vakanga vatosvika kare vakanga vatotanga basa ravo rekutora mavhidhiyo. Vaimbi wepraise and worship vachipedza kwakabva kwapihwa mukana kuna Mufundisi kuti vakushe shoko. Mufundisi Mazondo vakabva vasimuka kuti vatange kuparidza.
"Nhasi ndinokutendai vana vaMwari nekuuya kwamaita nehuwandu hwenyu. Ukaona vanhu vachiwanda pakereke zvinoreva kuti parikubatwa basa rakanaka.
Ndinoramba ndichikutendai zvekare mose munotsigira basa randakatumwa iri kuti riende mberi." Apa vanhu vakanga vakanyarara vachida kunzwa mashoko anotevera.
"Nhasi handina mashoko akawanda asi ndoda kungokusimbisai kuti musimbe pakunyengetera munokunda. Kana uchida chakanaka itawo chakanaka uone kuti hauchiwane here. Kana uchida kutenga mota ipa Mufundisi chegumi unoitenga mangwana chaiye." Apa pakamboita maungira eruzha vanhu vachifara.
 

"Mungaseka zvenyu asi zviedzei muone kuti hamukomborerwe here. Mukoma Jonhson vakazviedza vakakomborerwa nechipo chebasa raMwari ikozvino wava kuporofita uye wava Mufundisi. Ndizvo zvinoita zodzo yaMwari izvozvo. Ukapa uchapihwa nekukasika zvichienderana nekuti vapa zvakawanda sei." Pakaita maungira zvekare vamwe vachipotsera mari kumberi kwakanga kumire Mufundisi.
"Nhasi ndinoda kungoti warangarirwa guta reBulawayo, warangarirwa nemunhu waMwari. Rakakomborerwa guta rinotsikwa netsoka yemunhu waMwari nekuti richakomborerwa. Bulawayo zvauri guta ramadzimambo mauri muchatsika muzodziwa akazodzwa kukunda madzimambo ako uye uchasara nemakomborero.
Munhu waMwari arikuuyako nekukasika." Vanhu vakaridza mhururu nemiridzo vachinzwa mashoko akanga ataurwa naMufundisi Mazondo.
"Vana vaMwari ndinoda kuti tibude nehuwandu hwedu tiende kunobata basa muguta reBulawayo. Kune Makomborero akakumirirai ikoko ngatisunungukei tiende. Ndaona mucherechedzo wevana waMwari vachifamba munzira yegoridhe yanga ichipenya kwazvo. Ndaona vana vachinhonga goridhe zvekare munzira imomo." Vakataura Mufundisi vanhu vachibva vaita ruzha zvekare.
 

Vanhu wese vakasarudza kuenda kunozvionera ikoko. Mufundisi vakazogara pasi apo pakazosimuka Elder Mududu. Vaida chikwata chekuzoenda nacho kuBulawayo kuti vafanoparidzira shoko vasati vanobata basa. Apa vanhu vaiita kurwirana kuenda hapana aida kusara.
Vakazongosarudza gumi nevaviri chete avo vaizobuda nechipiri. Vakasimbisawo vanhu kuti vasununguke vabude nehuwandu hwavo kuenda kunorumbidza musiki. Vakavimbisa makomborero kuvanhu ayo aizobva kumuzodziwa waMwari.
Elder Mududu vachingogara pasi pakabva papihwa mukana kuvazodziwa waMwari vakanga vakanga vachida kuporofita. Mukati mevanhu makabva masimuka muchinda uya anonzi Frank kuti ataure. Vazhiji vakashamisika asi vamwe ndiwo vakazorangarira kuti zvakanga zvamborehwa musvondo rakapfuura.
"Nhasi ndinopa mbiri kuna Musiki naMufundisi zvese. Ndinofara nezvandiri muzuva ranhasi nekuti hazvina kuuya neni asi naMufundisi. Ndiwo vakandigamuchidza ropafadzo nazvino ndinooneswa zvakavanzika zveukuru hwaMwari. Itai zvakanaka muonewo." Akataura Frank achibuda muchaunga achienda kumberi kwevanhu.
Nenguva isipi akanga atomira kumberi kwevanhu avakubata basa.
 

"Ndirikuona vanhu vari parwendo rwatakatarisana narwo takananga Bulawayo. Rwendo urwu ndaona rwasiya makomborero muguta reBulawayo ndikaona vazhinji vachisunungurwa. Ndaona zvirema zvichifamba ndikaona vazhinji kwazvo varwere vachiporeswa.
Zvechokwadi Bulawayo warangarirwa." Vanhu vakamboita ruzha zvekare vachirumbidza Frank. Frank akaenderera mberi achisimudza vanhu achivaudza nyaya dzavo dzaakanga achioneswa. Muchinda uyu akanga atosimbiswa zvekuti kana tsono yakafushirwa muvhu aiinhonga. Vanhu vaingoridza mhururu vachinzwa Frank achifamba neshoko. Mufundisi Mazondo naJonhson vakanga vasina zvekutaura musi uyu saka Frank achigara pasi vakabva vapa mukana kune vakanga vachida kuoupura.
Apa ndipo pakanga pasingadanwi anonzwa manje. Wese vakanga vaporofitwa svondo rapfuura vakanga vachipupura kusunungurwa. Vakawanda vakanga vachitenda basa guru raMufundisi. Humwe hurongwa hwese hwakazoitwa kusanganisira hurongwa hwezvipo. Apa ndipo pakanga pava kuzoratidzanwa zvishandwa nekuti hapana akanga achida kusara. Hapana zvekare aida kukundwa kubvisa mari yakawanda nemumwe.
Mufundisi vaingosekerera havo vachiona mari isingazivani pamberi pavo. Kereke yakazopera vanhu vachibva vaenda kudzimba dzavo.
 

CHAPTER 30
TRIP TO BULAWAYO
Mufundisi vakasara nehutungamiri hwavo zvavaisiita svondo yega yega. Ndipo pavakaverenga mari vakaona yakapeta yesvondo rakapfuura katatu. Mufundisi vakazorongawo kuti vaizotengawo mota ine chiremera kuitira kwavakanga wavakuda kuenda.
Vakabva wavimbisawo kutengera vamwe vakanga vari muhutungamiru uhwu mota dzerudzi rwemaToyota Legend. Basa rese iri rakabva rapihwa Norest uyo aiona nezvemari. Mufundisi vaizonotsvaga yavo yavainzwa kuda nemoyo wavo. Jonhson akavaudzawo kuti zvake zvakanga zvakaringana.
Vachipedza musangano mumwe nemumwe akabva ananga kumba kwake. Mufundisi vakatyairawo vakananga kumba kwavo. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatosvika pamba pavo.
Vakasvika mudzimai wavo achishaura nziyo dzokurumbidza pamwechete nevana wavo vaviri. Mufundisi vakaramba vakamira vakatarira vachinzwa pachiimbwa kambo kekuti shara yako kune nzira mbiri.
 

Kambo aka kaivanzoita kuti Mufundisi vapinde panaMwari mazuva avo chaiwo vachamushumira pachokwadi. Vakazongopfuurira vachinosiya kabag kavo kavakanga vakataura vachibva vadzoka. Mai Mufundisi ndiwo vakabva vatanga kubvunza kuti kwakanga kwaswera sei kukereke.
"Ungagobvunza zvekukereke wadii kuuya kuzozvionera?" Kupindura kwaMufundisi kwakauya sechibhakera munzeve dzemudzimai wavo asi akazorangarira kuti aigona kuchivhika.
"Kuuya kukereke ndinoda chose baba wemwana asi zvunoda ndichinamata Mwari wechokwadi kwete kunamatiswa zvifananidzo." Mufundisi vakaita hasha vachinzwa mashoko aya zvekuda kuregedzera mudzimai wavo mbama. Vakazokasika kuzvidzora varangarira kuti vaizoshatisa zita rekereke guhwa rafamba.
Chemusi uyu vakazongorara havo asi pfungwa dzaiva kumota yavakanga vachazotenga. Kuseni havana kuda kumirira chikafu vakabva vabuda vakananga kuSam levy kuBorrowdale.
Vakasimudza mota yavo vachienda ikoko sezvo kuri iko kwakanga kuine mota yavaida. Nenguva isipi vakanga vasvika pagaraji raitengeswa mota.
 

Garaji iri raitengeswa mota dzerudzi rwemercedes benz chete. Mufundisi vainyemwerera havo vachitenderera apo vakanga vasati vaona mota yavaida. Vakazosvika pane imwe benz yerudzi rwe4matic gle 400d vachibva vamira ipapo. Ndiyo mota yakanga yatora moyo wavo.
Semunhu akanga asina nguva yekutambisa vakabva vaburitsa 165000 yaidiwa pamota iyoyo. Vakazopihwa mutyairi uyo aivabatsira kunosvitsa mota yavo kumba. Vakabuda vakatungamidzana apo vakambochovha rwendo rwurefu.
Mutyairi uya akasvitsa mota yaMufundisi kumba achibva adzokera kubasa kwake. Mufundisi pavaitarisira kuti mhuri yavo ichapemberera mota itsva vakaona zvisirizvo. Mudzimai wavo akabva avaudza kuti aisazopemberera mota yaasingazive kuti yauya nenzira ipi. Mufundisi vakazongozviudza kuti vaizoona zvekuita nemudzimai uyu.
Chipiri chakazosvika zvinhu zvese zvava panzvimbo. Projector yakanga yavapo uye boss Madzo vakanga vapedza kugadzira vhidhiyo yekuchechi. Elder Mududu vakangotorana nechikwata chavo vachibva vapihwa bhazi nemutyairi. Rwendo rwakatangwa vachibuda muMarondera vakananga Harare. Mubhazi akanga ari mafaro chete kusingadanwi anonzwa.
 

Nenguva isipi vakanga vapinda Harare vachibva vatora mugwagwa unonanga Bulawayo. Rwendo urwu rwakanga rwakareba asi mutyairi wacho aitoita kunge akambotyaira ndege. Airivhetemesa bhazi zvekuti Bulawayo paimuitira pedyo. Zuva rakazosvika pakurova nhongonya wavakupinda muGweru.
Ndimo mavakambotenderera vachishevedzera kuti vanhu vagouya kuBulawayo nehuwandu hwavo.
Vaingonzwa miridzo chete vanhu vachipemberera. Bhazi rakazosimudzwa rakananga Bulawayo kwavaizonobata basa guru.
Nenguva isipi vakanga vasvika paBulawayo centre vachibva vagadzira projector kuti ione mavhidhiyo. Pasina nguva vakanga wavakutoridza vhidhiyo iya yemusi wesvondo yaitorwa naBoss Madzo. Vanhu ndipo pavaidanwa vakadairaka apo vasina kutora nguva kuungana.
Vakomana nevasikana vakanga vari pabasa iri vakabva vatanga kupa vanhu maflier kuti vagozvionera wega nekuzvisarudzira. Vanhu wese vaipfuura neapa vaibva vachisekerera kuita kunge vatotambira makomborero. Sezvo nguva dzakanga dzisingamiri kufamba bhazi rakazosimuka richibva apa. Rakazomira rasvika paTshulu Tsha Nabe lodges panova ndipo pavaizorara.
 

CHAPTER 31
CHOTSVA PABULAWAYO
Mumwe nemumwe akapihwa kamuri rake raiva nezvese zvinotarisirwa kunzi zvinodiwa nemunhu. Husiku hwakatoita hupfupi apo vakazomuka vachipihwa kudya kwemakuseni. Vachipedza kudya kwemakuseni Elder Mududu vakabva vatanga kutotenderera neguta reBulawayo vachishevedzera kuti vanhu vagouya nehuwandu hwavo.
Pakanga pasingadanwi anonzwa apo vanhu vakanga vatononokerwa necrusade yacho. Vamwe vaitoita kunge vakanga vatotambidzwa makomborero muzodziwa asati auya. Svondo rese ravakagara ikoko rakavasiya vaine chivimbo chekuti vaizosiya nhoroondo muguta umu.
Vakasarudza kusimuka iri svondo apo vaizosvika vanhu vari pakereke.
Rakasimudzwa bhazi ravakubuda muguta reMadzimambo rakananga Harare. Machinda akana aina Elder Mududu akanga aine mufaro une kakusuwa mukati. Vaifara kuti vakanga vabata basa guru asi chaisuwisa inyaya yekuti vakanga wavakusiya guta iri vachiri kuda zvemo.
 

Rakavhetemeswa bhazi zvekuti rwendo rwacho rwakatoita rwupfupi. MuHarare havana kumira vakabva vatonanga kuMarondera. Vakasvika vanhu vari pakati pevhangeri apo Mufundisi akanga achivafundisa.
Mufundisi havana kuzotora nguva refu apo vakazosiira Elder Mududu kuti vambotaurawo mashoko avakanga vainawo. Vakabva vatomira pamberi pevanhu kuti vataure.
"Vana vaMwari ndinofara kumira pamberi penyu ndichikuudzai nyaya inofadza. Rwendo rwatakafamba rwakanga rwuri rwurefu asi rwakanga rwune makomborero. Ndinofara kuti vanhu varikutenda uye vakamirira zuva guru ratiri kuzoenda ikokoko." Pakamboita maungira eruzha vanhu vachinzwa mashoko aya.
"Takatenderera neguta rese reBulawayo tikavaudza kuti kune muzodziwa waMwari arikuuya. Vakatambira shoko ratakavaudza kunge vakanga vachiona muzodziwa wacho. Vana vaMawari shoko randinokuudzai nderekuti nzira yakachena uye kumberi kune mufaro chete.
Ndaona guta reBulawayo randengendeka nekusvika kwemunhu waMwari. Mufundisi Mazondo naMufundisi Jonhson basa rakakumirirai vanhu vanoda kupona." Pakaita maungira ekufara zvekare apo Elder Mududu vakanga wava kunogara pasi.
 

Rwendo rwakanga rwatogadzirirwa apo vanhu vaizomuka mangwana vakatogadzirira kuenda kubasa raMusiki. Mota dzevatungamiri dzakanga dzazotengwa dzakapembererwa kusanganisa neyaMufundisi Mazondo. Vachipedza zvemusi uyu vanhu vakabva vananga kudzimba dzavo. Vamwe vaida kukasika kuzorora sezvo kwaisazodanwa anonzwa zuva raitevera.
Mufundisi vakarara vachigadzirira zvinhu zvavo kuitira kuti vagofamba zvakanaka. Mai Mufundisi vakanga vakangotarisa hapana zvavaitaura. Nechemumoyo vaingoti dai Mwari anzwira vana wevanhu tsitsi nekuti hapana zvavanoziva. Mufundisiwo nechemumoyo vaingoti mukadzi iwe hauna nguva uri panyika ucharisiya sadza. Vakazopedza kugadzira zvinhu zvavo vachibva vapedza.
Kuchiedza vanhu vakaita chipata pata kuenda kukereke kunova ndiko kwavaizotangira rwendo. Mufundisi vakatyairawo vakananga ikoko sezvo vaizofamba pamwwechete.
Vakazadzwa nemufaro vachiona vanhu vatoungana vanonokerwa nerwendo. Rwendo rwakazotanga apo vanhu vakazadza mabhazi mashanu. Mabhazi akatungamira mberi mota dzevatungamiri dzichitevera. Vanhu vaiona vaifunga kuti kurikuendwa kumuchato.
 

Rwendo rwakanga rwakareba kunyangwe zvazvo vakapinda muBulawayo achiri masikati. Rwendo rwakachovhwa apo vakazoona vasvika parailway museum. Vachingobva parailway museum vakabva vapinda muna Khami road. Vakangofamba mbijana vachibva vasvika paiva nenzvimbo yavo yavakanga vatenga.
Vanhu vakaswera vachigadzira nzvimbo pamwe nekuisa tende apo vamwe vakambotenderera vachieuchidza vanhu kuti manheru kwakanga kusingadanwi anonzwa. Sezvo nguva dzichifamba mutambo vakazotanga apo vanhu vakatanga kuuya nehuwandu hwavo.
Chikwata chepraise and worship chakanga chichiimba nemanzwi anotora moyo apo chaitungamirwa nasisi Hazel. Manzwi avanasikana nevanakomana vaiimba apa aitora moyo zvaikoka vakanga vakarara mudzimba umu.
Nenguva isipi tende rakanga risisina pekufema napo nekuda kwevanhu vakanga vakazara uye vamwe vakanga vachiri kuuya. Mufundisi vakazosimuka apo vakanga vatogadzirira kubata basa. Tsvimbo yavo yemoto yakanga iri mumaoko apo yakanga yagadzirira kubata basa. Vakangairereka kudivi kamwechete vachibva vaona vanhu vachidonha nedivi. Vakaidzosa vachibva vaona vanhu vachimira zvekare zvavakanga vakaita. Vanhu vakabva vawedzera kuita ruzha.
 

CHAPTER 32
BLOOD BATH PAHIGHWAY
Ruzha rwakaitwa apa rwakaita kuti vanhu varambe vachiwanda apo Mufundisi vakamboshaya kuti vakanga vachibvepi. Vamwe ndivo vakanga vatyaira mota dzavo kubva kuGweru kuzoona munhu waMwari. Mufundisi Mazondo vakazoenderera mberi wavakutaura mashoko avakanga vainawo.
"Mwana weBulawayo ndauya kuzokusiira ropafadzo, varangarirwa mwana weBulawayo vatsikwa netsoka yemunhu waMwari. Munhu waMwari haangapinde muguta akabuda asina chaarisiira. Tambirai makomborero auya kwamuri ayo mufare mufarisise." Vanhu vakawedzera kuita ruzha rwekufara vachinzwa mashoko aya. Hapana akanga asingade makomborero wese vaiita kubvumira padenga.
"Ndakaona guta rino rakakombwa negoridhe uye raiva nenzira dzegoridhe. Ndikaona varume vakanga vakapfeka zvichena vakarikomba vakandiudza kuti pinda muguta iri. Nazvino ndinongoramba ndichiti rakomborerwa." Nemashoko aya chikwata chepraise and worship chakabva chaita manyemwe.
 

Sisi Hazel vakabva vatoshaura kambo apo inzwi ravo raiita kunge riri pamagetsi. Vaiti ukanzwa kuimba kwemwanasikana uyu vaitofunga kuti vasvika pamusuwo wekudenga. Vakomana wemagitare vaibva vabuda shavi chairo kuita kunge vakazvarwa vachimaridza. Vachipedza Mufundisi vakabva vaenderera mberi.
"Ndinokutenda mwanasikana nekushaura zvinonwisa mvura, Mwari vakukomborere vakuitire zvidhafu dhafu. Ndirikuona vamwe vachienda nemakomborero nhasi chaiye kana vachitenda. Kana paine vanotenda ngavasimudze maoko tione. Nhasi ndatumwa kuzodzinga mweya inotambudza vana wevanhu." Hapana akanga achida kusara pakusimudza maoko chaitova chipata pata.
Mufundisi ndipo pavaidanwa vakadaira vaibva vaita manyemwe. Vabva vanongedza tsvimbo yavo iya muchaunga makanga makasimudzwa maoko. Vanhu vakatanga kupunzika vamwe vachiumburuka. Vamwe ndiwo vaisvetuka svetuka.
"Ndinoraira mweya yerima ibude muvana wevanhu isavatambudza. Mweya yetsvina budai muvana wevanhu ndati budai." Mufundisi vanoshevedzera vakanongedza tsvimbo yavo kuchaunga.
 

Vamwe vakatanga kuumburuka vachichema zvinonzwisa tsitsi. Vamwe ndiwo vaichema vachiti tiregerereiwo munhu washe tatsva. Mufundisi vaibva vawedzera kuita manyemwe vobva vatoramba vakanongedza tsvimbo yavo.
"Calm down now, Masunungurwa vana vaMwari. Hatisati tatanga mutambo uchiripo. Ndinotenda kuti mese mauya pano hamudzokere makadaro, guta rino richava nenhoroondo." Vakataura Mufundisi Mazondo vachiita kunge vari kusvikirwa.
Svondo rese rakapera Mufundisi Mazondo naJonhson naFrank vachibata basa. Musi wekupedzisira ndipo pakanga pasingadanwi anonzwa. Maporofita matatu akanga achibata basa zvekuoneka chaizvo. Mumwe muchinda akauya ari pawheelchair achibva agadzwa kumberi kwechaunga. Mufundisi Mazondo naJonhson ndipo pavakabudirwa neshavi Frank achibata nerumwe rutivi.
Muchinda uya akangosimuka achibva atanga kutenderera achirumbidza basa rakanga rabatwa. Vanhu wese vakanga varipo vaiombera maoko vachifarira basa rakanga rabatwa apa. Vakawanda vakazouya nehurwere hwaityisa apo vaizodzokera vapora. Vamwe vakanga vakatyoka makumbo nemaoka vaibva vapora.
 

Zuva iri rakasiya nhoroondo apo rakanga rakasiyana nemamwe mazuva ese. Mufundisi vakazovhara musangano vanhu vasati voda apo vaikumbira kuti vaite rimwe svondo zvekare. Mufundisi vakazongovimbisa kuti vaizodzoka zvekare mumazuva aitevera.
Mabhazi akazosimuka avakubuda muguta iri akatarira Harare. Vatyairi vacho vaitoita kunge vaityaira ndege iwo ari mabhazi. Hazel akanga akagara munerimwe remabhazi iro rakanga rakatungamira mamwe.
Wavakuteremuka pamateru anosvika paroud about yepaKuwadzana ndipo paakabva anyangarika zvakavhundutsa aiva padivi pake.
Mutyairi webhazi akazongoerekana atarisana nenyoka kumberi kwake. Nyoka yacho yakanga yakakura zvekuti kana shato zana dzaisapinda pairi. Mutyairi ndipo paakati rega ndiinzvenge apo yakanga yava mhere mhere mubhazi. Mukunzvenga bhazi rakabva ratadza kugadzikana richibva rarara nemanhede.
Rimwe rakanga richitevera mumashure rakaedza kuda kunzvenga rakanga radonha apo rakanoyambukira mhiri kwenzira. Rakasvikorohwa negonyeti nepadivi richibva rapidiguka katatu. Rakabva razorora rakadaro. Vamwe vakazosvika vachiona nyatwa iyi apo ropa rakanga roita zvekuerera mumugwagwa.
 

CHAPTER 33 AFTER PAIN
Nenguva isipi vanhu vakanga vatoungana vachiona nyatwa iyi. Vatyairi wemabhazi aitevera kumashure vakaita kunge dzatamba nepwere vachiona chiitiko chinotyisa kudai. Mufundisi nevamwe vatungamiri vakanga vachitevera mumashure vakazosvika vachiona nyatwa iyi yatoitika.
Mufundisi Mazondo vakaburuka mumota mavo vachienda pakanga paine mabhazi aya. Murume mukuru akambopukuta kumeso katatu achida kunyatsoona kuti zvaiva mumaziso ake ndezvechokwadi here.
Vakazocheuka vachida kuona akanga avakwenya apo vakaona ari Jonhson. Haana kuda kutambisa nguva akangovazevezera kuti zvatoita. Mufundisi vakangogutsurira musoro kureva kuti vakanga vazvinzwa uye hurongwa hwakanga hwabudirira.
Hongu zvairwadza kuona rufu rwevanhu vakawanda kudai asi hurongwa hwezvaidiwa hwakanga hwafamba. Mapurisa nemaambulance vakazosvikawo kuti vanunure vanhu vakanga vari munyatwa iyi.
 

Chakava chinhu chinorwadza kuona kuti pavanhu vakanga vari mamabhazi aya mumwechete ndiye akanga ararama. Vamwe wese chakanga chava chando zvekuti maambulance akapinda basa kuvatakura vachirnda kumochari.
Vamwe vakazoenderera mberi vachipedzisa rwendo asi mufaro vakanga vapera. Zvakanga zvakangooma kuti vanhu vachibva kunosiya nhoroondo kunerimwe guta votadza kusvika vakakwana. Tsaona iyi yakava nenhoroondo sezvo zvakanga zvisingatsanangurike kuti pafa vanhu vanodarika zana.
Jonhson akazosara muZimre vamwe vachienderera mberi nerwendo. Mufundisi Mazondo vakazosvikawo nevamwe vatungamira wavo apo vakapinda basa kuzivisa hama dzevakanga vafa mutsaona yebhazi.
Yakarara iri mhere mumusha weMarondera vanhu vachichema rufu rwakanga rwavinga vadikanwa wavo nenzira inosuvisa.
Vapedza basa rekuzivisa vanhu vakazotyaira vachienda kumba kwavo. Vamwe vatungamiri vakatyairawo vachienda kudzimba dzavo. Mufundisi vakasvika nekungopinda mugedhe mavo vakanyarara. Vakasiya vanyatsoona kuti mota yavo yavharika vachibva vapinda mumba.
 

Mai Mufundisi vakatarisa murume wavo vachibva vaona kuti pfungwa dzakanga dzisiri panzvimbo. Ndipo pavakabva vafunga zvekubvunza.
"Ndimika makambofamba rwanga rwurisei rwendo. Vakapona here vanhu uye mafamba zvakanaka here." Kubvunza kwemudzimai uyu kwakambobata Mufundisi vachishaya kuti votangira papi. Hongu vanhu vakanga vapona uye vakanga vasiya nhoroondo kuBulawayo asi pakudzoka zvakazoenda nepamwe mufaro ukapera.
Pahurongwa hwavo zvakanga zvafamba asi zvaimbovaremera kwechinguva. Zita ravo raisazobva pamiromo yevanhu kunyanya panguva iyi yakanga yava kukura kereke.
"Mudzimai wangu rwendo takafamba zvakanaka uye tasiya vanhu vachitenda chaizvo. Basa takabata asi pakudzoka zvazoenda nepamwe. Mabhazi maviri edu abheuka uye vanhu vafa zvinopisa tsitsi. Pavanhu wese iwavo kwararama munhu mumwe chete Mukoma Kudzi." Amai Mufundisi vakapera simba vachinzwa mashoko aya. Vakazoerekana vaenda kuimba yavo yekurara apo vakatanga kuchema variko.
Zvinhu zvairwadza kunzwa kuti vanhu vanofa kunge huku. Chakanyanya kuvarwadza inyaya yekuti vakanga vambozviudzwa kuhope.
 

Neshungu vakazoerekana wava kunamata vachibvunza musiki kuti sei zvadaro. Shungu dzakaramba dzakavabata vachichema kuna musiki misodzi ichierera. Ndipo pavakanzwa kutaura munzeve mavo vakavhunduka sezvo zvakanga zvisati zvamboitika kwavari.
"Murandakadzi nhau yako yanzwikwa asi hazvaigona kumanikidza nguva. Hongu vakanga vazarurirwa ukambonyengetera asi vakaipa akanga akamirawo nesimba. Zvichakadaro ndinokuzivisa kuti hupenyu hwako huri panjodzi memurume vaunogara naye. Kuna hurongwa hwekuvigwa kwevanhu hwapera ndichakuudza zvekuita uzvichengetedze nekuti urikunzi urikuonesesa. Kubva zvino vhara muromo vako ichakwana nguva yekutaura." Inzwi riya richipedza kutaura rakabva ranyarara.
Mai Mufundisi vakamboramba vachieredza misodzi vakapfugama apo vakzosimuka. Kunze kwakasviba kukaedza apo Mufundisi vakamuka vachifambisa nyaya dzekuvigwa kwevakanga varasikirwa nehupenyu.
Yakava mhere muguta apo vanhu vakanga vari panguva yekuchema hama dzavo. Hurongwa hwakafambiswa apo Mufundisi vakamira mira kupa rubatsiro kuti vanhu varerukirwe. Vanhu vakazosvika pakuviga hama dzavo vachibva vadzokera kumisha yavo.
 

CHAPTER 34
NEW MISSION AHEAD
Vanhu vachipedza kuviga hama dzavo pakamboita svondo rese guta reMarondera risina mufaro. Mufundisi vakambosarudza kuvhara kereke kwerimwe svondo zvakare kuti maronda aiva pakati pemoyo yevanhu amboserera.
Mumwe musi Mufundisi vakafonerwa naJonhson vachinzi kwakanga kuine musangano mukuru vaida kuti munhu wese ange aripo. Mufundisi vakagadzirira vachibva vafonerawo Frank kuti vamuudze nyaya yakanga iripo. Vanotaura vanoti yatsika dope yanwa kureva kuti Frank akanga atopindawo mazviri.
Husiku huchisvika vakabuda vakananga kumota yaJonhson yavaigara vachifamba nayo nguva nenguva. Mota yakasimudzwa apo rwendo rwakanga rwatotanga. Yakavhetemeswa mota ichinopinda mumugwagwa mukuru.
Rwaiva rwendo rwurefu apo vakazoona vasvika pasi pemvura. Chikwata chese chakanga chiripo musi uyu hapana asina kuuya. Nenguva isipi vakanga vagarisana pazvigaro zvavo.
 

Vicky akabva apinda mudariro kuti ape hurongwa hwakanga huri mudariro musi uyu. Asati apa hurongwa akabva atanga nekutenda.
"Ndinoda kukutendai zvikuru nebasa ramarikubata munyika umu. Ndinonzwa kufara ndikaona tichiita chinhu chobva chabudirira. Nazvino ndinofara kuti ropa rataichemera takazoita rekuramwirwa chaiko zvekuti kwava kana tikaita imwe nguva tisina kudeura rimwe tinongorarama murambe muchishanda nesimba zvamakaita zvinodadisa." Akadaro Vicky vanhu vachibva vatanga kuombera maoko. Akazoenderera mberi nenyaya yake.
"Nyaya huru yandinaya muzuva ranhasi imwechete. Haina kunyanyokura zvakanyanya asi inogona kukura kana ikasabatwa zvakanaka. Nyaya iripo ndeyehurukuro yatakamboita paya tichiti tinoda humambo hwenyika.
Mukoma Steve mavapapi nenyaya yedu." Vicky achipedza kutaura akabva amirira Steve kuti ataure.
"Ichokwadi kuti ndakanga ndakakuvimbisai kuti humambo hwenyika ndichahutora hwouya mumaoko edu. Hongu ndanonoka kuzvizadzisa nekuti hazvaigona kuti ndimanikidze nguva isati yandikwanira. Kutaura kwatiri kuita kuno ndatogadzirira kubata basa uye handina mazuva ndiri kuzoribata." Vanhu vakabva vamboomberera Steve maoko achibva aenderera mberi.
 

"Sezvandakataura paya kuchaita nzara uye vanhu vachatambura zvichaunganidza vatungamiri wepasi pano. Ndipo panenge patotangira basa redu uye kana tapinda muhutungamiri tichaisa mitemo yatinoda munyika uye mukereke kunyanya. Ndiverengerei svondo chete ndinenge ndatotanga basa." Vanhu vakauchira zvekare vachinzwa mashoko aya.
Vicky akazosimbisa kuti basa iroro rigobatwa uye taifanirwa kuzoribudirira. Mufundisi vakazopinda mudariro apo vakanga vavakupa chichemo chavo chezvaivashaisa mufaro pabasa iri.
"Pamusoroi dare rose, pamusoroi mambokadzi. Ndinofara kuti basa tirikubata uye ririkufamba zvakanaka. Asi ini ndakazvimiririra ndine chinhu chimwechete chichiri kundivhiringa munzira yangu, mudzimai wangu anopesana neni pane zvese zvandinoronga maererano nekereke uye anooneswa zvese zvatinoita dzimwe nguva anooneswa nezvatinenge tichironga. Kana zvichibvira tinofanirwa kuona zvekuita naye." Pakamboita runyararo pasina aitaura.
Vanhu vakambotarisana apo vaifunga kuti nyaya iyi voitamba sei. Vanhu vakaita sana mai Mufundisi vaida kuronga tsoro makachenjera nekuti vaigona kuoneswa zvamuri kuvarongera.
 

"Ipapo regai gare tapedza dambudziko racho Mufundisi, mukamurwisa muri imi hazvibude zvakanaka.
Ndavakutobuda izvozvi ndakananga ikoko imi munozosara kubva kuno ndapedza basa. Hazvina mhosva mukaona wava chando nekuti vari kukanganisa basa kuti riende mberi." Hazel akadaro achipindura nhau yakanga yataurwa naMufundisi. Mufundisi havana kuita nharo nazvo uye Vicky akabva abvumira padenga.
Hazel akabva angonyangarika pakare achibuda mumvura umu. Musangano vakasara uchienderera mberi apo vakazoupendera vachisimbisana kuti basa ngaribatwe humambo huuye mumaoko avo.
Amai Mufundisi vakanga vakarara pamubhedha pavo apo vakanga vachirota. Ndipo pavakaona murume akanga achifamba akapfeka zvichena achiuya kwavari. Murume uye akaramba achifamba apo zvaakanga akapfeka zvaiita kunge zvinoteya amai Mufundisi.
Achisvika pavari haana kuda kumbovakwazisa akangovati muka izvozvi uende kugomo.
Mai Mufundisi vakapepuka pakarepo semunhu akanga ari pakurota. Ndipo pavakanzwa maungira ekutaura munzeve mavo vachinzi vabude vaende kugomo vanonamata variko. Havana kuda kutambisa nguva saka vakabva vabuda vakananga kugomo sekurairwa kwavakanga vaitwa.
 

CHAPTER 35
MAI MUFUNDISI ESCAPES
Kugomo kwacho rwaitova rwendo zvekuti vaitombokanganwa kuti vachasvika. Semunhu vakanga vaine ruchengetedzo havana kumbotarisa zvekuti kunze kune rima. Akanga avaraira kuti vabude ndiye aizovachengeta munzira.
Hazel zvaakabuda pasi pemvura akasimudza mota yake semunhu akanga asina nguva yekutambisa.
Yakavhetemeswa zvekuti vaifunga kuti pari kutyairwa mdege. Chinangwa chake chaiva chekuti akasvika pamba paamai Mufundisi obva aona zvekuita navo.
Akazoona avakupinda muMarondera kuti akanga achibhururuka. Kunze kwakanga kuchakasviba apo akaona asvika pagedhe raMufundisi.
"Nhasi mukadzi uya ndomuuraya achanovaudza varikumarinda kuti ndakazviparira nekutadza kuteerera murume. Ndinonzi Hazel ini pandinosvika ndinosiya pachirira mhere." Hazel aitaura ega akamira pagedhe raMufundisi. Ainyemwerera aine tarisiro yekuti aizoona amai Mufundisi varimo obva apedza basa osiya vasisafemi.
 

Pakarepo akabva anyangarika achibva azoona amira pamusuwo. Ndipo paakabva achinja kuita rovambira achibva apinda mukati. Nyoka yakafamba yakananga kuimba yairara amai Mufundisi apo yakaita kunge yafemerwa.
Ichingopinda yakabva yasimudza musoro yakagadzirira kuruma yobva yaenda. Ndipo payakaona iri nzvimbo amai Mufundisi vachiti vakandiisepi. Panguva iyi yakabva yatanga kutenderera mumba imomo yava kutsvaga dzimba dzese apo yakazopinda makanga muine vana. Vana yakanga isinei navo saka yakabva yabuda hayo yakananga kumusuwo. Ndipo payakazoshanduka zvekare kuita Hazel.
"Asi vaendepi chaizvo amai Mufundisi? Husiku huno munhukadzi angafamba achiendepi.?" Akazvibvunza Hazel apo akanga achigere kutenda zvaakanga aona. Akazobva pamba apa achibva avhetemesa mota akananga kudziva.
Mamhanyiro aakanga achiita aitova ekuti asvike vanhu vasati vaenda. Haana kutora nguva yakareba akanga atova pasi pemvura apo akaona musangano uchangopenderwa. Haana kuda kuswera achitenderera akabva avaudza kuti zvemusi uyu basa rakanga rabondera.
 

Vakazowirirana kuti vaisazomira kurwisa mudzimai uyu nguva yaizokwana chete. Mumwe nemumwe akazobuda mumvura akananga kumba kwake. Amai Mufundisi vakazosvika kugomo uko vakabva vapfugama kuti vambotaura namusiki. Nguva yakanga yatokwana yekuti Mwari vambovapa mhinduro. Ndipo pavakanzwa inzwi raitaura munzeve mavo.
"Murandakadzi warangarirwa nekuda kwekuramba vakasimba pakunyengetera. Kubva zvino uchagara mugomo rino kusvika hondo iyi yapera. Njodzi yavakatarisana nayo ihuru ukaita zvekutamba unodzika muvhu." Amai Mufundisi vakaramba vakanyara vachimirira kunzwa manzwi aizotevera.
Ndipo pavakaerekana wavakuita kunge kumberi kwavo kwakanga kwamera chivhiti vhiti. Vanotarisa pachivhiti vachibva vaona murume wavo ari pasi pembura nevamwe vanhu wavasina kuziva. Vakatarisa kudaro ndipo pavakaona munhu achichinja kuita nyoka achipinda mumba mavo.
Vakatarira nyoka ichitenderera nemba yese apo yakazopinda makanga makarara vana. Amai Mufundisi vakanzwa kutya vakatarisa chivhiti vhiti ichi vachityira vana wavo. Ndipo pavakanzwa inzwi richiti vana vakachengetwa. Inzwi raitaura munzeve mavo rakabva raenderera mberi.
 

"Murandakadzi zvavaona apa ndizvo zvirikutoitika. Uchagara mugomo muno kusvika ndakuudza kuti chiburuka. Kana chiri chikafu zvanga usatya hako nekuti uchaguta. Usafunganya kuti sei usina chikafu nekuti uchachiona chichiuya." Rakataura zvekare inzwi riya richibva raenderera mberi.
"Kugara kwauchata mugomo muno kuchakubatsira nekuti wanga ucharamba uchidya mari dzeropa idzi. Chiramba vakasimba unamate." Inzwi riya rinobva raenda apo amai Mufundisi vakabva vasara vari iwo.
Vakabva vapfugama vachitenda musiki nekuvazarurira nhau dzakanga dzakavanzika seidzi. Ndipo pavakabva vambosarudza kurara apo vaida kumbozorora zvishoma. Nenguva isipi vakanga wava kutorota.
Vakatanga kuona mukoma Kudzi avo vakanga vararama patsaona vakarara muchipatara. Vakaramba vakatarira apo vakaona mumwe murume akapfeka zvichena achibva paari. Ndipo paakauya kwavakanga vari achibva atanga kutaura navo. Muchinda uya akabva avaudza kuti mukoma Kudzi ava vaizomuka uye hutano hwavo hwaizowandudzwa. Muchinda uya akaenderera mberi achiudza amai Mufundisi kuti ndiye muchinda akanga achazobatsira kurwisa vakaipa vakanga wava kuuraya kereke. Amai Mufundisi vakabva vapepuka pakarepo.
 

CHAPTER 36
THE CHURCH SPLITS
Pavakapepuka amai Mufundisi ndipo pavakatanga kubatanidza hope dzavakanga vachangobva kurota. Kudzi vaimuziva zvakanyanya uye akanga akasimba pakushumira mwari. Vakambotenda Mwari nekununura mwanakomana uyu mutsaona kunyangwe zvazvo akanga atyoka ruoko pamwe negumbo.
"Asi mwana uyu akanga asingazvione here kuti ari kunochekereswa nababa ava? Akanga azonakidzwa zvakadii zvekutadza kuona kuti kunamata kurikuita baba ava ndekweropa? Asi ndinongofara hangu kuti Mwari vamupa mumwe mukana uye kana kuri kwekuti mashoko andanzwa munzeve dzangu kuhope achazoitika ndinoziva kuti nemwana iyeye tinobudirira." Amai Mufundisi vaingotaura vega vakagara zvavo.
Mufundisi Mazondo zvavakabva kudziva vakasvika mumba vachiona mudzimai asimo sekutaurwa kwakanga kwaitwa naHazel. Murume mukuru akapererwa zvekushaya kuziva kuti amai ava vakanga vaendepi. Zvaiva nani kuona vakafa zvavo asi vachionekwa kuti varere apo.
 

Vakamboedza kubvunza vana asi hapana aiziva kwakanga kwaenda amai. Vakazongozviudza kuti vachadzoka uye paizoita chimurenga chete. Ndiwo vaizoudza vamwe kuti mumba hamutizwe. Ndidzo pfungwa dzakanga dzina Mufundisi Mazondo.
Vakazoswera pamba semunhu akanga asisaendi kubasa. Vakanga vatoendesa tsamba yekusiya basa apo vakanga wava kuita zvekereke yavo. Imwe pfungwa yakauya mumusoro mavo vachibva vaenda kunotora tsvimbo yemoto. Vakaisimudza vachidaidza zita raMai Mufundisi vakainongedza mudenga. Vakasvika pakuona kuti hazvina chimuko vachibva vaidzorera mumba.
Hongu tsvimbo iyi yaibata mabasa makuru asi pamudzimai wavo yakanga isingashande.
Vanozoswera pamba zvavo apo vaigadzirira zvekuenda kusvondo zuva remangwana. Sezvo pakanga pamboita svondo mbiri vasingavhuri kereke paisazodanwa anonzwa.
Paizova nekusuwa hapo sezvo vanhu vakanga vachine maronda etsaona pamoyo asi vaizofara kuti kereke yava kuenderera mberi. Zvishamiso zviya zvakanga zvavakuenderera mberi. Husiku hwakazosvika apo Mufundisi vakabva vanorara. Husiku humwechete uhwu Elder Mududu vakabva vatanga kurota.
 

Vakatanga kuona zvese zvakanga zvaitika kuBulawayo zvichidzokorora mumaziso mavo. Vakatanga kuona zvishamiso zvese zvakaitwa muguta reBulawayo. Zvese izvi vakaramba vakazvitarira zvichipfuura nepameso avo.
Vakaramba vakatarira apo vakanga vooneswa vanhu vari parwendo rwekudzoka vachibuda muguta iri.
Elder Mududu vakaramba vakatarira vachiona vanhu vaifara vachibuda muguta iri uye vakanga vasara vaine mufaro vakapfuurikidza. Ndipo pavakaita kunge vasimudzwa vachibva vamira pamusoro pechikomo chaiva pedyo neround about yemuKuwadzana.
Vakatarira kudaro ndipo pavakaona mabhazi avo apo vaiona munhu wese akanga ari mukati. Vakaziva musikana akanga aimba zvinonwisa mvura kupraise and worship uyo akabva anyangarika vakatarisa.
Vakavhunduka panguva iyi apo vakazoona ashanduka kuita zinyoka iro rakazokonzeresa tsaona.
Ndipo pavakanzwa maungira ekutaura apo vakabvunzwa kuti vaizviziva here kuti ndizvo zvakaitika patsaona. Kuhope ikoko vakatadza kupindura nekutya zvavakanga vaona. Vakabva varairwa kunzi maoko aMufundisi akanga azara ropa uye kereke yakanga yatanga kutoputsika. Elder Mududu vakabva vapepuka pakarepo ziya richichururuka muviri wose. Hope dzavakanga varota dzaityisa.
 

Vakamutsa mudzimai wavo vachibva vamutaurira zvavakanga vaona kuhope. Mudzimai wavo yakanga iri imwe yemhare dzakasimba kana tasvika panguva dzekunamata. Akabva araira murume vake kuti Mwari vakanga vataura naye nenzira iyi kuti aone zvirikuitika mukereke.
Amai Mududu vakabva vatopfugama kuti vanamate vagodzikinurwa parwendo rwavakanga wava kufamba. Zvakanga zvoda kuzarurirwa nedenga kuti vofamba sei. Kunze kwakazoedza apo iwo nemurume wavo vakasarudza kunosiya mota yavakanga vatengerwa vosara neyeziya ravo. Ndipo pavaibva vaoneka apo vaizotsvaga imwe kereke yekuenda kana kunamata havo vari pamba.
Munhu wavakarangarira mudzimai waElder Marwei uyo wavakabva vaudza pafoni zvese zvakanga zvaitika. Mai Marwei vakazovimbisa kuudza murume wavo hameno kuti aizozvitambirawo sei.
Sezvo raiva zuva rekuenda kukereke vakagadzirira vachibva vaenda. Mufundisi Jonhson naMazondo vakanga vatovamo kare. Elder Mududu vakasvika vachingogara muchaunga nemhuri yavo izvo zvakaita kuti Mufundisi vaite mibvunzo. Vaiziva vachigara pazvigaro zvehutungamiri izvo zvaiva mberi kwekereke.
 

CHAPTER 37
THE CHURCH SPLITS
Mufundisi vakazongonyarara havo vachida kuzoona kuti chii chaitora nzvimbo. Hurongwa hwekereke hwakazotanga semazuva ese. Elder Marwei vakabva vapindawo nemhuri yavo. Vakasvikogara kuzvigaro zvekumashure izvo zvakashamisa Mufundisi zvekare.
Vamwe vana wesangano vakangotarisawo vachishamisika kuona zvigaro zvehutungamiri zvaiva zvisina vanhu kumberi asi varidzi vacho vakagara muchaunga. Praise and worship yakasimuka ichibva yaimba nziyo dzekurumbidza.
Mufundisi Mazondo vakazosimuka kuti vakushe shoko kuvana wesangano. Vana wesangano vakabva wavaimbira kambo kekuti Mufundisi wedu muvakomborere.
Pakusimuka kwakaita Mufundisi pane mumwe musikana akaerekana asimuka achida kutaura mashoko aakanga ainawo. Aiita kupopota achitaura nechimwe chirudzi izvo zvakaita kuti vanhu vamutarise ari paakanga ari. Ndipo paakaudza Mufundisi kuti ane mashoko aanoda kutaura.
 

"Mufundisi ndinokutendai nekuramba muchitidzidzisa pamwe nekutidzora zuva nezuva. Izvozvo zvakanaka chose asi pane zvandirikuudzwa munzeve dzangu zviri kundishungurudza. Mufundisi dai matsvaga Mwari pachiri pedyo musati mapedza vanhu. Nemiwo vana vaMwari ndati ndikunyeverei musati mapera kuti dai manamata. Ndaona kumberi kwazouya zvinodarika tsaona yamakaona iyi."
