Maziso evanhu akaramba akatarisa kumusikana uyu sezvo chaiva chishamiso.
Musikana uyu akanga asati amboimba mukereke kana kumbotaurawo asi zvakangotangira ipapo. Vanhu vazhinji vakatanga kumushora asi vamwe vakatenda zvaakanga achangobva kutaura. Mufundisi vakabva varaira mamwe machinda aiva mukereke umu kuti vamuburitse vamudzinge.
Achiona kuti ndizvo zvaakanga ari kurongerwa akabva atanga kutofamba ega achibuda mukereke umu.
Akangosiya shoko rekuti zita rangu ndinoitwa Nyasha vazhinji muchandirangarira henyu kana nguva yacho yakwana.
Panguva yaakabuda vamwe vashoma vakatanga kutevera vachibuda mumwe mumwe. Elder Mududu vakanga vakatarira vachinyemwerera vachiona chiitiko ichi. Zvakabva zvaratidza kuti hope dzavairota aisava manyepo.
 

Mufundisi vakazotanga kukusha shoko apo vakanga vasara vaibvumira hameni yepamusoro. Vakarikusha shoko vachiita kunge munhu aisvikirwa zvekuti vanhu vakanga vakateerera vaitoona masuvo edenga akazaruka. Vapedza ndipo pavakazopa mashoko avakanga vainawo pamusoro perwendo rwavakafamba kuenda kuBulawayo.
"Ndinokutendai vana vaMwari nerudo rwamakaratidza kuenda kunotimiririra kuguta reBulawayo. Mwari agokukomborerai uye ndinokuzivisai kuti kuBulawayo vachange wavakutanga kushumira svondo rinotevera uye Pastor Jonhson ndivo vanenge vachienda ikoko. Zvichakadaro ndinotaura ndakasuwa ndichiti ndine hurombo nechiitiko chakazoitika tava kudzoka." Panguva iyi maronda evanhu akambodzimbirwa apo vakabva varangarira tsaona yakatora vanhu vanopfuura zana. Mufundisi vakambonyarara vachiona misodzi yeshungu ichierera pameso avana wesangano.
Vakazoenderera mberi vachinyaradza vakanga vachieredza misodzi.
"Zvanga zvakaoma hazvo asi hazvaigona kuti timanikidze nguva. Yava nguva yekuti tiende mberi ndinovimba Mwari vachakunyaradzai." Mufundisi vachipedza kutaura mashoko avo ekupendera vakabva vagara zvavo pasi.
 

Hurongwa hwakateverana apo yakazosvika nguva yezvipo. Vanhu vaiita kunge varikusvikirwa kuri kubvisa zvipo apo Mufundisi vaisekerera vakagara kumberi.
Panobuda mari ndipoka pavaidanwa vakadaira. Musi uyu hakuna kuporofitwa apo vaiti vaida kumbosimudza mweya yevanhu kubva pakuchema.
Elder Mududu vakazosimuka nemhuri yavo vari muchaunga apo vakapa mashoko ekutenda nguva yavakashanda naMufundisi. Vachipedza kupa mashoko ekutenda vakabva vazivisa kereke kuti vakanga wava kumbomira kubata navo uye vaizovazivisa kana wavakuzodzoka. Mufundisi Mazondo vakaita kunge vachazvipanhira pasi vachinzwa mashoko aya.
Vachingogara pasi Elder Marwei vakabva vasimukawo nemhuri yavo vachipa mashoko ekuoneka. Chakava chishamiso kuona vamwe wavatungamiri vachisarudza kusiya kereke. Kereke yakazopera apo Elder Mududu naElder Marwei vakabva vanosiya kii dzemota kuna Mufundisi.
Vanhu vakazoparara vachibva vaenda kudzimba dzavo. Mufundisi vakatyairawo mota yavo vakananga kwavanogara asi musoro vakanga wavakutorema nekufunga. Pakazongouya imwe pfungwa mumusoro mavo yakavasiya vachisekerera wega.
 

CHAPTER 38
CHOTSVA CHIMURENGA
Murume mukuru akasvika pagedhe repamba pake achingosekerera ega pasina aimuudza nyaya dzinosetsa. Mufundisi vakanga vatofunga zvekupinda pahondo nana Elder avo vakanga vasarudza kusiya kereke.
Musikana uya akanga avanyadzisa pamberi pevanhu vakabva vamubatanidzira zvekare pavanhu wavakanga vachida kurwisa. Zvevamwe vakanga vabuda vakanga vasinei nazvo nekuti vamwe vacho vakanga vasingavazivi. Vakanga vaine basa nevavanoziva pamwe nemusikana uyu wavakanga vaziva chiso nezita.
Kuti vaite basa iri wega zvaivaremera saka vaizogara pasi nechimwe chikwata vasvika pasi pemvura. Ndipo pavaizoronga tsoro yavo kuti vangarwisa sei vanhu ava vakanga wavakuda kupesana navo.
Vakapinda pagedhe pavo vachibva vamisa mota pavaisimisa mazuva ese. Vakapinda mumba vachibva vatanga kufunga zvakadzama. Vaizoitamba sei nyaya iyi? Vaingozvifunga havo vakagara apo vaiona vhidhiyo ravo recrusade yavakaita kuBulawayo.
 

Vakazoshevedzwa pava paya nemwana wavo mukuru kuti vauye kuzodya. Vakadya havo chikafu chakanga chakabikwa nehunyanzvi nemwanasikana wavo akanga akura zvekugona mabasa emumba. Vachipedza kudya vakabva vafonera Jonhson semunhu akanga ari kumashure kwenguva.
Vakabva vatowirirana kuti vaizoenda kumvura manheru iwayo sezvo vakanga vaine nyaya yaida kugadziriswa. Vachipedza kutaura pafoni vakabva vadzokera kunoona vhidhiyo yavo iya yavakanga vasati vapedza kuona.
Jonhson akazosvika pava paya vachibva vatopinda parwendo. Nyasha zvaakabuda mukereke muya akatanga kufamba achienda kwaaisaziva. Aingonzwa kuti pane aimufambisa asi asingazive kwaaiendeswa. Akafamba rwendo rwurefu apo akazoona avakukwira mugomo. Ava mugomo akazonzwa kuimba kweinzwi raakaziva.
Akabva atanga kufamba achienda nedivi raibva inzwi riya. Akaramba achifamba apo akatanga kunzwa inzwi riya richisvika pedyo naye. Ndipo paakatanga kuona mukadzi aiva nechekure mbijana uyo vaakabva aziva kuti aiva amai Mufundisi. Akafambisa akananga ikoko apo iwo vakabva vasimukawo vachiuya kwaari.
Vakasvikombundirana vachibva vatora nguva vakadaro vachieredza misodzi.
 

"Ko mwana wangu urikubva nepi? Vaziva sei kuti ndirikuno?" Vakabvunza amai Mufundisi apo vakanga vachiri kushamisika kuona mwana wavo wesangano. Vakanga vasina kutarisira kuona munhu akadaro munzvimbo yavakanga vari.
"Amai zvakaoma mufunge, ndangosundwa kuti ndiuye kuno ndabva nekukereke. Mufundisi ndavaudza pamberi pechaunga kuti vatsvage Mwari uye nekuti maoko avo akazara ropa. Ndipo pavada kutumira vanhu kuti vandiburitse mukereke zvechisimba asi ndabva ndabuda ndega. Ndazongoudza vanhu kuti vachandifunga nekuti vamwe vandishora vamwe vakanditenda vachibva vabuda pamwechete neni. Ndazongosundwawo kuuya kuno." Akataura Nyasha achiudza amai Mufundisi avo vakanga wava kutoeredza misodzi.
Mai Mufundisi vakazoudza Nyasha kuti yakanga yava nguva yekusimba kupfugama nekuti pamberi pavo pakanga pane hondo hombe. Nyasha akatenderana navo sezvo akanga aona ropa richierera mumaoko emurume uyu.
Mai Mufundisi vakazoudza Nyasha kuti vakanga vatiza kumba nehusiku apo muvengi akanga ari munzira kuuya kuzovauraya. Vakazoratidzwa munhu akachinja kuita nyoka akanga atumwa kubva kugungwa kuti avatorere hupenyu hwavo.
 

Nyasha akazorangarira kuti ane chikafu chaakanga akatakura mubhegi make kuti azodya abuda mukereke. Akabva achiburitsa apo akatanga kudya naamai Mufundisi. Pachokwadiwo nzara yakanga yavabvunza mutupo asi vaishingirira semunha akanga ari panguva yekurwisana nemuvengi.
Kunze kwakazosviba apo vaiti vakagara gara vombopfugama. Mufundisi Mazondo vakazosvika kudziva apo vakaita wekutanga kupinda pamuzinda. Vamwe vakazotanga kuuya vatovapo kare.
Pakambokurukurwa dzakawanda apo Mufundisi Mazondo vakazopinza yavo mudariro.
Iyi yakatambirwa neHazel apo akanga ava nemamwe mafungiro. Akanga afunga zvekurwisa vanhu ava vari kwavakanga vari. Zvekuvashanyira zvainonoka nekuti aizosvika vapihwa chenjedzo. Sezvo vanhu vacho vakanga vakati wandei aizobatsirana naMillicent naLisa uye hondo iyi vaizoitamba ari masikati.
Vakazopedza musangano vachibva vanyangarika semazuva ese. Mufundisi vakatyairwa naJonhson apo vakazoona vatosvika kumba. Vakasiiwa pagedhe apo Jonhson akabva aenderera mberi nerwendo rwake.
Mugundisi vachipinda mumba nhare yavo yakabva yarira. Vakatarisa vachibva vaona vari Muvhangeri Sheshe vaifona.
 

CHAPTER 39
THE WAR CONTINUES
Mufundisi Mazondo pavakadaira nhare iyi vakavhunduka nemashoko avakanzwa. Vakanga vasina kutarisira mashoko akadai panguva iyi. Saka vaizosara nani kana zvinhu zvakanga zvamira mamiriro aya.
Muvhangeri Sheshe zvavakabva kukereke vakanga vambopinda muhurukuro nemudzimai wavo maererano nezvakanga zvava kuitika mukereke.
Vakazongopedzisira nekusimbisana kuti paida nyasha dzaMusiki kuti vapindire.
Vakazonorara havo semunhu aida kuzomukira kubasa mangwana acho. Ndipo pavakaona vapinda munyika yezviroto iyo yaunosangana nezvakawanda kusanganisira zvausati wamboona.
Vakatanga kurota vari pakufamba nemota yavo vachienda kukereke. Ndipo pavakati wavakuda kusvika mota yakabva yamira yega. Vakaedza kuimutsa asi yakaramba iri panzvimbo imwechete. Vari pakurwisana nayo vakabva vaona murume aiuya pamota ipapo akapfeka zvichena. Aifambisa zvairatidza kuti akanga ari mumashure menguva.
 

Muvhangeri vakabva vambosiyana zvekunetsana nemota yavo apo vakayeva murume uya kusvika asvika pavakanga vari. Airatidza kuti akanga aine hasha uye akanga asina nguva yekuseka.
"Urikumanikidza mota kufamba urikuti urikuenda kupi? Urikuenda kunoitei zvekare?" Akataura murume uya nenzwi rinehasha.
"Ndirikuenda kukereke mukuru wangu ndirikushaya kuti chii chatora nzvimbo pamota yangu." Vakapindura Muvhangeri Sheshe apo vaitarisa chiso chemurume uyu vachiita zvekubiridzira. Chiso chemurume wacho chaisatarisika nekugumbuka kwaakanga akaita.
"Ndavakuda kuchikuudza inini chokwadi chizere, kereke yaurikuenda ikereke yeropa. Kana uchida hupenyu hwako regera kuenda ikoko, uyezve kusiya kwauchaita wobva vasimba mabvi nekuti Mufundisi vachakuronda. Chitendeuka udzokere kumba ndichakuudza zvekuita." Akataura murume uya achibva anyangarika.
Muvhangeri vakamutsa moto pakarepo ichibva yamuka. Havana kuda kutambisa nguva vakabva vatarira kwavakanga vabva. Havana kure kwavakaenda vakabva vapepuka. Vachingopepuka vakabva vamutsa mudzimai wavo vachimuudza zvavakanga varota. Mudzimai wavo akabva atovasimbisa kuti vasiye kereke.
 

Vakazosvika pakurara vawirirana kuti vaizonodzosera mota vobva vasiyana nezvekunamatiswa zvifananidzo. Kuseni ndipo pavakamuka vachiudza Mufundisi pafoni kuti vakanga vafunga kumbomira kubata navo uye vakanga wachida kumbozorora vachifunga imwe kereke yekuzoenda.
Apa ndipo pakanyatsoona Mufundisi kuti vakanga wakusara wega hutungamiri hwavo huchienda.
Vakazorangarira kuti pane wavakanga vapa basa rekuranga saka vaizomisa humwe hutungamiri.
Elder Mududu vakamukawo kuseni kwakare vachigadzirira kuenda kubasa. Vaishanda samaneja kuFood world saka vaipinda mudhorobha mazuva ese. Vakapinda mumota yavo iyo yakanga yakauya neziya ravo vachibva vatanga rwendo.
Mota yaivhetemeswa zvayakanga isati yamboitwa musi uyu. Elder vakaga vari mumashure menguva vaitoda kufambira mudenga chaimo. Mota yakaramba yakatsikwa zvekuti vakatozovhunduka vachiona vasvika muMsasa. Mota yakaramba yakatsikwa apo yakanga yatarisana neround about yepaTM. Elder Mududu vakangoerekana vaona mukadzi akanga akamira pamberi pavo. Pavakada kumisa mota vakabva vainzwa ichiita zvekusundwa kumashure apo yakasvika ichinorovana nebhazi.
 

Nenguva isipi vanhu vakanga vatoungana vachiona chiitiko ichi. Vanhu vaingoona mota yakaparara isingatarisike asi mutyairi anga ari mumota macho vasingamuoni. Elder Mududu vakanga vabuda mutsaona iyi vasina kana vanga izvo zvaitoshamisa vanhu pavaitaura kuti ndiwo vakanga vachityaira.
Zvemusi uyu vakabva vafona kubasa vachitaura kuti ndizvo zvakanga zvaitika. Vakabva vafonerawo mudzimai wavo vachimuudza chiitiko ichi. Vakabva vaudzwawo chimwe chiitiko chinosuwisa chakanga chaitika. Mwana waElder Marwei akanga angodonha achibva anyarara akadaro.
Izvi zvaireva kuti akanga arwiswa nezvaasingaoni uye akanga ari pedyo nerufu. Elder Mududu vachinzwa nyaya iyi vakanga vatononokerwa nekunonunura mwana uyu neminamato. Mapurisa akazosvikawo achiongorora tsaona iyi apo vakabata basa ravo sezvariri.
Elder Mududu vakazotsvaga mota yaivamhanyisa kuMarondera nekukasika. Zveyavo yakanga yaparara zvakanga zvapfuura chikuru ndechekuti vakanga vararama. Mota yakavhetemeswa yakananga paMarondera apo Elder vaingonamata nechemumoyo. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatosvika kumba kwaElder Marwei. Panguva iyi akanga ava matambudziko maviri apo mudzimai waMarwei akanga angozvimba dumbu.
 

CHAPTER 40 SURPRISE VISIT
Elder Mududu havana kumboda kuita nguva yekukwazisa vanhu kana kubvunza kuti chii chirikutora nzvimbo. Vakangodhonza mumwe wavo Elder Marwei vachibva vatanga kunamata.
Mwana akaramba akangati zii akarara pasi asingambopfakanyiki. Nerimwe divi mudzimai waElder Marwei dumbu rakabva rawedzera kuzvimba. Varume vakuru vachipedza kunamata vakadikitira vachiona kuti hondo yacho yakanga isina kumira mushe.
Vakapfugama zvekare apa nguva iyi vakanga wava kunamata neshungu. Mudzimai waMarwei ndiye aingozhamba asisagoni kugarisika nemarwadzo. Elder Marwei vachipedza kunamata vakangotarisana vapererwa.
Nekunamata kwavakanga vaita vaitarisira kuti vachaona shanduko. Elder Marwei vakambobata shaya vakatarisa mwana wavo nemudzimai akanga achingozhamba apo inzwi rakanga razoshoshoma. Vakanga vari panguva yakaoma zvekuti vakanga vasisina tarisiro yekuona vanhu awa vari vapenyu zvekare.
 

"Saka toitasei Elder Mududu, ini ndapererwa ndakutorwadziwa nekuramba ndakatarisa zvinhu zvakadai." Vakabvunza Elder Marwei vachikumbira zano kune mumwe wavo.
"Apa pakutoda chipatara mukuru wangu, zvimwe tinobatsirana kunamata chipatara chichibatsirawo." Elder Mududu vakataura mashoko aya vachitokumbira kii dzemota yavaMarwei. Vasati vatambidzwa kii dzemota vakabva vanzwa manzwi evakadzi vaiimba panze.
Wese vakateerera apo aiva manzwi evanhu wavanoziva. Pasina nguva vakaona Sisi Nyasha naamai Mufundisi Mazondo vachipinda pamusuwo. Havana kumboita nguva yekugogodza sezvo vakanga vari mumashure menguva. Havana kumboda kukwazisana nevanhu vakangonanga paiva nevarwere wavo.
Vakabatana maoko vari vaviri vachibva vatanga kuimba kambo kekuti Mwari wangu ndibate ruoko. Elder Mududu naElder Marwei vakanga vangotarisa vachida kuona kuti zvaizoperera papi. Mupfungwa dzavo zvaiva pachena kuti vanhu ava vakanga wavatumirwa naMwari kuti vagovabatsira pakunamatira varwere. Mai Mufundisi naSisi Nyasha vakaramba vachiimba apo vakazenge vapfugama paiva nemwana waElder Marwei.
 

Mai Mufundisi vakabata mwana uya kumeso apo Nyasha akaita zvimwechetezvo. Vakabva vashevedzera wese kuti Munashe muka vachibva vamuregedza.
Pakarepo Munashe mwana waElder Marwei akabva amuka. Vachipedza naMunashe vakabva vaenda pakanga paina amai wacho avo vakanga vachiri kungozhamba vachitadza kugarisika.
Apa vakasvikobatirana dumbu riya vachitaura kuti amai Elder matopora apo vakabva variregedza. Pakarepo amai Elder vakabva vatanga kurutsa zvinhu zvaiita kunga zvipikiri. Pavakaedza kuzvirutsa dumbu rakabva raserera.
Elder Mududu naElder Marwei avo vakanga vachibvumira kambo kaiimbwa vakabva vatanga kutobvumira padenga. Nguva iyi vakanga vasina kutarisira kuzosangana nayo asi Musiki vakaratidza simba ravo.
Vakazoisa munamato wekupedza basa ravakanga vabata. Vachipedza vakabva vagara zvavo pasi kuti vapinde muhurukuro. Mai Mufundisi vakanga vaine mashoko ekutaura saka vakabva vatora mukana iwoyo kuti vamataure. Vane zvavakanga vaoneswa vari kugomo varipakunamata. Uyezve pamunamato wavakaita pamba paElder vane zvavakanga vaoneswa zvekare.
 

"Vanababa hondo yandiri kurwa nayo ndiyo hondo yamuri kurwa nayo zvekare. Elder Mududu mutende Mwari vakuratidzai kuti nyangwe mota ikaparara kusara yakaita kunge bhora munongobuda musina vanga.
Manga matongerwa rufu asi kana nguva yemukuru isati yakwana zvinoramba." Amai Mufundisi vakambonyarara Nyasha achibva apindawo mudariro.
"Vana Elder Mwari vanokudai mufunge. Minamato yamabata hamuna kukundikana nekuti ndiyo yatishevedza kubva kure kwatanga tiri. Asi dai mazoenda kuchipatara kwamanga muchida kuenda manga muri kuperera mumugwagwa mese nekuti riva ranga ratoteiwa kare. Tinongotenda hedu kuti panogumirwa vanhu ndipo panotangira Mwari." Akataura Nyasha achibva azonyarara.
Mai Mufundisi vakazotsanangura matiziro avakaita kumba kwavo vatumirwa muvengi kuti avauraye.
Vakabva vatoudza vanaElder kuti vachibva pamba apa vakanga vari kutonanga kugomo.
Nyasha akabva avaudzawo kuti zuva raakafumura Mufundisi pamberi pechaunga akazongosundwawo apo akaerekana ava mugomo achiona amai Mufundisi.
Vakazosimbisana kuti vaizoramba vachibatsirana kusvika hutongi hwepasi pemvura hwakurirwa. Vakadzi vaviri ava vakazooneka vachibva vaenda.
 

CHAPTER 41
NEW MISSION STARTED
Mai Mufundisi naNyasha vakafamba vachibva vadzokera nedivi rekugomo. Ndipo pakaerekana Nyasha ati handei nekwaMuvhangeri Sheshe. Amai Mufundisi havana kuita nharo vakangotevedzera zvavakanga vaudzwa.
Vaviri vakafamba apo vasina kutora nguva kusvika pamba pavo. Vakasvika nekuisa munamato vasina kumbotaura nemunhu. Vachipedza kunamata vakabva vagara zvavo kuti vambokurukura.
Nyasha ndipo paakatanga kutaura zvaakanga aona paakazoti handei nekwaMuvhangeri. Akanga aona Muvhangeri Sheshe vachityaira moto vakananga kubasa. Ndipo paakaona museve uchipfurwa asi haana kuona kwavakanga vabva. Paakazoudza Mai Mufundisi kuti handei kumba kwaMuvhangeri akanga atoona museve vakatarisana nemota.
Zvakanga zvanaka kuti musi uyu vakanga vasina kuenda kubasa zvimwe vaizodzoka varemara kana kutorerwa hupenyu zvachose.
 

Muvhangeri Sheshe vakabva varairwa kunzi vaifanirwa kutenderera mota yavo kuseni kwega kwega vachinamata vasati vatanga rwendo. Izvi zvaiitira kuti vagare vachengetedzwa parwendo rwavo pavanenge wava mumugwagwa.
Amai Muvhangeri vakazonzi vambomira kufamba famba nekuti vakanga vakateiwa kuti pavanongobuda vosangana netsaona inovaremadza. Nyasha naamai Mufundisi vakazobva apa vachitora divi rekugomo.
Vachifamba kudaro pakabva papinda meseji pafoni paNyasha. NdiAmai vake vaibvunza kuti akanga aripi nekuti vakanga vakapedzisira kumuona achibuda mukereke.
Akabva avaudza kuti akanga akachengetedzeka aitova munzira naamai Mufundisi kuenda kugomo. Amai Nyasha vakatomboshamisika kunzwa kuti akanga aina amai Mufundisi. Vakazongovimbisa kuti vaizouya nechikafu kugomo ikoko.
Mai Mufundisi naNyasha vakafambisa vakananga kugomo kuya apa zuva rakanga ravapedyo nekunorereka. Vakasvika pavaikwira napo mugomo vachibva vambozorora mbijana. Pavakanga wava kusimuka ndipo pakacheuka Nyasha anzwa mutsindo kumashure kwake. Akashamisika kuona zinyoka rakanga rakatosimudza musoro.
 

Nyasha akabva audzwa munzeve make kuti muvengi akanga avagarira panzira. Nyoka iya yakasvipa mate yakananga kumeso kwaNyasha asi akatadza kusvika. Yakaedza kuna amai Mufundisi haana kusvika zvekare. Payakaona kuti yakundikana zvekupfira mate yakanga yavakuda zvekuruma.
Nyasha akangoerekana ashevedzera kuti moto akainongedza nechigunwe. Nyoka iya yakabva yashaya simba rekufamba ichiuya kwakanga kumire vazodziwa waMwari. Payakaona kuti yakundikana yakabva yatanga kufamba ichidzokera kwayakanga yabva nako.
Mai Mufundisi naNyasha vakazopedzisa rwendo rwavo apo vairumbidza musiki nekuvarwira. Husiku uhwu vakazorara vachiimba nekurumbidza vachiti vakagara gara vonamata.
Nekunerimwe divi Steve akanga ari mumba make achitambisa computer yake. Ndipo paakafunga tsoro yaizoita kuti panyika pave nenzara. Akabva afunga tsoro yekuti kana paizoita mafashamo chikafu chaizokukurwa nyika yoshaya zvibereko. Kune nzvimbo dzinenge dzisina kusvika mafashamo aizotumira mhepo yodzura zvirimwa zvese nyika yosara isina zvirimwa. Akabva aenda kunotora tsvimbo yake yaaishandisa kana afunga kuita basa iri.
 

Akabuda panze achibva asimudza tsvimbo yake achitaura mashoko echirudzi chaisanzwikwa.
Akatenderedza tsvimbo iya achibva ainongedza divi reMozambique rinova ndiro raiva negungwa.
Pasina nguva nhau dzakanga dzava kutotenderera mumaredhiyo nemaTV kuti vanhu vakanga varikufa nemafashamo. Chikafu chakanga chakukurwa zvekusara minda isina chinhu uye dzimba dzakasara dzine nzara.
Manheru aya Steve akarara avakuziva kuti akanga abudirira chidanho chimwechete. Akanyatsorara hope dzehumambo achiziva kuti nyika yakanga yava kuzouya mumaoko avo. Husiku hwakanga hwakareba asi kunze kwakasvika pakuedza.
Steve akamuka achivhura paTv apo ainzwa kuti mafashamo akanga aparadza nzvimbo zhinji pamwe nezvirimwa zvakawanda. Munyika dzakakomberedza makanga motarisirwa kuita nzara uye vatungamiri vakanga vachiri kubatanidza kuti voitasei vanhu vararame.
Steve akazofunga zvekutumira mhepo yobva yapedzisa mbesa dzakanga dzararama dzacho. Ndipo paakabuda panze achibva anhonga ivhu muchivanze chake.
Akangorikandira mudenga mhepo ichibva yatouya.
 

CHAPTER 42 DISASTER STRIKES
Mhepo yakavhuvhuta zvekuda kutoparadza chaiko. Vakanga usiri mwedzi waNyamavhuvhu asi maitiro aiita mhepo yacho akanga akatooma. Yaiti ikarova nzvimbo dzine zvirimwa paisara pakaita kunge pasina kumbobvira padyarwa.
Paakaona zvadai Steve akabva apinda hake mumba. Akatanga kuona hake Tv apo nyaya yemafashamo yakanga ichiri kunetsa. Vanhu vazhinji vakanga wava kuchema chikafu sezvo chakanga chaeredzwa nemafashamo uye zvirimwa zvakanga zvakukurwa.
Akazotanga kuona hake firimu akamirira kuenda kumvura. Ndiko kwaaizovaudza paakanga ava apo vakanga wava pedyo nekuisa hutungamiri hwenyika mumaoko avo.
Nguva dzakafamba apo akaona dzekunanga kumvura dzakwana. Sezvo kwakanga kuine mafashamo munzvimbo yaakanga achida kuenda nayo akabva aronga rimwe zano raimusvitsa ikoko. Akangopfugama akakotamisa uso hwake achitaura mutauro usinganzwike. Pakarepo akabva anyangarika.
 

Akatozoona wava pasi pamvura hurukuro dzichibva dzatotanga. Ndipo pavakanga wavakuronga kuti zvofamba sei kunze kwavakanga vari. Vana Hazel vakapinda mudariro vachitaura mafambiro avakanga vaita mumazuva apfuura.
"Kwamakatituma uko Mufundisi takambozama kubata basa. Elder Mududu ndakamutumira Lisa akadzoka achindiudza kuti asiya vaita tsaona uye mota yacha yaparara zvinopisa tsitsi. Millicent akaendawo akanorova Mwana waElder Marwei pamwe nemudzimai akangosiya ari manyama amire nerongo. Kutaura kuno handifunge kuti vanhu iwavo vachiri vapenyu." Akataura Hazel apo aifunga kuti vanhu vakarwiswa vakasara vakafa.
"Muvhangeri Sheshe takaedza kuvarindira munzira asi takavashaya. Patakaenda kumba kwavo takashaya nzira asi ndakazokwanisa kuona amai Mufundisi naNyasha vachibuda ipapo. Ava ndivo vandaida saka ndakanovagarira kunzira inokwira mugomo mavaienda. Ndakaedza kuvarwisa nepavanogona asi ndakakundikana ndicho chokwadi. Asi zvichakadaro ndichavaendera zvekare nekuti tsuro haizombopona murutsva kaviri." Akataura Hazel achiudza vamwe vake mafambiro aakanga aita. Chaimubata inyaya yekuti vanhu vake vaaida aitadza kuvabata.
 

Steve akazopindawo mudariro achitaura paakanga ava nebasa rake. Chiso chake chakanga chakafara zvekuti vaiti igudo ranhonga roro mubani.
"Ini kudivi kwangu kurikufamba zvakanaka, ndakarova nyika nemafashamo kutaura kuno haasati apera.
Ndakazosimudza mhepo zvekare iyo yakabva yapedzisa zvakanga zvasiiwa nemafashamo. Kutaura kuno hutongi hwenyika hwatova pedyo neni. Mirai muone kuti hazvina nguva zvinhu zvandiri kutaura izvi." Akataura Steve vanhu vachibva vaombera maoko.
Ndicho chinhu chikuru chaidiwa naVicky saka akabva atora Steve kuti adzike naye pasi pasi pemvura. Ndipo paakamusimbisa masimba ake kuti agogona kusvika paakanga achida kusvika. Hazel akazosimbiswawo apo akanzi achingobva mumvura aifanirwa kunorwisa amai Mufundisi naNyasha.
Vicky akamusimbisa achimuudza kuti aisafanirwa kukundikana sezvo aiva mutevedzeri vake. Kuva mutevedzeri wemukuru wemasimba zvaitoreva kuti aiva nesimba rakawanda kudarika wakanga varipo pasi pemvura apa. Akabva arairwa kuti aizofanirwa kuenda kuhondo iyi naLisa naMillicent havaizokundwa vari vatatu kudaro. Steve akazorairwa kuti kana nguva yacho yaizokwana aizoenda naMufundisi kuhofisi dzenyika.
Ndivo vaiziva maendero avaizoita.
 

Vanhu vakazonyangarika vachidzokera munzvimbo dzavaizoraramira. Mumwe nemumwe akanga avakuziva kwaainanga uye basa raaizoita Hazel haana kuda kusvika kumba asati apedza basa rake. Akabva atobatana nevasikana vake.
Amai Mufundisi vakanga vachitoimba zvavo vari mugomo naNyasha. Ndipo pavakatanga kuoneswa rima guru raibva nechekudivi remugwagwa mukuru vainanga Harare. Havana chavakataura vakangobata Nyasha ruoko vachibva vatanga kuimba kambo kekuti ndibate ruoko.
Vari pakuimba kudaro ndipo pavakaona varume vakanga vakapfeka zvichena vachitenderera mugomo mavakanga vari. Nyasha aitoonawo mabhiza nengoro dzehondo zvakanga zvagadzirira kurwa. Pasina nguva ndipo pavakaona mombe nhatu dzichitenderera mugomo umu. Mugomo umu maisaonekwa mombe saka idzi kakanga kari kekutanga kudziona.
Mai Mufundisi vakabva vanzwa inzwi richivataurira kuti mhandu dzenyu dzasvika asi imi murikuona semombe. Inzwi riya rakabva raenderera mberi richiti hondo dzamaona ndidzo dzichabata basa imi makatarira. Amai Mufundisi naNyasha vakabva vadzikama havo vachibva vatotanga kuimba nenzwi riri pamusoro.
 

CHAPTER 43 DISASTER CONTINUES
Panguva yavaiimba mombe dziya dzakaramba dzakatarira. Vaviri ava vakawedzera kukwidza manzwi avo vachiimba kambo kavo vakamirira kuona hondo ichirwiwa.
Mombe dziya ndipo padzakatanga kufamba dzichiuya kwavari. Panguva iyoyo mombe dziya dzaiti dzikafamba dzomira. Padzaimira vaiona dzakavharirwa nemauto edenga. Imwe yacho yakanga iri hombe pane dzese yakambodzokera kumashure apo yakadzoka yakateya nyanga ichiti zvimwe ingangorwisa ikakunda.
Yakasvikogumira payakanga yambogumira apo yaishaya nzira yekuenda mberi. Mumwe wevarwi wedenga ndiye akazonongedza ruoko rwake kumombe dziya rwuchibva rwaburitsa moto.
Mombe dzakaita nguva dzichipiswa nemoto kuti dzitize zvairamba. Varume wezvichena vaye vakazenge vanongedzera maoko avo ikoko achibudawo moto uyo vaipisa mombe dziya. Mai Mufundisi naNyasha vakazoshamisika vachiona mombe dziya dzichishanduka kuita vanhu.
 

"Ko sisi Hazel ndimi zvenyu, ko manga mauya kuzotirwisa maiti munokunda here?" NdiNyasha aitaura achishevedzera kuna Hazel uyo akanga akamira nechekure.
"Ko iwe Hazel vakambomuonepi wavabva vaziva kudaro. Pane kwamakambosangana here kana kuti vafemerwa." Vakabvunza amai Mufundisi vachishamisika nemaziviro akanga aita Nyasha mhandu yavo iyi.
"Hazel ndisisi wekukereke, patakaenda kucrusade paya akaimba zvinonwisa mvura kungoti ndakanga ndisati ndaziva nezvake asi ndava kutozviona izvozvi kuti imhandu." Akataura Nyasha apa zvese izvi zvaiva munzeve dzaHazel. Vamwe vasikana wacho vakanga varipo vakanga vakambovaona kukereke zvekarw asi hapana aiziva mazita avo.
Vatatu ava vakangofuratira vachibva vaenda. Nyasha naamai Mufundisi vakabva vapfugama kuti vamborumbidza musiki. Nyasha akabva aoneswa achifamba mugwenga achiona musina kana chirimwa chaivamo. Akaramba achifamba mugwenga muya achiedza kubatanidza kuti aitsvagei munzvimbo yakadaro. Nzvimbo yacho yaipisa asi zvekutomboda kuenda pamumvuri asi makanga musina miti. Ndipo paanotanga kuudzwa munzeve dzake.
 

"Mwana wangu zvavaona izvi matambudziko atarisana nenyika. Vanhu vachafa nenzara nyika dzakapoteredza zvichasvika pakuunganidza vatungamiri wenyika vachironga kuti voitasei. Mwana wangu musazotya henyu nekuti ndinenge ndinemi panguva iyoyo." Nyasha akambonyarara kunamata achiteerera mashoko aya.
Inzwi riya rakabva raenderera mberi.
"Chikafu chichavapo asi ndapota musazochitora. Vazhinji vachadya chikafu ichi vachapinda muhumambo hwekumadokero vasingazivi uye vamwe ndiwo vachafa. Kereke ichachinjwa manamatiro uye vanhu vachanamatiswa chavasingazivi nechisimba nekuti humambo hwenyika ino hunenge hwava mumaoko evakaipa. Uchengetedze mashoko iwayo ugorangarira kana zvoitika." Inzwi riya raitaura munzeve maNyasha rakabva ranyarara apo akazoona asisiri mugwenga maanga ambori.
Vakapedza munamato wavo vachibva vagara kuti vambokurukura. Nyasha akabva audza amai Mufundisi zvaakanga aona uye zvese zvaakanga anzwa.
Vakasimbisana kuti havaizokundwa nerima iwo vachinamata Mwari mupenyu. Chakanga chobata amai Mufundisi inyaya yekuti vana wavo vaizodyiswa chikafu chakadaro nababa wavo. Inzwi rakabva rataura munzeve dzavo kuti nguva yekuvatora ichakwana.
 

Mazuva akatanga kufamba kubva zvakanga zvaitika mafashamo nemhepo panyika. Vanhu vakatanga kuchema nenzara pasi rose nekuti zvirimwa zvakanga zvaeredzwa pamwe nekutakurwa nemhepo. Mudzimba umu rakanga rangova bopoto nekuda kwenzara.
Zvakabva zvawedzera kushaikwa kwemari munyika zvekuti nyangwe vapfumi vakanga wavakudya nhoko dzezvironda. Izvi zvakaita kuti vatungamiri wenyika dzakapoteredza vaite musangano sezvo nyika dzakanga dzasvika pasina kunaka. Steve akanga akatarira TV yake achiona musangano wevatungamiri wenyika uyo vaiitwa paTv vanhu wese vachiona.
Akasekerera achiona kuti zvakanga zvavakuenda negwara raaida chairo. Akangonotora tsvimbo yake nengowani yake yegoridhe achibva adzoka paTv. Apa akanga agadzirira kupedza basa rake sezvo akanga achine mukana.
Akangonongedza tsvimbo yake kutv achitaura mashoko emutauro usinganzwiki. Akaramba achitaura apo akaona vanhu vaya vaibuda patv vanyarara vachiratidza kuti varikuteerera mashoko ake aakanga achitaura.
Akazosimudza tsvimbo yake achibva atswinzwinya akatarisa kwaiva netv. Panguva iyoyo akanzwa kunge atakurwa nemhepo. Akazovhura maziso achiona ari pakati pevatungamiri wenyika.
 

CHAPTER 44 ACCESS GRANTED
Steve zvaakaona agara pakati pevakuru wenyika akabva amirira kunzwa zvavaizotaura. Nechemumoyo aiziva hake kuti akanga atokunda kupinda muhutongi hwenyika. Pakamboramba paine runyararo apo mumwe wevakuru vakanga vakagara apa akabva ashama muromo kuti ataure.
"Taura tinzwe chikomana, unokwanisa kubatsira nyika here nekuti isu tapererwa. Kutaura kuno tangogara hedu musangano sevatungamiri wenyika asi hapana chirikubuda." Mukuru uya akabva anyarara apo vamwe wese vakabva vateya nzeve kuti vanzwe kuti paizouya mhinduro yakaitasei. Izvo zviso zvacho zvevakuru vakuru zvakanga zvatopusa nekuda kwenzara.
"Vakuru vangu nyaya yenyu idiki kana ichinge yapinda mumaoko angu. Ini nzvimbo yandinobva haina matambudziko ine maguta akapfuurikidza. Nyaya iripo ndeyekuwirirana chete isu tobva tabatsira nyika. Zvese zvingadiwa panyika zvinowanikwa kwandinobva." Akataura Steve achipindura vakuru vaya vakanga vakateya nzeve.
 

Pakamboita runyararo vakuru wese vakanga vari mumusangano uyu vachifunga zvakadzama. Mumwe nemumwe aizvobvunza mubvunzo mupfungwa dzavo. Ko zvaanoti kwandinobva iye anombobvepi muchinda uyu? Mimwe mibvunzo yaiva mumisoro yevamwe. Ko zvaanoti inyaya yekuwirirana arikurevei? Ipfungwa dzaingopishanawo mumisoro yevamwe.
Runyararo rwakamboramba rwuripo apo paishaya anopindura mashoko aSteve. Vakambozevezerama zvishoma mukuru uya wekumbotaura naSteve achibva azoshama muromo kuti ataure.
"Ipapo panzwika changamire, tazvinzwa kuti kwamunobva kune maguta zvichireva kuti nyika dzose dzakapoteredza dzinokwanisa kuguta kuburikidza nemi. Izvozvo tinozvitenda uye tinovimba kuti muchabatsira nyika. Mubvunzo uri pamati zvinoda kuwirirana mobva mabatsira nyika, tinenge tichiwirirana panezvipi tigoona kuti tingafambe tese here." Muchinda uya akazopedza kutaura Steve atogadzirira.
"Nyaya iripo ndeyekuti munongotipawo mugove muhutungamiri hwenyika. Kana mukatitendera kuva nemi muhutongi hwenyika muchaona kuti zvinhu zvichafamba mushe uye vanhu vachasunungurwa." Akataura Steve achibva amirira kunzwa kuti aizopindurwa kutii.
 

Vakambotarisana kwekanguva vachishaya kuti kana zvadai poitwa sei. Zvinhu zvairema kuti hutungamiri hwongoenda kumunhu angosvika asina kuhushandira. Ipapo panga pakaoma asi nzara yakanga yarumawo zvekare. Vakuru vakuru vakadikitira misoro vachiedza kifunga kuti vobvuma here kana kuti vorega.
Mumwe wevatungamiri ava ndiye akazoti zvakanga zvisina mhosva sevanhu vakanga vachibatsirwa.
Vaizoronga kuti muchinda uyu vaizomugadzirira chigaro chitsva chaizova pamusoro pezvigaro zvese.
Aizoitwa Great President kureva kuti vatungamiri wese wenyika vaizova pasi pake. Mumwe nemumwe aizotungamira munyika make asi uyu aizotonga nyika dzese. Zvekuti vakanga wava pasi pake zvaisava nemhosva chikuru kwaiva kubatsirika nekuti nyika yakanga yava parumananzombe.
Vapedza kutaurirana vakazopira nyaya kuna Steve vachimuudza zvavakanga varonga. Steve akaita kunge achabata denga achinzwa mashoko aya. Chigaro chaaizowana ichi chaibva chamupa masimba ekuti kana iwo vakuru wenyika vaizoteerera zvaanotaura.
Musangano vakazoenderera mberi apo Steve akabva asainiswa gwaro raitaura kuti akanga ava mutungamiri wenyika dzese.
 

Musangano vakazopera apo Steve akavimbisa kuti paizoitwa mabiko ekugadzwa kwake. Ndipo paaizouya nevamwe vake vaakanga ainawo muchirongwa chake avo vakabva vavimbiswa kupihwa zvigaro muhutungamiri. Zvichipera izvozvo Steve akazoita zvekunyangarika achidzoka paakanga akagara nguva dzaaiona tv.
Chikamu chikuru chakanga chapfuura kwakanga kwasara kuzadzisa chete. Iri shoko rekubudirira akanga atononokerwa nekurisvitsa kune vamwe vake.
Akazomirira husiku apo aizoenda kumvura. Sezvineiwo nguva dzekumvura dzakabva dzakwana apo aizoenda kunovaudza nhau inofadza. Akangotswinzwinya akagara pasofa rake achibva atosimuka achienda mumhepo.
Akazosvinura achiona ava pasi pemvura.
Hazel ndiye akatanga kupinda mudariro achichema chema nekwaakanga atumwa. Akaudza mukuru vake kuti mukana wekusvika pavanhu vake aushaiwa nekuti vanga vakakombwa nehondo huru. Vakazosimbisana kuti vaizopagadzira asi panguva iyi vakanga wava kumboona nezvehumambo hwenyika.
Ndipo pakabva papinda Steve nenyaya yake mudariro apo aitaura mafambiro aakanga aita. Nguva iyi vanhu wese vakanga vateya nzeve.
 

CHAPTER 45
ENJOYING THE NEW KINGDOM
"Hama dzadiwa muchindiona kudai ndinenyaya yakanaka, hurongwa hwedu hwese hwafamba mushe uye tirikupfuurira mberi kubva patava izvozvi. Humambo hwenyika hwatanga tichida hwava mumaoko edu uye hapana achahutora." Steve achipedza kutaura mashoko aya panomboita ruzha rwekuombera vanhu vachifarira basa rakanga rabatwa.
"Basa ravabata iguru mwana wangu zvazvadai voramba uchibata basa kuti humambo husabve mumaoko edu, chiramba vakatsika pavatsika ipapo toenderera mberi takadaro." Akadaro Vicky achikorokotedza Steve.
Akazovataurira mafambiro aakanga aita kuti asvike pakuonana nevakuru wenyika. Akabva avaudza zvese zvavakanga vanyorerana nechigaro chaakanga apihwa. Akanga angomirira kunogadzwa chete.
Zvese izvi kwakanga kwava kuzadzisa asi humambo hwakanga hwatopinda mumaoko avo. Pakazoitwa mabiko pasi pemvura apa vanhu vachifarira humambo hwakanga hwauya. Paidyiwa nekunwiwa vanhu vachiita waini yakudira pasi.
 

Steve akazonzi aifanirwa kutora Mufundisi kuti vagobatsira pakugadza humambo musi uyu. Aizotorawo Jonhson naBrighton pamwe naFrank vaizofamba vakamuchenhetedza musi uyu. Hazel aizovapowo kuitira waya vane shavi rekuda kudeurwa ropa ravo. Aizenge aina Millicent naLisa vake.
Vicky aizongoshanyawo kuti aone zvichiitika hapana hake basa raaizobata ikoko. Vapedza kuwirirana wese vakabva vanyangarika vachidzokera kunzvimbo dzavanogara.
Mazuva akaramba achifamba apo vakuru wenyika vakaona zvakakodzera kukasika kuronga mutambo wekugadza mutungamiri mutsva wenyika. Nenzara yakanga yarova panyika zvaitoda kuti vakasike kupa vane chikafu chinzvimbo chavo izvo zvaizounza maguta. Zuva racho rakabva ratorongwa vachibva vazivisa Steve. Ndiye akazounza chikafu chese chaizodyiwa pamutambo uyu sezvo nyika yakanga yaomerwa.
Zuva racho parakasvika kwakanga kusingadanwe anonzwa. Vanhu vakanga vari mavhu nemarara vachibva kunyika dzakasiyana siyana kuti vaone mutungamiri mutsva achigadzwa. Zvese izvi zvaifadza vanhu sezvo vakanga vaudzwa kuti ndiye mutungamiri aizogutisa nyika.
 

Mutambo vakatanga kuseni apo Steve akasvika nechikwata chake vachiburuka mumota. Mota dzacho dzaiva apa hapana kana dzevatungamiri wenyika dzaienderana nadzo. Vanhu ndiwo vaiita ruzha rwemafaro vachiona mukuru uyu achifamba pajira dzvuku achifamba nepakati pavanhu.
Aifamba hake zvinyoro nyoro semunhu akanga ava muridzi wenyika dzese. Nenguva isipi akanga amira kumberi kwevanhu wese avo vakatanga kuridza mhururu nemiridzo. Zvinhu zvaifadza panguva iyi nekuti vanhu vakanga vapererwa. Chaifadza ndechekuti zvinhu zvakanga zvava kuzovanakira. Mukana vakabva vazopihwa kuna Mufundisi Mazondo avo vaizobata basa rekugadza mutungamiri uyu.
"Chekutanga ndinoda kukutendai mose mauya nehuwandu hwenyu kuti muzoona kugadzwa kwemutungamiri wenyu mutsva. Shoko rinotaura kuti chimwe nechimwe chine nguva yacho yachakatarirwa nashe. Kune nguva yekudyara kune nguva yekukohwa, zvese izvi hausi hurongwa hwemunhu wenyama asi zvinorongwa newekumusoro. Ndinofara ndichiona chiitiko chiripano chinofadza kudai. Nyika yanga yaoma asi Mwari vamutsa mumwe mubatsiri kuti agova mukuru pakati pedu." Panguva iyi vanhu vakaombera vachinzwa mashomo aMufundisi.
 

"Ndinotenda nemukana wandapihwa wekuti ndimbotaura zvishoma ndisati ndabata basa rinoda kubatwa pano. Zvandavakuita parizvino ndinoda kutenderera vakuru wese wenyika ndichivazodza kuti vagopihwa huchenjeri hwekushandisa kana zvichinge zvavaremera." Panguva iyi Mufundisi Mazondo vakabva vatanga kutenderera vachizora vatungamiri wese wenyika mafuta pahuma ayo ainhuwirira. Vachipedza vakabva vauya pana Steve vachibva vamuzora zvekare.
"Nguva iya yamanga makamirira yakwana zvino. Ndiyo nguva yatava kugadza mambo wemadzimambo uyo achange ari pamusoro pemadzimambo ese." Mufundisi vanotaura apo Steve akanga agariswa pachigaro chegoridhe chinopenya. Mumusoro make akanga akapfeka ngowani yeumambo yegoridhe. Mufundisi vakabva vamubatisa tsvimbo yavo iya vachimuraira kuti aisimudze mudenga.
Panguva iyoyo kunze kwakashanduka kuita husiku kuchibva kwatanga kupenya kunge kurikuda kunaya. Pava paya kunze kwakazodzaka zvekare kuita zvakwakanga kuri pakutanga.
"Zvamaona izvi zvinoreva kuti humambo hwemwanakomana hwatambirwa." Mufundisi pavanotaura mashoko aya vanhu vakabva vaita ruzha rwakapfuurikidza rwemufaro.
 

CHAPTER 46
NEW WORLD ORDER
Chakava chiitiko chinofadza kuva nemutungamiri mutsva. Jonhson naBrighton pamwe naFrank ndiwo vakazogadzwa sevachengeti wemutungamiri wenyika. Ndiwo vaizofamba naye kwese kwaanoenda.
Hazel akazopihwawo chinzvimbo apo aizova secretary wehurumende itsva yakanga yavapo iyi.zvese izvi zvichipera vanhu vakabva vaparara. Mazuva akatanga kufamba munyika muchibva maita shanduko. Chikafu chakatanga kuwanikwa kwese kwese uye mari yakanga isisanetse.
Zita raPresident Steve ndiro rakanga rava kugara riri pamiromo yevanhu wese. Vamwe vaiti ane moyo murefu murume uyu vamwe vachimurumbidza kuti ingirozi yakanga yabva kuna baba.
Zvese zvakanga zvaparadzwa nemvura nemhepo zvakatanga kuvakwa patsva pasina muripo. Zvese izvi zvaifadza waruzhinji avo vakabva vafunga zvekuenda kukereke yaMufundisi Mazondo. Kereke yacho yakanga yazoita mapazi kumativi mana nenyika dzakapoteredza.
 

Sezvo mazuva aifamba simbi yakanga yavakuda kurohwa isati yapora. Vanhu vakanga wava kufanirwa kuziviswa chokwadi chezvakanga zviripo zvaizoita kuti varambe vachidya vachiguta. Yakanga yava nguva yekubudirana pachena anenge asingade obva awonekana nenyika apo aizosiiwa ari kumarinda.
Pasi pemvura huwandu hwevanhu hwakanga hwakwira saka vakanga wava nemauta avo aingoshevedzwa kana paine aita nharo. Nguva zhinji mauto aya aisara pasi pemvura nekuti vakaona vanhu vaibva vanzwa kuda ropa. Vanhu vakanga vakaungana vachimirira kunzwa zvaida kutaura mutungamiri wenyika Steve.
"Ndinoda kukutendai mose kunyanya vatungamiri wenyika dzino vakanditendera kuti ndive zvandiri. Zvinhu zvakaoma kupihwa mvumo yakadaro asi imi makandipa mukati batsira nyika sezvavakatumwa." Pakaita maungira ekufara apo vanhu vainzwa inzwi remurume uyu kekutanga kubva paakagadzwa.
"Nyaya yandinayo muzuva ranhasi ndeyekuti kwandinobva kunova ndiko kunobva maguta kune vakuru wedu vatinonamata. Vakuru vatinonamata ava vanoda kuramba vachinamatwa uye vanofara kwazvo zvinozoita kuti varambe vachitipa chikafu." Mashoko aya akaita kuti pamboita runyararo vanhu vachingotarisana.
 

"Zvingaita sezvakuvhundutsai hazvo asi ino inguva yekutaurirana chokwadi. Wedu vatinonamata anonzi THE GREAT MARINE KING anova ndiye anesimba rinokunda vaMwari wese. Ndiye anotiwanisa chikafu chese chatinodya ichi uye akatizivisa kuti anoda kunamatwa nemunhu wese anorarama panyika pano." Vanhu vakaramba vakanyarara pasina aikwanisa kupindura.
"Musavhunduka zvenyu muchinzwa nezvamwari wedu batataura nezvake uyu. Kana mukamunamata achakukomborerai uye nyika yose ichafarwa nehupfumi hwakapfuurikidza huchavapo. Zvava kwatiri kuzvitambira kana kusazvitambira asi ndizvo zviripo.
Vanhu tichanga tava kunamata kereke imwechete uye hakuna mumwe achatenderwa kumutsa imwe kereke." Panguva iyi pakanzwikwa mahon'era kureva kuti pane vanhu vaipesana nazvo.
"Ndanzwa mahon'era mukati menyu kureva kuti pane vanopesana nazvo, izvi zvinoreva kuti vanoda kuzviita vakuru kudarika vamwari wedu vanotipa hupfumi nechikafu. Kana varipo vanopikisa zvandataura ngavagare vazvipatsanura mukati mevamwe tivaone." Akataura Steve achibva amirira kuona kuti ndevapi vanhu vacho. Vanhu vakatanga kuzvipatsanura mukati mevamwe nehuwandu hwavo.
 

Steve akazobvunza kuti sei vakanga vapokana nezvaaitaura vachibva vamupindura kuti vaizodana zita reMwanakomana chete. Uyezve vakanga vasina basa nechikafu nekuti dumbu rakanzi ndere zvekudya nezvekudya ndezvedumbu asi Mwari vachaparadza zvese pazuva rekuguma. Steve akazotaura kekupedzisira achiti azvipira hake kufa panguva ino nekuda kusateerera zvandinotaura ngaarambe ari kudivi ikoko.
Vamwe pavakanzwa zvekufa vakabva vachinja moyo. Ndiwo vakazoerekana kwaiva nechaunga chairumbidza Steve. Vamwe vakasara vakamira vakanga vaine hushingi hwekufira Kristu mwanakomana waMwari.
Panguva iyi Steve akabva asimudza tsvimbo yaaiva nayo mumaoko iri nzira yekushevedza mauto ake.
Nenguva isipi nzvimbo iyi yakanga yatokombwa nevarume vakanga vakapfeka zvitema vakavhara kumeso. Mumaoko vakanga vakabata mapanga aipenya achicheka nemativi ese. Izvi zvakaita kuti huwangu hwavakanga vasarudza kufira Mwari mupenyu huderere apo vamwe vakazvitsaura zvekare vachipinda muchaunga. Mauto akazopihwa mvumo achibva atanga kubata basa vanhu vakatarisa. Aingorova mutsipa nebanga kamwechete musoro vobva vadonha. Pakava nemhere mhere panguva iyi vanhu vachiona ropa.
 

CHAPTER 47 FIGHT BEGINS
Izvi zvakaita kuti vanhu vapete miswe vachitya kutorerwa hupenyu hwavo. Vaichekwa misoro vakazotakurwa nemisoro yavo vachibva vaendwa navo kunoraswa. Steve akazoendererawo mberi apo mauto aya akanga azodzokera.
"Ndizvo zvatinoita izvozvo kune vanenge vasingateereri. Unozvidemba kuti chandazviirira vasiya sadza.
Ndinoenderera mberi ndichiti mwari wedu uyu wandataura nezvake avakunamatwa zviri pamutemo. Tichatuma vanhu vachafamba vachiisa zvidhindo zvinoratidza kuti ndiye mwari waunonamata uye hapana anofanirwa kupokana nazvo. Anenge apokana nazvo rufu rwunomushanyira." Pakataurwa mashoko aya hapana akadaira kana kupikisa. Steve akazoenderera mberi nemashoko ekupedzisira.
"Chekupedzisira ndinoda kutenda nenguva yamandipa semutungamiri wenyu. Ndinoti mugova nenguva yakanaka." Akataura achibva atobva pastage paakanga akamira. Hapana akakwanisa kuona kuti akazofamba sei.
 

Vanhu vakazoparara wava kuenda kunzvimbo dzavanoraramira. Vamwe ndivo vaikurukura pamusoro pechiitiko chakanga chaitika. Vamwe vakanga vasina kufara nechiitiko ichi asi kuti vataure zvairema. Vaitya kuitya kanyama zvavakanga vaona zvichiitwa vamwe.
Mazuva akafamba zvinhu zvichingochinja mazuva ese. Mukereke makanga mavakutyisa kupikisa zvinenge zvataurwa nekuti rufu rwakanga rwavakugara pedyo.
Vaiti uchipinda pamusuwo vaiona pakamira varume wechiuto vakaita sevaya wekuuraya vanhu pamusangano. Ava vakanga vazosiyana pakuti vakanga vasina hasha dzakanyanya sewekuuraya vanhu vaya.
Amai Mufundisi naNyasha vaingoshumira mazuva ese vachirumbidza Mwari mupenyu. Zvavaizooneswa mumaziso avo ndizvo zvaivarwadza kusvika pakuzvibvuza kuti zvichapera here.
Mumwe musi vakanga vakagara vachibva vatanga kuoneswa vana wavo. Vakaoneswa vachipihwa chikafu chiya chakanga chabva pasi pegungwa apo vakabva vatanga kuchema. Zvinhu zvaivarwadza kuona mwana wavo wekubereka achipihwa mhando yechikafu chakanga chabva pasi pemvura ichi. Zvaiva nani kuti afe nenzara pane kudya chikafu ichi. Vakabva vatanga kunzwa kutaura munzeve dzavo.
 

"Muranda washe usachema zvako uchiona zviri pameso ako izvo, iyi inyaya diki nhasi chaiye vana vako uchanovatora ugouya navo pano. Ko vambenge vaona here zvaita nyika nekereke?" Pakarepo amai Mufundisi vakatanga kuona zvese zvakanga zvichiitika munyika nemanamatirwo akanga avakuitwa mukereke.
Vakatarisana naNyasha uyo aitoererawo misodzi. Vakashaya kuti aichemei vachibva vamubvunza. Ndipo pavakaziva kuti akanga achiona zvavakanga vachionawo. Vakazotanga kuona Mukoma Kudzi avo vakanga vachiri muchipatara kubva pavakaita tsaona nebhazi. Inzwi rakabva rauya munzeve dzavo richitaura.
"Muchinda waurikuona uyu ndakamusarudza kuti andishumire asi achiri pakumanikidzwa. Ruoko rwake ndirwo rwandakasarudza kuti rwubatsirane nemi pakusunungura kereke uye kudzoka kwake kuchaita kuti kereke idzoke panzvimbo. Shoko riripo nderekuti pfugamai mumunamatire nekuti aripedyo nekurwiswa nehondi yepasi pemvura. Arikuzivikanwa kuti ndiye achaponesa nyika saka vachazoda kumuuraya." Amai Mufundisi vachinzwa mashoko aya vakangobatana maoko naNyasha vachibva vatanga kunamata.
Zuva iri vakazodzika gomo vachibva vaenda kunotora vana wavo sezvo baba vacho vakanga vabuda. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatodzoka kugomo.
 

Vakatanga kunamata apo vakanga varairwa kunzi vanamate pamusoro pevana wavo. Vana vakatanga kuzvongonyoka kuita kunge nyoka vachiridza mhere. Amai Mufundisi naNyasha vakabva vatowedzera minamato yacho. Pava paya ndipo pakazorutsa vana ava zvinhu zvitema zvakatadza kuzivikanwa kuti zvaiva zvii.
Vakazoenderera mberi neminamato yavo apo vakanga wavakurumbidza Mwari mupenyu. Mazuva ose ainetsa chikafu paiuya njiva yakatakura tswanda ichisiira vana amai Mufundisi. Havana kumbobvira vashaya chikafu mazuva ese aya.
Kubva zvakanga zvapindawo mukoma Kudzi muchipatara havana kuzoziva zvairongwa panyika. Vakanga vachingorapwa vachiziva kuti nerimwe zuva vachazobuda. Mazuva akafamba apo vanhu vaiisa zvidhindo vakanga wavakufamba nemuzvipatara.
Vakasvika pachipatara pakanga paina Mukoma Kudzi vachibva vatanga kubaya varwere.
Mukoma Kudzi avo vakanga vakatyoka gumbo hameno kuti vakarivanepi simba. Vakangokwanisa kusimuka vachibva vafamba vachibuda mukamuri ravakanga vachirapirwa.
 

CHAPTER 48 FIGHTING CONTINUES
Pasina nguva mukoma Kudzi vabuda mumamuri mavairapirwa pakabva papinda vanhu vaviri murume nemukadzi. Vakatanga kudhinda varwere wese vakanga vari mukamuri umu apo Mukoma Kudzi vaiterera zvavaitaura.
Vaiti vakabaya munhu vaibva vamuudza kuti makorokoto wavakurarama muhumambo hwedu uye uchararama zvaunoda ugopora. Vamwe ndivo vaimboedza kuda kuita nharo apo vaibva vabaiwa majekiseni ekuti vafe.
Vachisvika pamubhedha vaKudzi vakambomira vachitarisa tarisa kuti vaone kwaakanga aenda. Chiremba akanga achimurapa akashamisika nekuti aimuziva akatyoka gumbo.
Panguva iyo ndipo pavakatanga kufamba vachiuya nekwakanga kwakahwanda Kudzi. Kudzi paakanzwa tsoka dzichofamba kuuya kwaari akabva atanga kufamba achienda mberi. Akazozvivharira muchimbuzi apo akanzwa vachishevedzera kuti vakanga vakamumirira pamubhedha vake.
 

Ndipo paakazongoona kumberi kwake kwakamira murume akanga akapfeka zvichena. Akatanga kuoneswa zvakanga zvichiitwa nevanhu vaya vakanga vachiisa vanhu zvidhindo. Ndipo paakazoudzwa kunzi simba ramweya mutsvene ndiro rakanga ramupa simba rekumuka raakanga asina.
Sezvo akanga akamirirwa pamubhedha vake akabva atanga kurairwa mafambiro aaizoita. Akarairwa kunzi aizopinda nemukamuri iroro uye hapana aizoita simba rekumubata. Akabva arairwa kunzi pane varwere vaviri vakanga vabaiwa majekiseni ekuti vafe asi vaifanirwa kurarama kuti simba raMwari rionekwe.
Akabva arairwa kunzi avabate musoro obva apfuura hake achienda. Aizopfuura nepamubhedha vake paakanga akamirirwa achienda sezvo akanga asisina nzvimbo umu. Nzvimbo yake yakanga yatova kumberi kwakanga kuine basa.
Muchinda uya akangonyangarika Kudzi achibva asara ega. Gumbo rake rakabva rapora zvachose akanga avakuita kunge asina kumbokuvara. Akatanga kufamba akananga kukamuri riya raakanga achirapirwa.
Zvechokwadiwo akaona akamirirwa pamubhedha vake. Akangofamba akananga nekudivi raiva nevarwere vaakana arairwa.
 

Akasvikobata misoro yevanhu vaya achibva apfuura nepaiva nemubhedha vake. Akapfuura nepakati pavanhu vaya avo vakaramba vakamira vakatarira. Chiremba vake akangokwanisa kumunongedza achiratidza vanhu vaakanga anawo kuti ndiye munhu wavakanga vakamirira.
Mumwe wevanhu vakanga vachidhinda vanhu ava akamboda kufamba kuti amudzose achibva apera simba rese. Vakazongosiyana nazvo nekuti vakanga vatoona kuti pane zvaivapo zvavaisakwanisa kukurira. Mukoma Kudzi zvavakabuda vakabva vatanga kufamba vachienda kwavaisaziva.
Vaingonzwa kunzi famba saka vaingotevedzera izvozvo. Varipakufamba vakazoerekana vasvika pamba paElder Mududu. Vachisvika apa vakatanga kuoneswa mauto achitenderera achivhima Elder ava. Munamato vakabva vatotanga apo vakazorairwa kunzi pamba paElder Mududu pakanga pachengetedzwa uye vanhu vakanga vachiisa zvidhindo vakanga vasisina simba rekusvika pamba apa.
Mukoma Kudzi havana kugara pamba apa sezvo vakanga vachinzwa kunzi havasati vapedza. Vachibuda pamba apa vakaona vanhu vakanga vakapfeka zvakafanana nevaya wavakanga vaona kuchipatara vachitsvaga kuti vopinda sei pamba paMududu.
 

Semunhu akanga aine rwendo rwake havana kumboita basa nazvo vakangofamba vachienda vakazoerekana vasvika pamba paElder Marwei vachiona paine vanhu vamwechete iwawo vachida kutopinda muchivanze.
Mukoma Kudzi vakangosimudza ruoko apo vanhu vakabva vatanga kudzungaira vachitenderera paya.
Mukoma vakabva vatorairwa kunzi zvatoringana saka vakabva vapfuurira. Vakaramba vachifamba apo vakaona vasvika pamba paMuvhangeri Sheshe.
Vakatosvika Muvhangeri vakamira nevanhu vaya vachiramba kuiswa chidhindo. Mumwe wacho akanga atoburitsa banga kuti abaye Muvhangeri naro.
Nguva idzodzo Kudzi akangodaidzira kuti nezita raJesu hauna simba pamusoro penyama yake. Panguva iyoyo banga rakabva radonha mumaoko. Vanhu vaya vakabva vabva apa vasina kuoneka vachienda.
Kudzi akasiya aita munamato achibva anzwa inzwi richiti musha uyu vakanga vachengetedzwa. Akazotanga kufamba achibva apa asingazive kwaaizonanga zvekare. Apa ndipo paakazofamba rwendo rwurefu apo munzira aingoona vanhu vachiiswa zvidhindo. Pamwe pacho ndipo paaiona vakanga vakapfeka zvitema vakavharwa kumeso. Akabva aziva kuti ndivo vakanga vari mauto ehondo. Afamba kwechinhambwe akazoona avakukwidza kuenda mugomo.
 

CHAPTER 49 CHRIST AT WORK
Akafamba chinhambwe kukwira mugomo apo akazonzwa manzwi evakadzi vaiimba. Akaramba achifamba achiswedera kwakanga kuine vakadzi vaya achingotevera mazwi avo chete. Nenguva isipi akanga avakuona vanhu vakanga vari nechekure.
Nenguva isipi akanga asvika paiva nevakadzi ava vachibva vatoshamisikawo. Aizivikanwa kunzi akanga ari muchipatara saka huvepo hwake panzvimbo iyi hwakasiya amai Mufundisi naNyasha vaine mibvunzo.
"Ko wekuchipatara makabuda riinhiko takangonzwa kunzi makapotswa nerufu." Vakabvunza amai Mufundisi vachida kunyatsonzwisisa. Vaiziva kuti muchinda uyu akanga akatyoka gumbo asi apa raitoratidza kuti rakasimba.
"NdezvaMwari izvi amai, ndangonzwa simba rekusimuka ndichibva pandanga ndakarara ndikatoshaya kuti ndini here ndanga ndisiri kugona kufamba. Kusimuka kwandaita ndatozoona kuti kwanga kuri kuyamurwa pahondo." Akataura Kudzi achiudza amai Mufundisi avo vakanga vakateerera.
 

Akazovarondedzera zvese zvakanga zvaitika kusvika abude muchipatara. Akarondedzerawo zvese zvavanhu vaakashanyira achiisa minamato yeruchengetedzo panguva yavakanga vari iyi. Ari pakutaura kudaro ndipo paakatanga kuona vanhu vaya vaiisa zvidhindo vachifamba vakananga nekudiva raigara amai vake.
Baba vake vakanga vakaoneka nyika mumakore matatu akapfuura saka amai vake ndivo wega vakanga vasara. Paakaona chiitiko chavanhu vaifamba ava mumaziso ake haana kuzoda kugara ipapo.
Akabva atooneka achivimbisa amai Mufundisi naNyasha kuti aizodzoka. Zvakanga zvanakira kuti akanga ava kuziva pavari uye aiziva kuti vakachengetedzeka. Akabva atodzika gomo riye ari mhepo izvo zvaitomushamisa semunhu akanga asati ambomhanya zvakadaro.
Munzira vanhu vaingocheuka vachishaya kuti munhu uyu mamhanyiro ake aiva mamhanyiro rudzii. Nenguva isipi akanga atopinda munzira inonanga kumba kwavo tichangopfuura paDombo tombo. Ndipo paakasangana nevanhu vaya vaakanga achioneswa ari mugomo.
"Ko maiswa chidhindo here nhai mukoma." Akabvunza mumwe wacho achiswedera kwandakanga ndakamira. Ipapo shavi rekupindura zvandinoda rakabva rabata.
 

"Chinomboshandeiko chidhindo chamunongotaura nezvacho ichocho? Chinondiunzira chikafu mumba mangu here kana ndikachiiswa? Pane kungozviisa zvinhu zvisina basa zvisina zvazvinondibatsira muhupenyu." Akataura Kudzi zvakaita kuti vanhu vaye vatarisane vasina zvekutaura. Mumwe vacho ndiye akazoshama muromo kuti ataure.
"Mukoma wangu izvi zvakabva kuvakuru wenyika uye vakati anenge aramba ngaafe nekuti haangadye chikafu chatiri kuunza asingateerere zvaanotaura. Saka nyaya iripo ndeyekuti vosarudza kuiswa chidhindo kana kufa." Akadaro muchinda uya apo mukadzi vaakanga achifamba naye akabva agutsurira musoro senzira yekuwirirana nazvo.
" Manje ini handidye chikafu chenyu uye hapana anokwanisa kusvika pedyo neni akandiuraya. Kana paine anokwanisa ngaaedze tione." Panguva iyi pakabva pangonyuka varume vatatu vakanga vakapfeka zvitema vakavhara kumeso.
Kudzi akabva aziva kuti varume ava vakanga vauya kuzomurwisa nekuti akanga achipikisa zvavaitaura. Akaramba akatarisana nevarume vaya asingavhunduke semunhu akanga aine anomurwira. Mumwe wevarume vatatu ava ndiye akabva afamba kuuya padhuze. Akabva ashama muromo vake kuti ataure.
 

"Saka muchinda iwewe vazvipira here kuonekana nenyika ino? Vazvipira here kuti tikurange tokusiya usingafemi nekuda kwekusateerera kwako?" Kudzi asati apindura akabva atanga kuseka hake. Ndipo paakataura kuti akanga aine simba rekumuuraya ngaamuuraye.
Mumwe wemauto aya akasimudza banga raakanga ainaro mumaoko achiti anyatsotema musoro zvobva zvarova.
Panguva iyoyo simba rese rakabva rapera achibva akundikana kurova Kudzi naro. Akapamhazve kepiri achibva aona ngoma ichingova ndiyo. Mumwe wavo akanga akabata demo akambozamawo kurwisa apo akaita rekusimudza mudenga achikoka simba.
Paakangorisimudza maoko ake akabva aoma zvekuti akanga asisadzike pasi. Kudzi akazovasiya vakabata miromo achipinda muchivanze chavo. Achisvika amai vake vakashamisika kuona achifamba. Vakanga vamusiya kuchipatara pazuva rakanga rapfuura achinzi akanga achida mamwe masvondo maviri kuti abude.
Akazovarondedzera zvese zvakanga zvatora nzvimbo kuti azosvika paakanga ari nguva iyi.
Akavatsanangurirawo zvese zvenzendo dzaakanga afamba achiisa minamato yeruchengetedzo mudzimba dzakanga dzasarudzwa nashe. Achipedza kutsanangura akabva aisa munamato weruchengetedzo.
 

CHAPTER 50 UNTOUCHABLE KUDZI
Kudzi achipedza kuisa munamato akazotanga kukurukura hake dzimwe nyaya naamai vake. Nguva yakanga yareba arimo muchipatara achingoshanyirwa chete asi apa Mwari vakanga varatidza simba ravo.
Mazuva akaramba achimhanya ikava Mwedzi vachiedza kurwisa Kudzi vachikundikana. Vaiedza nepese pavanogona kuti vamuuraye asi pese pavaisvika padhuze vaipera simba. Iye mukoma Kudzi vacho akanga asingatombotye kufamba pakati pevanhu vakadaro.
Mumwe musi vakanga vari pasi pemvura vakaungana apo vaikurukura nyaya dzaiitika panyika. Pazvinhu zvizhinji vakanga vachibudirira uye ropa vakanga vadeura rakawanda.
Rakanga radeurwa mukereke rakanga rakawanda nekuti vanhu vaizoti vabatwa nemashoko anenge achiparidzwa obva ashevedzera kuti Jesus. Ndipo pavaibva vaona musoja achonanga paari osvikoita musoro wekutema mebanga. Nekuda kwaizvozvi ropa rakanga risiri renhamo.
 

Vakakurukura nyaya vachifara sevanhu vaibudirira pazvirongwa zvavo. Kunyangwe zvazvo zvaifamba mushe pane vanhu vashoma shoma vaivashaisa mufaro. Akanga anyanyisa ndiKudzi asi hapana zvavaimuita.
Vaiti vakasvika paElder Mududu vaishaya gedhe vobva vadzokera havo. PaElder Marwei vaiona rwizi chete apo vaibva vashaya kuti imba yanga iripo yaendepi.
Vaizongoona zvirinani kudzokera pane kutambisa nguva. PaMuvhangeri Sheshe vaiti vakasvika vaipera simba nyangwe vakatarisana navo. Zvese izvi aiva mabasa aKudzi akanga afamba achivaka minamato.
Kana kuri kugomo kwaiva naaMai Mufundisi naNyasha ndiko kwaitopisa. Mamwe masoja akaenda akaburuka achiita zvekukunguruka. Vakamboendesa vamwe kepiri vakadzoka mumwe wavo arumwa nenyoka. Hazel aimboratidza simba rake nepese paanogona napo asi aikundikana.
Zvese izvi zvakanga zvichidzosa basa ravo mumashure zvichiita kuti vasasvike pavanoda. Vakanga wava kutyira kuti zvinhu zvinogona kungomuka zvakachinja nekuda kwevanhu iwawa sezvo vakanga vari pabasa rekuparidzira nyika. Ndipo pavakatanga kuronga kuti voitasei nekuti zvakanga zvavakuda kuti vaise pfungwa pamwechete.
 

"Machinda zvinhu zvinofadza kuziva kuti nyika yose iri mumaoko edu uye ndisu tinoisa mitemo yatinoda. Kana tikamuka takaisa mutemo mutsva hapana anotipikisa nekuti inyika yedu." Steve akataura apo vanhu vakamboombera maoko.
"Kunyangwe zvakadaro hazvo handina mufaro nekuda kwevanhu vashoma shoma varikuedza kudzosa basa redu mumashure. Tirikuedza kuti zvifambe asi vanhu iwawo varikuzvivhara." Akadaro Steve achida kumbonzwa pfungwa dzevamwe. Mumwe wemauto epasi pemvura apa akabva apinda mudariro.
"Hongu mungataura zvavangu vakawanda asi pane mumwechete vatambozama zvichiramba. Iyeye anotoda hondo yese yemumuzinda muno tobatanidza masimba edu tese. Tikaita zvekutamba anogona kutikurira taenda nehuwandu hwedu kudaro. Ndirikureva chikomana Kudzi." Akataura muchinda uya vanhu vakateya nzeve.
Pachokwadi Kudzi ndiye akanga achinetsa kubata pavanhu wese vakanga vachitaurwa nezvavo.
Vaitosangana naye munzira mazuva ese vachikundikana kumutorera hupenyu. Ndipo pavakazofunga kushevedza mauto avaiti ndiwo epamusoro aye ekumbouraya vanhu pamusangano. Machinda aya aiti pese pasvika aisiya ropa richierera kunge riri mudhamu.
 

"Machinda angu ndinoda kuti muende kunovhima chikomana chinonzi kudzi muuye nacho. Munhu iyeye arikuda kundiuraira basa rangu saka nhasi ndinoda musoro vake mumuzinda muno ndigoupa mambokadzi vangu ava." Akataura Steve apo akabva araira vakomana kuti vabude pakarepo. Akabva avaraira kuti vamwe vaizonovhima amai Mufundisi kugomo ravo ravaiswera naNyasha nevana wavo.
Machinda aya akaita sezvavakanga varairwa vachibva vapinda panyika vari museve. Vaiti vachifamba munzira vaisaona kana katsi zvayo padhuze. Vakanga vaine tsika yekuti kana vachifamba munzira wese asvika padhuze navo vaimutema musoro nebanga.
Nenguva isipi vakanga vasvika pamba paigara Kudzi apo vakasvikopinda muchivanze chake kuti vamubate. Kudzi uyo akanga anzwa mutsindo panze akabva abuda kuti aone vakanga vashanya pamba pavo.
Ndipo paakaona machinda aya achibva ataurirwa kunzi ndiye akanga achidiwa. Akabva avaraire kuti vaite zvavakanga vavinga. Mumwe vacho akada kusvika paiva naKudzi achibva awira pasi nemusana. Vamwe vakamboda kuedza kupotsera mapanga avakanga vakabata asi vaibva vapera simba. Pavakaona vakundikana vakabva vabva havo pamba apa vakananga kugomo kwaiva naMai Mufundisi.
 

CHAPTER 51 DOUBLE TROUBLE
Masoja aya aiita zvekumhanya akananga kugomo kunobata basa. Hasha dzekutadza kubata Kudzi ndidzo dzakanga dzava kuzopedzerwa kunaamai Mufundisi.
Vanhu ndiwo vaiita kunge vachatyoka makumbo munzira vachitiza varume wechiuto ava. Vamwe ndiwo vaiita munyama apo vaisanganidzana navo hupenyu hwobva hwatorwa rakacheka nyika.
Nekunerimwe divi amai Mufundisi vakanga vakagara mugomo naNyasha wavo vachangopedza kunamata. Vana vaamai Mufundisi vakanga vatosimbawo pakunamata zvekukwanisawo kurwira vamwe kune vakaipa.
Nyasha ndipo paakabva atanga kuona varume vaikwidza gomo vakabata mapanga. Akacherechedza varume vaya achibva aona kuti panyika akanga asati ambosangana nevakadaro. Akatarira varume vaya vachikwidza gomo apo vakanga vakawanda zvekutopinda muzana. Ndipo paakaudza amai Mufundisi zvaakanga achiona. Mai Mufundisi vakabva vamuudza kuti hondo iyi yakanga yabinga ivo vari vaviri asi hapana zvayaikwanisa kuvaita.
 

Pakarepo pakabva patanga kuimbwa nziyo apo vaidana vatumwa kuti vabate basa. Panguva iyoyo vakabva vaona varume vana vakabakomberedza kumativi ose vakabata mwenje yavo mumaoko.
Vakawedzera kuimba apo mauto aye akazenge asvika pamuzinda wavo. Inzwi rakabva radzika richitaura munzeve dzaamai Mufundisi avo vakabva variteerera.
"Musatye vana vangu nekuti ndinemi, ndakambokurwirai pakutanga uye ndakanga ndinemi musango muno mazuva ese. Nazvino ndinofara kana muchindishumira nekurevesa. Hondo yamurikuona iyo musatya zvenyu nekuti haina simba. Varikuzama nesimba ravo asi havakundi. Ndavatumira vachavarwisa zvichaita kuti vadzokere vakashota. Imi chingotarirai chete muchiimba nekuti zvekurwa hazvisi zvenyu." Inzwi riya richipedza kutaura rakabva raenda.
Amai Mufundisi vakabva vaudzawo Nyasha pamwe nevana wavo zvakanga zvapinda munzeve mavo.
Vakatanga kuimba vakatarira kwaibva nemauto aya apa inzwi rakanga rava pamusoro.
Varume wechiuto vaya vakamboseka vachitaura zvavanoda pamusoro pavakanga vachiimba ava. Vaitofunga kuti amai Mufundisi naNyasha vaiita zvedamba. Vakabva vatanga kufamba vachienda pedyo.
 

"Nhasi chaiye urikurisiya sadza nekuda kwekuzviti unonamata. Iwe nevana vako nekamusikana kauri kuimba nako ikako garai matiudza mashoko enyu ekupedzisira tisati taudza musiku kuti agadzirire kutambira mweya yenyu. Ukaona isu tauya patinosvika panonhuwa rufu izvozvi ndakatonzwa ropa kunhuwa." Akataura mumwe wemasoja aya achibva atanga kuseka zvekusvotesa.
"Mashoko angu ekupedzisira ndeekuti kana matenderwa itai henyu zvamafambira. Kana Mwari varikumusoro vakutenderai zvirokwazvo muchatisiya tava kumarinda." Vakataura amai Mufundisi zvakaita kuti muchinda uye aseke zvekare.
Masoja aya akabva atanga kufamba achiswedera paiva nanamai Mufundisi. Izvi hazvina kuvamisa kuimba vakabva vatowedzera. Varume vaya vakanga vakakomba amai Mufundisi vakabva vasimudza mwenje yavo mudenga vari panzvimbo dzavakanga vari.
Pakatanga kunzwikwa mitsindo yemabhiza nengoro zvakanga zvichiuya kuzorwa izvo zvakavhundutsa masoja aya. Kuti vasvike paiva naamai Mufundisi zvakaramba vaingoona kupenya kwechiedza pobva paita rima. Nenguva isipi ngoro dziya dzakanga dzava kunzwika mudhuze apo pakabva pasvika varume vatatu vakabata minondo mumaoko.
 

Masoja aya akatanga kurwiswa zvekuti hapana kana mumwe wavo akakwanisa kudzorera. Vamwe ndivo vaiti vakada kuvhika vaibva vatyorwa maoko. Hondo yakatsva nziyo dzichiimbwa nenzwi repamusoro.
Masoja aya akatanga kuita aziva kwake aziva kwake nekuti pakanga pasisina chekumirira.
Pakutiza ipapo vaviri wavo ndiwo vakazorasikirwa nehupenyu. Mumwe akarohwa mbama yaasina kuona kuti yabva nekupi achibva adonha pasi. Akabva angooma zvakadaro. Mumwe akangonzwa kuti abaiwa nemunondo achibva awira muvhu. Akabva angosiya sadza pakarepo.
Vamwe vakazonosangana kumberi apo vakatanga kukurukura kupunyuka kwavakanga vaita. Amai Mufundisi naNyasha vakasara vachirumbidza Mwari nekuvarwira pahondo yakanga ichityisa kudai.
Mauto aya akasvika kumvura achibva atsanangura zvakanga zvaitika uye kuti vaviri wavo vakanga vafa. Izvi zvakapa Vicky hasha apo akafunga zvekunopedza hondo idzi ega. Aizobuda nehondo yake yese asi ndiye aizomira mberi pakurwa. Ndiyo yakanga yava nguva yekuratidza masimba ake ese. Ndipo zvekare paakanga ava kuzoonekwa hukuru hwake.
 

CHAPTER 52
END OF THE ROAD
Mazuva akaramba achifamba kubva musi varongwa zvekuti Vicky aende nehondo yake yese kunorwa. Aida kuzohwandira vanhu vake pavanenge vari pakamanikana. Iye Vicky aingozvishingisa asi dzimwevpfungwa dzaimuti vanhu ava havana kumira mushe.
Akazongozviudza kuti paaizosangana nevanhu iwawo paisazomera huswa. Semunhu akanga aine masimba ekuita zvese zvaanoda uye ndiye aitopa vamwe haaitarisira kukundwa.
Mumwe musi iri svondo vanhu vakaenda kukereke zvavaisiita. Mufundisi Mazondo vakagadzirira semazuva ese vachibva vaenda kukereke. Munhu aiti kana achipinda mukereke aitanga atariswa kuti ane chidhindo here. Kana asina chaibva chaiswa ipapo.
Nekunerimwe divi Mukoma Kudzi vakanga vakarara apo vakanzwa inzwi raitaura munzeve dzavo.
Vakanyatsoteya nzeva kuti vanzwe zvaitaura inzwi iri.
 

"Mwanakomana basa rako rakaita kuti udzoswe panyika ratanga, muka uende kukereke unebasa rakakumirira ikoko. Ndoda kuti udzore makwai ari kurasika ayo adzoke mugwara. Kana vari vatungamiri wavo mutongo uripo kare." Inzwi riya rakataura richibva raenda.
Ipapo Kudzi haana kuda kutambisa nguva akabva atomuka achigadzirira. Nenguva isipi akanga atochena chena agadzirira kupinda. Akabva asarudza kuenda asina kudya semunhu akanga aine basa raida kuti anyatsoenda pamberi paMwari.
Amai vake vakagadzirirawo vachibva vapinda munzira wese. Nenguva isipi vakanga vatosvika apo vakatanga kufamba vachipinda mukati. Vachisvika pamusuwo vakaona uya aiongorora vanhu vane zvidhindo aripo pamusuwo.
Paakavabvunza vakabva vamuudza kuti vakanga vasingaiswe zvidhindo vachitopfuura vachienda. Muchinda uya akada kuvatevera kuti avadzose achibva ashaya simba rekufamba. Paakati rega ndiite zvekushevedzera akabva ashaya simba rekushamisa muromo vake. Paakaona zvadaro akabva asiyana hake nazvo. Kudzi naamai vake vakabva vaenda havo kunogara makanga muine vamwe. Nziyo dzakanga dzichiimbwa apa dzaimubata nekuti dzakanga dzasiyana nedzaaiziva kare.
 

Mwanakomana akanyatsoona kuti zvinhu zvachinja uye vanhu vakanga vatorasika zvaitoda nyasha dzaMwari kuti vadzoke. Mumadziro mese makanga makanyorwa nemavara makuru kunzi THE GREAT MARINE KING. Akabva atozviona pachena kuti ndiye mwari akanga ava kunamatwa mukereke.
Chimwe chakamubata achipinda inyaya yekuona masoja mukereke. Zvairevaka kuti vanhu ava vaitoita zvekumanikidzwa kunamata zvavasingazivi. Izvi zvakapa Kudzi rimwe simba raasina kumboziva kuti rabva nekupi.
Akangosimuka achibva atanga kufamba achienda kumberi kwechaunga. Maziso ese akanga atarisa kwaari apo vanhu vaida kuona kuti aidei kumberi ikoko.
Nenguva isipi akanga atomira kumberi kuti ataure shoko raMwari mupenyu.
"Ndinokutendai vana vaMwari nechido chenyu chamaratidza kuuya pano kunyangwe tirikushumira zvakasiyana. Ndinoda kudzorerawo mbiri kuna iye Musiki anotipa hupenyu nekutitarira panyika yatinofamba iyi. Neniwo ndimire pano ndinofara kukuudzai kuti nekuda kwesimba riri muropa raJesu ndakadzoswa panyika kuti ndigobata basa." Panguva iyi vanhu vakanga vachakamutarisa vasinganzwisisi zvaitora nzvimbo. Akabva aenderera hake mberi.
 

"Nhasi shoko rangu ndicharitora panenyaya dzaJohani kuna Zvakazarurwa. Ndidzo nyaya dzenguva ino yatiri kurarama. Nekuti chikara chakaonekwa chichibuda mugungwa chine masimba makuru. Zvino zvachakanga chine masimba makuru chaida kuti chitsause avo vakasanangurwa." Vanhu vakaramba vakanyarara vakateya nzeve kushoko iri.
"Vanhu vakasvika pakunamata chikara akati ndiani anesimba angakwanise kurwa nacho. Nazvino ndizvo zvirikuitika mukereke muno kuti vanhu vasarudza kutevera chikara nekuda kwesimba rachiri kushandisa kubata basa rinoshamisa. Nazvino vanhu vari mukereke varikuti ndiani anesimba rinokunda revatiri kunamata uyu, hama muzive kuti kudenga kuna Mwari mukuru kuru kwete wenyu wamuri kunamata nhasi uyu." Pakatanga kuita mahon'era muvanhu apo vaipikisa zvaaitaura.
"Vashumiri wemarimwezuro vakauraiwa vari pakushumira shoko iri uye vamwe vainzvengeswa. Nhasi uno ndauya kuzoitawo sevashumiri iwawo kuna ndichifa ndigofirawo shoko irori. Andituma anditi enda unodzora vana vari kurasika. Ndanzwa tsitsi kwazvo ndikati regai ndiita kuda kweandituma." Panguva iyi amai Mufundisi vakabva vapinda naNyasha pamwechete nevana wavo vaviri. Pakangoitika zvimwechete hapana akaita simba rekuti avaise chidhindo.
 

Kudzi akaenderera mberi neshoko rake izvo zvakazoita kuti masoja akanga ari mukereke umu ade kumurwisa.
"Muchinda iwe vabvira kare uchitiparidzira nhema. Nguva yatanyarara yareba takateerera madhaka ako auri kutaura." Akadaro mumwe wemasoja aya apo vamwe vanhu vakanga vari muchaunga umu vakabvumira.
Kudzi akabva avaudza asingatye kuti Mwari waakanga achiparidza nezvake akanga ari Mwari wekumusoro soro akasika zvese zviri pasi pano. Akanga akasiyana newavo wemumvura wekuti vanoenda vachinosuma matambudziko avapa mazano.
Musoja uya akaita hasha achibva atanga kufamba achiuya kumberi ikoko. Ndipo paakaona kuti Kudzi akanga amira akabatana maoko naamai Mufundisi pamwe naNyasha. Paakada kusvika padhuze navo pakabva paita muganhu wemoto vaipisa kwazvo. Akabva aona kuti pakanga pasingasvikike achibva akanda banga raaiva naro kwakadaro uko.
Akangopfugama pamberi ipapo achiudza vanhu vaMwari kuti vamunamatire. Akanga asarudza kutendeuka nekuti simba raakanga aratidzwa raiva gurusa. Panguva iyoyo ndipo pakapinda Mufundisi Mazondo mukereke vachiona mashura ese aya.
Vakashaya kuti chii chakanga chichitora nzvimbo.
 

Vamwe vanhu vakatanga kubuda muchaunga vachienda kumberi kunonamatirwa apo vakanga vafunga kuzvarwa patsva. Pakarepo pakangoita chamupupuri mukereke umu vanhu vakashamisika kuti chii chakanga chavakutora nzvimbo.
Chamupupuri chiya chakazoshanduka kuita munhu uyo akatanga kufamba achiuya kumberi kwaiva nanaKudzi. Aiva mukadzi mutsvuka akasimba uye aine bvudzi raida kutosvika kumakumbo. Nenguva isipi akanga atarisana nevanhu vaMwari ava vaibata basa. Wese vakanga vari pakunamatira vanhu vakanga vachitendeuka.
"In ndinonzi Vicky ndini THE GREAT MARINE KING ndini ndine masimba ose anonamatwa nevanhu muno uyezve ndini ndinopa hupenyu nerufu. Ndini zvekare ndinopa hupfumi nehurombo. Nyaya yangu iripakuti imi muri vatatu ndoda kuona simba renyu nhasi rinoita kuti mupikise mutemo wangu muchiita kuda kwenyu." Panguva iyi vanhu vakanga vachinyarara vakateya nzeve kuti vanzwe zvaiitika.
Kudzi akabva apindura kuti akanga asina simba asi akanga amutuma aiva nesimba rakapetwa zvakanyanya kudarika raiye Vicky. Akabva amuudza zvekare kuti akanga akashinga kuita zvese zvaakanga achifunga kuita vaizoona kunowira tsvimbo nedohwe.
 

Izvi zvakaita kuti Vicky aite hasha apo akabva afunga kutanga basa rake. Akangoshanduka apo vanaKudzi vakaona vatarisana nevanhu gumi vakafanana. Izvozvo hazvina kuvavhundutsa vakabva vatowedzera kuimba apo vakanga vabatana maoko.
Vanhu vaya vakanga vakatarisana nanaKudzi vakanga vakabata mapanga mumaoko vakagadzirira kubaya vanhu vaMwari ava. Inzwi rakauya munzeve dzakudzi richiti namatai musatye, muchaona zvichaiitika. Kudzi akabva audzawo vamwe vake munamato uchibva vatotanga kutsva.
Vanhu vaya vaiti vakada kuswedera pedyo vaibva vadonha nemanhede. Pavaisimuka vaibva vadzokera nehasha asi zvairamba zvakadaro. Hondo haina kupera apo vanhu vaya vakanyangarika. Apa Vicky akanga afunga kurwisa asingaonekwi achiuya ari mhepo chete. Ndiye ega aizoona muvengi vake.
Chaasina kuziva ndechekuti vanhu vaairwisa vaitomuonawo. Aiti akada kusvika pedyo navo ari mumhepo kudaro aibva atsva nemoto. Vatatu ava havana kuda kudzosera vaingonamata chete hondo dzichirwiwa nevatumwa. Vicky paakaona zvichidai akabva ashanduka kuita mombe. Akanga asati agutsikana kuti akundwa.
 

Mombe yakanyatsoteya nyanga apo yakanga yagadzirira kutunga. Apa yakati ichisvika padhuze yakabva yaita zvekunamirira. VanaKudzi vakanamata mombe iya yakanamira kudaro ichibva yashanduka zvekare kuita Vicky.
Panguva iyi akatanga kubvira mota achichema izvo zvaionekwa nemunhu wese mukereke. Akaramba achibvira apo akazongoita zvekunyangarika achitiza kuenda. Wese vaakanga auya navo kuzorwisa hapana akada kuuya kuzomira nevanhu ava pahondo.
Kudzi pamwe naamai Mufundisi naNyasha vakazotanga kuimba nziyo dzekurumbidza musiki sezvo vakanga vapedza basa. Musi uyu vanhu vakazotendeuka asi vawe vashoma vakabuda vakaenda. Mufundisi Mazondo vakazongodonha vachibva vaoma mutezo.
Vakazokumbira ruregerero kuvana vaMwari asi hapana zvazvakachinja pavari.
Kubva musi uyu amai Mufundisi vakabva vatanga kugara kumba kwavo. Nyasha akabva aendavo kumba kwavo zvekare. Mazuva zvaakafamba humambo hwaJonhsona hwakabva hwabviswa zvichinzi hauna kukodzera. Mai Mufundisi vakasarudza kuchengeta havo murume wavo akaoma mutezo kudaro nyangwe zvazvo akanga avatadzira. Kutaura kuno kereke yavakuenderera mberi uye vanhu wava nerugare.
 

Kana chiri chikwata chepasi pamvura kune mariro izvozvi. Hazel akazombodzoka achida kurwisa achibva afa. Millicent naLisa vaakanga ainavo vakaremara makumbo. Vachibva kunochema Hazel ndipo pavacharonga kuti voenderera nebasa here asi Vicky akati akuda kusiyana nazvo.

Zuva rakanga rowoneka nyika, rasiti piriviri kumavirira sorutondondo, mhepo yaivhuvhudza zvine rutsigo ichibva kuChamhembe yakadziva kuMaodzanyemba. Dai kwaive kumusha, gwenhure, jesa, dhimba nekasirisiri zvingadai zvaive pamakundano okuimbira kunyura kwezuva zvichitenda kuti kwanhasi tambovhenekerwa. Zvino zvamaive mudhorobha, huta dzemotokari ndidzo dzainzwika dzichikwikwiridza nemhando yadzo, kuchiti mabhazi, marori, nemota duku dzakaita sePeugeot, Mazda 323, Datsun 120Y, nedzimwe wo dzainetsa mazuva aya.
Panguva inongunorehwa iyi, Sekai akanga agere pasofa akaita kutambarara makumbo, ruoko rwerudyi rwaive pashaya rwakatengwa nerweruboshwe irwo rwaive rwakabatira pazvipapadzo zvesofa. Ainge akapfeka rokwe reruvara rwemhererwa iro raivewo zvaro mukubudu asi zvichipedzerana nedumbu rakanga rakati duduma kutungamira mberi seraambuya mutegede. Pamusoro aive akatipo dzva bhareta dzvuku raive nezibhatani ziguru nechepano pahuma. Mutsoka maive nehwashu dzaive dzakagadzirwa kubva pavhiri remotokari.
Mvura yakanga iri mupoto huru yaive pachitofu chemagetsi yakanga yatambura nekuvira. Ko, yaigodii zvayo iye mwene akanga ave mhiri kwaRunde achipotedza nemasango mundangariro. Pane zvaidya pfungwa kudarika mvura, poto, chitofu nemagetsi acho zvose.
Sekai aive mukadzi akanga ave nemwedzi mitanhatu apinda mumba. Zvaakanga abva kumusha kwavo kwaMurehwa achiuya kuzogara nemukoma wake aive mukoti pachipatara cheKaroi haana kuita gore ainavo, akanga atotuta mabhegi ake achinogara nemukomana ainzi Charles waakanga adanana naye kwemwedzi mishanu. Chikuru chakanga chamupa kusvovera saizvi idumbu ranga rava nemwedzi mitatu richisundaidzwa nemhuru yaizouya.
Nyangwe zvazvo mukoma wake, nevamwe voukama vakamumhura pakutiza mukumbo kwaakanga aita, vakazofara apo vakaona mukomana wacho adungamidzana nevekwake vakatakura mabhokisi emagirosari nezvikwama zvizere mari. Tsvakirai kuno, nhendamurandu, rupwanyaruzhowa, nezvimwe zvibinge zvakabviswa zvose ndokungosara rusambo rwave chimedu. Akaroorwa zvakanaka kwazvo Sekai.
Agere pasofa saizvozvo, zvaive mupfungwa dzake indangariro dzemavambo okusangana kwaakanga aita naCharles nekuronga zvokutizisana kwavakazoita. Zvose vaiita vari pamwechete, vachinzwana, rudo ruchibvira moto sezvinoita huni dzemupani dzave pedyo nekuorera. Tambudzai ndiye aive mukuru uye panguva iyi akanga ava nemakore adzoka kumurume ndokuuya nemwana wake ainzi Solomon. Uyuwo Shylet akanga achiita fomu yetatu paSekondari yeMwami.
